# Archive 2026-05

Continuous-archival monthly bucket. One section per archival day,
newest day first. Per `.claude/rules/ai-workflow.md`
"Continuous archival rule".

For the current work plan, see [docs/ROADMAP.md](../ROADMAP.md).

## Archived 2026-05-27 (SETTINGS-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-REORGANIZATION-01 CLOSED — stale filing; full scope already shipped under SETT-PHASE-2-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-SPLIT-01 in v0.38.0)

Closed retroactively after a backlog re-sync audit surfaced
that the entire scope of this item shipped under a different
ID in the v0.38.0 release cycle.

### Coverage map

| Original SETTINGS-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-REORGANIZATION-01 scope | Where it shipped |
|---|---|
| Option B (preferred): split "Allgemein" into multiple top-level tabs | SETT-PHASE-2-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-SPLIT-01 (v0.38.0, 2026-05-26, commits `b194ddf..2b28d17`) |
| Grouping strategy (Erscheinung / Verhalten / Daten / etc.) | Erscheinungsbild + Verhalten + Erweitert + Editor (4 tabs, matches the proposed grouping with Editor lifted out in Phase 1) |
| AppSettings.tsx removal + per-tab component extraction | `2b28d17` deleted AppSettings.tsx + tabDefs entry |
| i18n: new tab labels × 8 catalogs | 10 new keys × 8 catalogs (80 string entries) shipped under SETT-PHASE-2 |
| Vitest + E2E for new tab navigation | Vitest 2052 → 2056 (net +4); E2E `trash-view-mode-defaults.spec.ts` + `ux-audit-group3.spec.ts` updated |

### Why this closure is retroactive

The two items were filed independently with different
session contexts: SETTINGS-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-REORGANIZATION-01
was filed 2026-05-16 (Hotfix-Session, post-Bug-4 evening)
as a deferred IMPROVEMENT for the next Settings-Polish-
Session. SETT-PHASE-2-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-SPLIT-01 was filed
2026-05-25 (post-v0.37.0 Settings UX audit) as the Phase 2
of the larger Settings-UX overhaul. Both proposed the same
"split Allgemein into multiple top-level tabs" Option B
solution; SETT-PHASE-2 shipped it first.

Surfaced 2026-05-27 during the backlog re-sync after two
consecutive prompt-collisions with already-archived work.
The 17-item P3 inventory pass flagged this as "PARTIALLY
SHIPPED" → audit confirmed FULL coverage → close +
archive.

### Lessons-learned anchor

The two filings exemplify the recurring pattern of
"same scope filed under different IDs from different
session contexts". The 2026-05-20 backlog re-prioritization
audit's discipline (cross-reference IDs at filing time to
catch semantic-duplicates) would have caught this at filing
time. Absent that, the periodic re-prioritization audit
catches it at next-sweep time. Both layers held.

---

## Archived 2026-05-27 (PICTURE-BOOK-TEXT-STACK CLOSED — 3 backlog items, 2 sessions, 18 commits; Fix B namespace + Tier 1+2 across all 3 image layouts + Bug D width/height)

Three backlog items closed together — they ship as one
coherent text-stack feature even though they were filed
independently:

1. `PICTURE-BOOK-PAGE-TEXT-TIPTAP-INTEGRATION-01` (P3) —
   TipTap rich-text editing for image_top + image_left +
   text_only layouts. D1 MVP shipped v0.35.0; D2-D6
   confirmed at Pre-Inspection as ALREADY SHIPPED in
   v0.35.0 (only D4 active-migration remains, filed
   separately as `PICTURE-BOOK-LAYOUT-SWITCH-TEXT-
   CONVERSION-01`, P3, trigger-gated; zero user-impact
   today via parseTextContentToJson read-side wrapping).
2. `PICTURE-BOOK-OVERLAY-TEXT-TIER-PROPERTIES-01` (P3) —
   apply Tier-Property pattern (14 fields: 8 Visual-Style
   + 6 Typography) to image_full_text_overlay text band
   + Bug D scope-add (text_container_width +
   text_container_height sliders).
3. `PICTURE-BOOK-TEXT-CONFIGURATION-01` (P3) — extend the
   same Tier 1+2 pattern to image_top_text_bottom +
   image_left_text_right + Fix B sub-item (layout_config
   per-layout namespace).

### Pre-Inspection (2026-05-27)

`docs/audits/picture-book-text-stack-pre-inspection-2026-05-27.md`
covered 8 tracks + 8 A-decisions. Key findings (re-framed
the user's scope):

- D2-D6 of TIPTAP-INTEGRATION-01 mostly already shipped in
  v0.35.0 — RichTextEditor + 11-button RichTextToolbar +
  parseTextContentToJson + _render_tiptap_doc PDF walker
  all live. Only D4 active-migration remains, filed
  separately.
- Tier1Section + Tier2Section components ALREADY EXIST as
  extracted reusables (comics/Tier1Section.tsx +
  Tier2Section.tsx, Comics-Session-2 C5). Extending them
  is wiring, not framework-creation.
- Fix B (layout_config namespace per-layout) is the only
  real foundational refactor. Bundled with the Tier
  extensions to avoid double-migration.
- Genuine new work: Fix B + Tier 1+2 across overlay
  (Bug D scope-add) + image_top + image_left.

8 A-decisions adjudicated; no STOP-conditions.

### Notable architecture decisions

- **Fix B namespacing**: `layout_config` becomes
  `{[layout]: {...settings}}`. Per-layout configs survive
  switches. Legacy-flat configs are detected via
  `looksNamespaced` and treated as the current layout's
  namespace; first write through `writeLayoutNamespace`
  migrates them to namespaced shape. Bubbles[0] wrapper
  stays INSIDE the speech_bubble namespace.
- **Shared `computeTierTextStyles` helper** (Session 2
  C1): extracted from the overlay branch when the 3rd
  surface (image_top) landed — the 2-surface RCU threshold
  had been satisfied at Session 1 C5 by overlay joining
  speech_bubble. Same shape in the Python walker
  (`_compute_tier_text_style`).
- **No bubbles[0] wrapping for non-bubble layouts**:
  image_top + image_left + overlay all use FLAT
  partials inside their layout namespace. speech_bubble
  keeps bubbles[0] (which lives inside the
  speech_bubble namespace post-Fix-B).
- **Tier sections use existing Tier1Section/Tier2Section
  reusables** (extracted in Comics-Session-2 C5). No
  further `<TierPropertiesEditor>` super-wrapper —
  direct mounts are clearer (per A5).
- **text_only layout has NO Tier sections in v1** (per
  A7). The layout currently has no config UI at all;
  adding one opens a UX question deferred to a separate
  filing if author demand surfaces.
- **D4 active-migration deferred** (per A2). Filed
  separately as `PICTURE-BOOK-LAYOUT-SWITCH-TEXT-
  CONVERSION-01` (P3, trigger-gated). Zero user-impact
  today via the read-side parseTextContentToJson shim.
- **CollapsibleSection helper extraction deferred**
  (per A4). Tier sections use Radix.Collapsible directly;
  works fine. P3 cleanup filed separately.

### Cumulative deltas (both sessions)

- Backend pytest: 2294 (no change — backend layer
  unchanged; all work in frontend + plugin)
- Plugin-export pytest: 268 → **307** (+39 cumulative
  across Sessions 1+2; +49 with Session 2 C3/C4 adds:

- Frontend Vitest: 2125 → **2186** (+61 cumulative

  `writeLayoutNamespace` + `looksNamespaced` helpers
  (TS + Python mirror); 6 new mount points
  (Tier1Section + Tier2Section in 3 layouts) + 1

- New help pages: `docs/help/{de,en}/books/text-configuration.md`
  wired into `docs/help/_meta.yaml` + `mkdocs.yml`

### Disciplines re-validated

- Audit-First Pre-Inspection (8 A-decisions adjudicated
  before any code-write; the audit correctly identified
  that D2-D6 were mostly shipped, reframing scope)
- Pre-Coding-Reality-Check at C1 boundaries of both
  sessions (verified the actual touch surfaces before
  writing code)

  because the writer change and reader change had to
  ship atomically; Session 2 C1 included the
  computeTierTextStyles extraction in the same commit

- Atomic-green per commit-delta (every commit
  individually green; backend pytest 2294 + plugin tests

- Backward-compat: legacy-flat layout_config configs
  continue to render correctly via the namespace
  helpers' flat-shape detection

  vitest from frontend/, not repo root" lessons-learned

- Numeric claims verified per commit message

## Archived 2026-05-27 (PICTURE-BOOK-STORYBOARD-VIEW-01 CLOSED — 2 sessions, 16 commits; Storyboard MVP + Annotations shipped; Operations deferred)

Filed 2026-05-18 as a brainstorming P3 with 10-15-commit
estimate. Closed 2026-05-27 after two coordinated sessions on
the same day. Total scope shipped: schema (4 nullable columns
+ Alembic migration) + read-only grid + drag-reorder +
4 annotation editors (notes / story-beat / mood-color /
act-group) + i18n × 8 catalogs + Vitest pins + Playwright E2E +
DE + EN help docs.

### Pre-Inspection (2026-05-27 morning)

`docs/audits/picture-book-storyboard-pre-inspection-2026-05-27.md`
covered 7 tracks + 8 A-decisions. Key findings:

- PageThumbnails was already shared between PageEditor and
  ComicBookEditor via `testidNamespace` (RCU done prior).
  Storyboard adds a 3rd surface but the grid+annotations shape
  diverged enough from the sidebar-strip shape that A5 ships
  a sibling `StoryboardCard` rather than a 3rd-level shared
  card. Design-intent-axis rule per coding-standards.md.
- Schema is purely additive nullable columns (zero data
  migration); `batch_alter_table` migration follows the
  established v0.37.0 `s8c9d0e1f234_add_book_repository_url`
  template.
- Mount via `?view=storyboard` query-param flip mirrors the
  existing `?view=metadata` convention — no new editor_component
  entry in book-types.yaml, no new top-level route.

All 8 A-decisions confirmed default (no overrides). No
STOP-conditions surfaced.

### Session 1 — Schema-Foundation + MVP (8 commits)

| # | Commit subject | Test delta |
|---|---|---|
| C1 | feat(pages): add storyboard schema columns | backend 2269 (no change) |
| C2 | feat(pages): extend Pydantic schemas + create wiring | backend 2269 |
| C3 | test(pages): storyboard-field round-trip + validation pins | backend 2269 → **2294** (+25) |
| C4 | feat(storyboard): Storyboard + StoryboardCard read-only grid | vitest 2080 (no change) |
| C5 | feat(storyboard): wire ?view=storyboard mount + PageEditor button | vitest 2080 |
| C6 | feat(storyboard): drag-reorder via existing /reorder endpoint | vitest 2080 |
| C7 | i18n(storyboard): ui.storyboard.* + show_storyboard × 8 catalogs | i18n parity 75/75 |
| C8 | test(storyboard): structural Vitest pins | vitest 2080 → **2098** (+18) |

Outcome: Storyboard reachable from PageEditor header, shows
all pages in a grid with thumbnails + titles + layout tags,
supports drag-reorder, click-card returns to PageEditor.
Annotations columns exist in DB but not yet UI-editable.

### Session 2 — Annotations (7 commits)

| # | Commit subject | Test delta |
|---|---|---|
| S2-C1 | feat(storyboard): inline notes editing on StoryboardCard | vitest 2098 → 2105 (+7) |
| S2-C2 | feat(storyboard): story-beat tag selector | vitest 2105 → 2111 (+6) |
| S2-C3 | feat(storyboard): mood-color preset palette (10 swatches) | vitest 2111 → 2118 (+7) |
| S2-C4 | feat(storyboard): act-group inline editing | vitest 2118 → **2125** (+7) |
| S2-C5 | i18n(storyboard): annotation strings × 8 catalogs (18 keys) | i18n parity 75/75 |
| S2-C6 | test(e2e): Playwright smoke for storyboard annotations | 3 specs |
| S2-C7 | docs(storyboard): help DE + EN + backlog archival | — |

#### Notable Session 2 architecture decisions

- **Card root refactor (S2-C1)**: `<button>` → `<div role="button"
  tabIndex={0}>` so nested form controls (textarea + select +
  color-swatch buttons + text input) are valid HTML. Mirrors the
  PageThumbnails SortablePageRow pattern. Keyboard handler only
  navigates when `e.target === e.currentTarget` so typing in a
  child input doesn't trigger card navigation.

- **Native `<select>` over Radix Select (S2-C2)**: per the
  "Radix DropdownMenu + happy-dom is brittle for Vitest"
  lessons-learned rule, the same brittleness applies to Radix
  Select. Native `<select>`'s onChange fires deterministically
  in Vitest; the existing beatTag badge above the selector
  already shows the localised value.

- **Preset palette over free-color-picker (S2-C3)**: per the
  Stop-Condition guidance (no new dependency for a free
  picker). 10 curated mood colors cover the typical picture-book
  emotional range. Free-picker filed as
  `STORYBOARD-MOOD-FREE-PICKER-01` (P5, trigger-gated).

- **Drag-across-groups stays reorder-only (S2-C4)**:
  Pre-Coding-Reality-Check finding. The SortableContext wraps
  the flat page-id list; dragging a card across visual group
  boundaries reorders position but leaves act_group unchanged
  (the next render snaps the card back to its own group).
  Authors set the group via the inline label. Auto-update on
  cross-group drag filed as
  `STORYBOARD-DRAG-CROSS-GROUP-ACT-UPDATE-01` (P5).

- **`mockClear` vs `mockReset` discipline (S2-C1)**: surfaced
  during test development — a prior test's `mockResolvedValue`
  on `api.pages.update` leaked call history into the next
  test's `.not.toHaveBeenCalled()` assertion. Fixed per the
  "Module-level caches survive test boundaries"
  lessons-learned rule: `mockClear` in beforeEach (NOT
  `mockReset`) to preserve any factory defaults.

### Cumulative deltas (both sessions)

- Backend pytest: 2269 → **2294** (+25, all in
  TestStoryboardFields)
- Frontend Vitest: 2080 → **2125** (+45, all in
  Storyboard.test.tsx)
- i18n parity: 75/75 holds; +16 (Session 1 C7) + 18 (S2-C5) =
  34 new ui.storyboard.* keys × 8 catalogs = 272 entries
  added across both sessions
- Playwright smoke: 3 new specs (notes + beat + mood + act-
  group round-trip, clear-notes, toggle-mood)
- E2E specs run separately (per project convention; not on
  the `make test` path)
- New components: `Storyboard.tsx`, `StoryboardCard`,
  `SortableStoryboardCard`, `NotesEditor`, `BeatSelector`,
  `MoodColorPicker`, `ActGroupInput` (all in
  `frontend/src/components/Storyboard.tsx`)
- New help pages: `docs/help/{de,en}/books/storyboard.md`
  wired into `docs/help/_meta.yaml` + `mkdocs.yml`

### Disciplines re-validated

- Audit-First Pre-Inspection (8 A-decisions adjudicated
  before any code-write)
- Plain `git status` before every commit + explicit-paths
  staging (16 atomic commits across both sessions)
- Atomic-green-per-commit-delta (every commit individually
  green; backend baseline 2269 / vitest baseline maintained
  throughout)
- Half-wired-prevention: C3 ships round-trip + validation
  pins paired with C1+C2; every annotation editor (S2-C1 to
  S2-C4) ships its tests in the same commit
- TipTap `imageFigure` rule honoured (Storyboard reads
  text_content but emits no TipTap nodes)
- `mockClear` over `mockReset` (Module-level cache test
  boundary discipline)
- Pre-Coding-Reality-Check fired twice in Session 2:
  drag-across-groups semantics (S2-C4) and Enter-blurs-save
  happy-dom brittleness (S2-C4 test) — both surfaced before
  the relevant commit landed.
- Single-Source-of-Truth: `page.position` shared with
  PageThumbnails reorder; no parallel ordering shape.

### Follow-ups filed at close

- `PICTURE-BOOK-STORYBOARD-OPERATIONS-01` (P5, trigger-gated)
  — page operations (add-in-between, duplicate, split, merge,
  print, auto-act-group-on-cross-group-drag).
- `STORYBOARD-MOOD-FREE-PICKER-01` (P5, trigger-gated) —
  free-hex color picker beyond the 10 preset swatches.
- `STORYBOARD-DRAG-CROSS-GROUP-ACT-UPDATE-01` (P5,
  trigger-gated) — auto-update act_group when dragging across
  visual group boundaries.

All three are filed against real user-pull triggers, not
speculation. v2 (annotations) covers the daily picture-book
authoring rhythm that the original brainstorming session
identified as the load-bearing value.

## Archived 2026-05-26 (HELP-DOCS-V0.37.0-GAPS-01 CLOSED — 6 help topics × DE + EN + 5 Playwright-generated screenshots)

Filed 2026-05-25 from v0.37.0 release-time help-docs review as
4 missing pages (Dashboard pagination, Word-wrap, Editor display
settings, Book.repository_url). Extended at close-time to also
cover the v0.38.0 Settings-UX overhaul (Settings sidebar nav) +
the v0.37.0 trash/bulk-restore feature that the original filing
didn't list. Total scope: 6 help topics × 2 languages = 12 new
Markdown pages.

### Pre-Coding-Reality-Check finding

The user's session prompt asked for "10 sites remaining" Toggle
migration sweep as Task 2. Audit found the SETT-PHASE-3 archive
entry (482c685, 2026-05-26) had explicitly documented that the
remaining checkbox sites are intentional design-intent
exemptions — NOT deferred work. Surfaced as STOP condition;
user adjudicated α (skip Task 2 + correct v0.38.0 CHANGELOG
mis-statement). Correction landed in commit ``2bd9ad4``.

### Strategy

Playwright-driven screenshots (per user direction) in the app's
default theme (warm-literary light) at 1280×800 viewport. New
manual-only ``screenshots`` Playwright project so the spec
doesn't fire on every ``make test`` (it resets DB state per-
test for seeded fixtures).

### Help pages shipped

1. ``settings/sidebar`` — Settings page sidebar nav (5 groups,
   mobile menu, URL deep-linking, legacy redirects). v0.38.0
   SETT-L-1.
2. ``editor/display-settings`` — toolbar popover for
   width/font/size/line-height + per-device persistence.
   v0.37.0 EDITOR-DISPLAY-SETTINGS-01.
3. ``editor/word-wrap`` — Alt+Z toggle + per-browser
   localStorage persistence. Was only in shortcuts.md before.
4. ``books/repository-url`` — optional Book.repository_url with
   git-sync read-precedence (managed vs manual mode). v0.37.0
   BOOK-REPOSITORY-URL-FIELD-01.
5. ``dashboard/pagination`` — "Mehr laden" + 10/25/50/100 page-
   size dropdown + persistence semantics + full-filtered-set
   selection. v0.37.0 DASHBOARD-PAGINATION-LOAD-MORE-01.
6. ``dashboard/trash-and-restore`` — 90-day soft-delete +
   bulk-restore Undo toast + auto-delete config. v0.37.0
   BULK-RESTORE-PARITY (Articles + Books).

### Screenshots

5 PNGs committed to ``docs/help/assets/screenshots/``:
``settings-sidebar.png``, ``editor-display-settings.png``,
``book-metadata-repository-url.png``, ``dashboard-pagination.png``,
``trash-and-restore.png``. Word-wrap page is text-only.

### Generator

New ``e2e/screenshots/help-docs.spec.ts`` + new "screenshots"
Playwright project in ``e2e/playwright.config.ts``. Invoke via:

```bash
cd e2e && npx playwright test --project=screenshots
```

The spec seeds the minimum state per test via the existing
``resetDb`` + ``createBook`` + ``createChapter`` helpers, then
writes PNGs. Re-run only when the screenshotted surface
changes. The committed PNGs render the help-doc site without
re-running Playwright.

### Navigation updates (_meta.yaml)

- New top-level "Dashboard" group with ``pagination`` +
  ``trash-and-restore`` children. The shared dashboard chrome
  applies to both Books and Articles, so a unified section is
  cleaner than duplicating under each.
- "Bücher / Books" gained ``repository-url`` child.
- "Editor" gained ``display-settings`` + ``word-wrap`` children.
- "Einstellungen / Settings" gained ``sidebar`` child as the
  new overview entry; ``danger-zone`` stays as the second
  child.

mkdocs.yml regenerated via ``make sync-mkdocs-nav``.
``make verify-docs-discipline`` green (verify-mkdocs-nav +
check-mkdocs-orphans).

### Commits

1. ``2bd9ad4`` — docs: fix post-v0.38.0 stale refs + correct
   Toggle-migration framing. README.md + README-de.md bumped
   from v0.36.0 → v0.38.0; CLAUDE.md headline trimmed (had
   v0.37.0 prose concatenated mid-paragraph from yesterday's
   release-doc-update Edit); Toggle "remaining 10 sites
   deferred" wording corrected to "intentional design-intent
   exemptions" in 3 surfaces.
2. ``383cfeb`` — docs(help): 21 files (12 Markdown + 5
   screenshots + 2 nav files + 1 Playwright project + 1
   playwright.config.ts edit). HELP-DOCS-V0.37.0-GAPS-01
   closed; SETT-L-1 sidebar + dashboard trash/restore added
   on top of the original filing's scope.

### Followups

- ``SETT-M-2-PER-TAB-SUBSECTION-HEADERS-01`` (P4) annotated
  as **partially shipped** — SectionHeader (per-TAB) shipped
  in SETT-QW-7; per-subsection-within-tab layer still pending
  (effort revised 3-4 → 2-3 commits).
- ``SETT-M-4-SETTINGS-SEARCH-01`` (P4) stays trigger-gated
  (user complaint OR 15+ tabs; currently 13).
- ``SETT-L-2-FULL-RESPONSIVE-AND-SEARCH-01`` (P5) stays
  speculative.

### Lessons-learned re-validated

- "Run vitest from `frontend/`" — N/A for Playwright (uses its
  own cwd via webServer config).
- "Real-world data audit BEFORE implementation" — the Task 2
  Pre-Coding-Reality-Check caught the Toggle-migration false
  framing before any code shipped.
- "Numeric claims verification" — book seeding count for
  dashboard-pagination screenshot re-verified after the first
  run only showed page-size dropdown (12 books < 25 default
  page size → no "Mehr laden"). Re-seeded with 30 books.

## Archived 2026-05-26 (SETT-L-1-SIDEBAR-REDESIGN-01 CLOSED — 5-commit ship; horizontal tab bar replaced by left-sidebar grouped nav)

User-pull trigger fired the same day: 13 tabs after SETT-AUTHORS-
TAB-CONSOLIDATION-01 closed earlier in the day produced a
horizontal scrollbar at the 900px max-width. The Settings page
redesign moved from P4 (deferred per the original filing) to
"do now" via a brief paste-in commit plan from the user.

### Pre-Inspection findings

- 13 tabs after the Authors-consolidation: erscheinungsbild +
  verhalten + editor + ai + autoren + topics + plugins +
  comments + backups + support (cond) + about + erweitert +
  danger_zone. The horizontal Radix.Tabs rendering overflowed
  the 900px content rail.
- The 4 settings tabs the original SETT-L-1 filing proposed
  (Authoring / Data / Meta / Danger) had drifted with the
  Phase-1/2/3 splits; the new design groups them as
  Darstellung (Erscheinungsbild, Verhalten, Editor) / Inhalt
  (KI-Assistent, Autoren, Themen) / System (Plugins, Kommentare,
  Backups, Erweitert) / Info (Über, Unterstützen-cond) /
  Gefahrenzone (danger).
- 3 existing E2E specs (about-dialog, trash-view-mode-defaults,
  article-topic-seo) reach the settings via ``settings-tab-*``
  testids; these MUST be preserved on the sidebar items.
- Radix.Tabs is also used by CreateBookModal +
  BookMetadataEditor + Help, so removing the import from
  Settings.tsx is correct but the package stays installed.

### Pre-Coding-Reality-Check finding

User's commit-plan design listed 11 items across 5 groups but
Settings.tsx ships 13 tabs. ``Verhalten`` + ``Erweitert`` weren't
slotted in any group. Surfaced as stop-condition to user; user
adjudicated (α): spec-omission — both tabs retain their content,
Verhalten → Darstellung group, Erweitert → System group.

### Strategy

Five coordinated commits, all atomic-green per the Vitest +
tsc + i18n-parity chain.

### Commit chain

1. **C1 (`85ae7fe`)** — `refactor(settings): replace horizontal
   tabs with sidebar layout`. New ``SettingsSidebar`` component
   (5-group nav, ``<nav>`` landmark, ``aria-current="page"``,
   plain buttons — no Radix-portal trap). New
   ``SettingsSidebar.module.css`` (structural shell, sticky
   positioning, independent scroll). ``Settings.tsx`` drops
   ``Tabs.Root/.List/.Trigger/.Content`` for conditional render
   keyed on ``activeTab``; ``?tab=`` URL routing preserved
   including ``LEGACY_TAB_REDIRECTS``. Canonical
   ``settings-tab-{value}`` testids preserved verbatim.
   ``Settings.module.css`` gains ``.layout`` grid (220px + 1fr,
   1180px outer cap) + responsive ``<=768px`` collapse.
   Vitest: 2063 → 2069 (+6 SettingsSidebar pins).

2. **C2 (`ddcbf45`)** — `refactor(settings): responsive sidebar
   (mobile collapse)`. Extracts the inline mobile dropdown into a
   dedicated ``SettingsMobileMenu`` component sharing the same
   ``groups`` data structure. Adds ``DropdownMenu.Separator``
   between groups inside the mobile popover so the group
   structure surfaces on mobile too. Vitest: 2069 → 2074 (+5
   trigger-only pins per the "Radix DropdownMenu + happy-dom is
   brittle" rule — popover content is E2E-only).

3. **C3 (`f1d72ad`)** — `feat(settings): sidebar group headers +
   Danger Zone visual treatment`. ``SidebarGroup`` gains optional
   ``label`` (visible ``<h2>``) + ``variant`` (drives the red
   accent + visual separation). 4 group headers render
   (Darstellung, Inhalt, System, Info); Danger Zone group has no
   header (single-item group; header would duplicate). Danger
   section adds a ``--border`` divider above + 16px margin; the
   red is the load-bearing destructive signal, not the line.
   ``<ul>`` carries ``aria-labelledby`` pointing at each
   heading. Vitest: 2074 → 2080 (+6 C3 pins).

4. **C4 (`b62a98a`)** — `feat(i18n): sidebar nav + group labels
   in 8 catalogs`. 5 keys × 8 catalogs = 40 cells:
   ``sidebar_nav`` + ``group_darstellung/inhalt/system/info``.
   DE canonical, EN direct-translation authored, ES/FR/EL/PT/TR/
   JA machine-translated and recorded in ``AUTO_TRANSLATED.md``
   for native-speaker review. EN group label is "Display" (not
   "Appearance") to avoid duplication with the ``tab_erscheinungsbild``
   item label. Parity: 51/51 tests pass.

5. **C5 (this commit)** — `docs(settings): close SETT-L-1 +
   archive + Playwright smoke`. Backlog entry removed; new
   ``e2e/smoke/settings-sidebar.spec.ts`` (7 cases) pins the
   wired-up page in a real browser including the deep-link
   ``?tab=`` preservation + legacy ``?tab=author`` →
   ``autoren`` redirect + Danger Zone visual cue.

### Verification

- pytest: unchanged (frontend-only refactor); i18n parity 51/51
  green after C4.
- Vitest: 2063 → 2080 (+17 net).
- tsc: clean throughout.
- Testid preservation: all 13 ``settings-tab-{value}`` testids
  intact; 3 existing E2E specs (about-dialog,
  trash-view-mode-defaults, article-topic-seo) keep working
  without modification.
- ``?tab=`` routing + ``LEGACY_TAB_REDIRECTS`` preserved.
- Mobile (<=768px): sidebar hides, DropdownMenu pattern stays
  with new group separators.

### Acceptance criteria — all met

| Criterion | Status |
|---|---|
| Horizontal scrollbar gone at 900px max-width | ✅ — sidebar 220px + content 900px fits in 1180px outer container |
| 13 sections grouped into 5 themes | ✅ — Darstellung (3), Inhalt (3), System (4), Info (2), Gefahrenzone (1) |
| Danger Zone visually separated + red accent | ✅ — ``--border`` divider + 16px margin + ``--danger`` color |
| URL deep-links preserved | ✅ — ``?tab=`` routing + legacy redirects + Playwright spec |
| i18n parity 75/75 (now 80/80 after +5 keys) | ✅ — 51/51 parity tests green |
| Sidebar testid namespace preserved | ✅ — all 13 ``settings-tab-{value}`` testids unchanged |
| Mobile responsive | ✅ — <=768px collapses to DropdownMenu with group separators |

### Followups

None. The "Effort: 8-10 commits" estimate from the original
filing was conservative; the refined 5-commit plan from the
user closed the work without scope cuts.

### Related to lessons-learned

This work re-validated three existing disciplines without
generating new rules:

- "Testid namespace pinning prevents silent E2E skips" — the
  ``settings-tab-{value}`` preservation across the redesign
  kept 3 specs green without any spec edits.
- "Radix DropdownMenu + happy-dom is brittle for Vitest" — the
  C2 mobile-menu test pinned trigger-only per this rule;
  popover content lives in the C5 Playwright spec.
- "Pre-Coding-Reality-Check: re-audit at the keystroke" — the
  Verhalten + Erweitert spec-omission caught at C1 keystroke
  time; user adjudicated before any code shipped.

## Archived 2026-05-26 (SETT-AUTHORS-TAB-CONSOLIDATION-01 CLOSED — 2-commit ship; Autor + Autoren-Datenbank consolidated into single Autoren tab)

Filed and shipped mid-session 2026-05-26 per user adjudication
after the three Settings UX phases (Phase 1 + Phase 2 + Phase 3)
all closed. The new spec arrived as a parallel-agent message
written against pre-Phase-2 state (HEAD `b62c698`) and would
have re-implemented work already shipped; the only actionable
delta was the author-tab consolidation. User confirmed "ship it
in this session" without filing as a backlog item first.

### Pre-Inspection findings

- ``AuthorSettings.tsx`` (122 LOC): author profile — real name +
  pen names. Save envelope: ``{author: {name, pen_names}}`` via
  ``api.settings.updateApp``.
- ``AuthorsDatabase.tsx`` (405 LOC): CRUD over known authors
  via ``api.authors.*``. Self-contained — no props, own save
  flow.
- The two save flows are **independent**. Consolidation is
  purely a UI-grouping change with zero behavior risk.
- Existing per-component tests (``AuthorSettings.test.tsx`` 10
  cases + ``AuthorsDatabase.test.tsx``) render each component
  in isolation, NOT via the Settings page — so they remain
  unchanged after consolidation.
- Consumers needing updates: ``e2e/smoke/settings-author.spec.ts``
  (3x ``?tab=author``), ``e2e/tests/ux-audit-group3.spec.ts``
  (04 case label).

### Strategy

Build a **thin wrapper** ``AutorenSettings`` that mounts both
existing components unchanged. Each child keeps its own
``SectionHeader`` + ``card`` shell, so:
- Existing testids preserved verbatim (no E2E testid drift).
- Existing per-component Vitest files unchanged.
- Zero behaviour change in either save flow.

### Commits

1. `e45d8ae` — refactor(settings): consolidate Autor +
   Autoren-Datenbank into Autoren tab. New
   ``AutorenSettings.tsx`` + ``AutorenSettings.test.tsx`` (1
   Vitest pinning the composition contract). Settings.tsx tab
   list updated (drop ``author`` + ``authors_database``, add
   ``autoren``). New ``LEGACY_TAB_REDIRECTS`` map preserves
   bookmarks. 8 i18n catalogs gain ``tab_autoren``. E2E spec
   updates.
2. (this commit) — docs(backlog): close
   SETT-AUTHORS-TAB-CONSOLIDATION-01 + archive entry.

### Test signal

Vitest 2062 → 2063 (+1 from
``AutorenSettings.test.tsx``). i18n parity 75/75. tsc clean.

### Intentional decisions

- **Thin-wrapper composition (not flattened merge)**: keeping
  the two child components as-is preserved all 10 of the
  ``AuthorSettings.test.tsx`` cases + the full
  ``AuthorsDatabase.test.tsx`` suite without changes. A
  flattened-merge variant would have forced rewriting both
  test files for ~zero user-visible benefit.
- **``LEGACY_TAB_REDIRECTS`` map** instead of just updating
  consumers: covers the broader risk surface (help-doc
  ``?tab=author`` links, user bookmarks, external
  documentation) — the e2e spec updates are belt-and-braces.
- **``tab_author`` + ``tab_authors_database`` i18n keys
  retained**: matches the Phase 2 ``tab_general`` precedent.
  An i18n-cleanup pass can drop them later.
- **No backlog round-trip**: user explicitly requested mid-
  session ship without filing as a backlog item first ("Not
  a backlog item, ship it in this session.").

### Cross-references

- ``SETT-PHASE-1`` / ``SETT-PHASE-2`` / ``SETT-PHASE-3``
  (all closed 2026-05-26): the consolidation builds on the
  ``SectionHeader`` infrastructure from Phase 1 and the
  Allgemein-tab-split from Phase 2.
- Multi-tool collaboration drift surfaced when the user-side
  Phase 2 spec arrived during this session referencing a stale
  HEAD; the status-correction protocol (per the
  ``lessons-learned.md`` "Multi-tool collaboration tracking"
  rule) identified the consolidation as the only actionable
  delta. Working as designed.

## Archived 2026-05-26 (SETT-PHASE-3-TOGGLE-COMPONENT-01 CLOSED — 4-commit ship; shared Toggle composition component + 5-site migration)

Filed 2026-05-25 from the post-v0.37.0 Settings-page UX audit per
user adjudication (Phase 1 then Phase 2 then Phase 3, all
immediate post-release). Extracts a shared ``<Toggle>``
composition component for the recurring checkbox-with-description
pattern across Settings sub-components and migrates the
canonical-shape sites.

### Pre-Inspection findings

The Settings page's checkbox-style settings followed three
distinct patterns:

1. **Canonical shape** (label + HelpText description below): 5
   sites — VerhaltenSettings (3: trash-enabled / delete-
   permanently / allow-without-author), AiAssistantSettings (1:
   ai-enable), AudiobookSettingsPanel (1: readChapterNumber).
2. **Inline label-after-checkbox**: 2 sites
   (AudiobookSettingsPanel highQualityOnly, TranslationSettings-
   Panel freeApi). Already simple; Toggle adds no value.
3. **List-row** (strong+span side-by-side, no description): 3
   sites in ErweitertSettings white-label-core-* loop. Different
   structural shape; intentional asymmetry per the RCU rule.

Plus 1 site in ``ScalarSettingField`` (generic plugin-setting
renderer) — out of scope for Settings-specific component.

The audit's "~15 checkbox sites" framing was rough; the
canonical-shape count was 5.

### Toggle API

``<Toggle label description checked onChange testId
indentedDescription>{children}</Toggle>``

The ``children`` slot lets nested conditional controls (e.g. a
follow-up RadixSelect that only renders when the toggle is on)
sit between the checkbox row and the description without
fighting the layout. ``indentedDescription`` matches the
HelpText ``indented`` prop for descriptions that should align
under the label rather than under the checkbox.

### Commits

1. `cabd51c` — feat(settings): add Toggle composition component.
   New ``Toggle.tsx`` + ``Toggle.test.tsx`` (6 Vitest cases:
   shape, no-description-no-paragraph, description-as-HelpText,
   indented-description, children slot, onChange wiring).
2. `917122b` — refactor(settings): migrate VerhaltenSettings to
   Toggle. 3 sites — trash-enabled uses the ``children`` slot
   for the nested trash-days RadixSelect; delete-permanently +
   allow-books-without-author use indentedDescription. Existing
   testids preserved on the internal ``<input>``.
3. `1404cc0` — refactor(settings): migrate AI + Audiobook
   checkboxes to Toggle. 2 sites — ai-enable (indented) +
   readChapterNumber (non-indented). Drops the now-unused
   ``HelpText`` import from ``AudiobookSettingsPanel.tsx``.
   Adds ``audiobook-read-chapter-number`` testid (positive
   coverage; didn't exist before).
4. (this commit) — docs(backlog): close SETT-PHASE-3-TOGGLE-
   COMPONENT-01 + archive entry.

### Test signal

Vitest 2056 → 2062 (+6 from Toggle.test.tsx). The 5 migration
sites land without testid changes (testids preserved verbatim on
the inner ``<input>``), so VerhaltenSettings.test.tsx + the
other consumer tests pass without changes. tsc clean across all
4 commits.

### Intentional decisions

- **5-site migration scope (not the audit's ~15)**: pre-
  inspection sub-categorised the checkbox sites; only the
  canonical-shape pattern (5 sites) fits ``Toggle``'s API. The
  inline label-after-checkbox sites + the list-row sites + the
  generic plugin renderer stay distinct per the RCU rule's
  intentional-asymmetry override.
- **``children`` slot for trash-enabled**: the conditional
  trash-days RadixSelect is structurally a follow-up control,
  not a description. Putting it in ``description`` would force
  the dynamic ``trash_info`` text up into a less prominent
  location and break the visual hierarchy. The children-between-
  row-and-description shape preserves both.
- **New ``audiobook-read-chapter-number`` testid**: positive
  testid coverage per the rule "testid-namespace pinning
  prevents silent E2E skips". The original site had no testid
  at all.

### Cross-references

- ``SETT-PHASE-1-QUICK-WINS-01`` (closed 2026-05-26): Phase 1
  paved the way by extracting ``HelpText`` (Toggle composes
  HelpText for its description) and ``SectionHeader``.
- ``SETT-PHASE-2-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-SPLIT-01`` (closed 2026-05-26):
  Phase 2 re-grouped the checkboxes into the Verhalten tab +
  Erweitert tab, which made the Toggle migration cleaner — most
  consumers now live in one focused tab.

## Archived 2026-05-26 (SETT-PHASE-2-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-SPLIT-01 CLOSED — 5-commit ship; Settings UX Phase 2 Allgemein-tab split)

Filed 2026-05-25 from the post-v0.37.0 Settings-page UX audit per
user adjudication (Phase 1 then Phase 2 then Phase 3, all
immediate post-release). Splits the catch-all "Allgemein" tab
into three focused tabs and lifts White-Label customisation into
its own dedicated tab.

### Pre-Inspection findings

After Phase 1 shipped, the Allgemein tab still mixed three
distinct concerns inside `AppSettings.tsx` (411 LOC): theme +
dashboard views, language + trash + permission flags, and
SshKeySection + White-Label. Audit-pull from SETT-M-1: each
concern deserves its own tab so the page becomes scannable.

The spec named three replacement tabs (Erscheinungsbild +
Verhalten + Editor) plus an Erweitert tab for White-Label, but
left SshKeySection's placement unaddressed. Decision: place in
Erweitert alongside White-Label. Both are power-user concerns;
the tab label "Erweitert" signals opt-in.

Tab count: 12 (post-Phase-1) → 14 (post-Phase-2). The
`.radix-tabs-list` has `overflow-x: auto + white-space: nowrap`,
so the bar scrolls horizontally rather than wrapping. Mobile
keeps using the hamburger. SETT-L-1 (sidebar redesign, P4)
remains deferred.

### Commits

1. `b194ddf` — refactor(settings): extract ErscheinungsbildSettings
   tab. New component hosting Theme RadixSelect + the 4
   Dashboard-View selects in the Standard-Ansichten sub-card from
   SETT-QW-1. Save envelope: `{ui: {theme, dashboard: {...}}}`.
   2 Vitest cases.
2. `86e95bc` — refactor(settings): extract VerhaltenSettings
   tab. New component hosting Language RadixSelect + trash-
   enabled / trash-days / delete-permanently / allow-books-
   without-author checkboxes. Save envelope: `{app: {...}}`
   preserving the live-language-switch handler.
   3 Vitest cases.
3. `017acf1` — refactor(settings): extract ErweitertSettings
   tab. New component hosting SshKeySection + the uncollapsed
   White-Label card. The Phase 1 Radix Collapsible wrapper is
   dropped because the tab itself is the affordance. Save
   envelope: `{ui: {title, subtitle}, plugins: {enabled}}`
   preserving the non-core-plugin merge logic.
   3 Vitest cases.
4. `2b28d17` — refactor(settings): remove obsolete AppSettings
   + Allgemein tab. Deletes `AppSettings.tsx` + the matching
   test file. Removes `"app"` from `VALID_SETTINGS_TABS`, drops
   the Allgemein entry from `tabDefs`, removes the
   `<Tabs.Content value="app">` block. Default `initialTab`
   moves from `"app"` to `"erscheinungsbild"`. Updates:
   `back-button-navigation.test.tsx` stub list,
   `e2e/smoke/trash-view-mode-defaults.spec.ts` (5x
   `settings-tab-app` → `settings-tab-erscheinungsbild`,
   4x `settings-save` → `erscheinungsbild-settings-save`),
   `e2e/tests/ux-audit-group3.spec.ts` (label retarget).
5. (this commit) — docs(backlog): close
   SETT-PHASE-2-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-SPLIT-01 + archive entry.

### Test signal

Vitest 2052 → 2056 (+4 net; +11 cases shipped across the 4 new
test files, -7 cases lost with `AppSettings.test.tsx` deletion).
i18n parity 75/75. tsc clean across all 5 commits.

### i18n hygiene

10 new keys × 8 catalogs (80 string entries):
- `tab_erscheinungsbild` + `erscheinungsbild_title` +
  `erscheinungsbild_description` (3 keys)
- `tab_verhalten` + `verhalten_title` +
  `verhalten_description` (3 keys)
- `tab_erweitert` + `erweitert_title` +
  `erweitert_description` (3 keys)
- (the Phase-1 `tab_editor` keys carried over unchanged)

`ui.settings.tab_general` ("Allgemein" / "General" / local
equivalents) stays in all 8 catalogs as an orphaned key —
matches the SETT-QW-6 precedent of keeping
`white_label_hide` for backwards-compat. An i18n-cleanup pass
can drop both later.

### Intentional decisions

- **SshKeySection in Erweitert (not its own "Git" tab)**: the
  spec was silent; Erweitert collects "advanced/power-user"
  concerns naturally.
- **White-Label uncollapsed in Erweitert**: once the tab label
  itself signals advanced opt-in, the Phase 1 Collapsible
  wrapper adds no value. Card stays a card.
- **`tab_general` i18n key retained**: catalog hygiene deferred
  per the SETT-QW-6 precedent.

### Cross-references

## Archived 2026-05-26 (SETT-PHASE-1-QUICK-WINS-01 CLOSED — 9-commit ship; Settings UX Phase 1 quick-win bundle)

Filed 2026-05-25 from the post-v0.37.0 Settings-page UX audit
per user adjudication. Bundle of 7 quick wins targeted at
visual hygiene + structural clarity of the Settings page that
the audit identified during the pre-release sweep.

Pre-Inspection finding: the Settings page had grown organically
since v0.30.0 with three classes of audit-surfaced issues:
(1) **visual drift** — inline `<h2 style={{margin: 0}}>`
fragments coexisting with the canonical `styles.sectionTitle`
class across BackupsSettings, AboutSettings, DangerZoneSettings,
plus 3 inconsistent font sizes (0.7 / 0.75 / 0.8125rem) for the
small italic help-text under inputs in ~30 sites;
(2) **structural ambiguity** — 4 dashboard-view selects sitting
flat in the AppSettings card with no visual grouping,
SshKeySection floating between cards with no separator, the
Editor settings block hidden inside the catch-all "Allgemein"
tab; (3) **affordance opacity** — White-Label configuration
behind a bare Wrench-icon button few users would discover, and
no per-section descriptions matching the Notion / Linear
convention.

Ship shape: 9 commits across one session, all green
individually. Tab count grew from 11 → 12 (the Editor
extraction). The Phase 2 work (SETT-PHASE-2-ALLGEMEIN-TAB-SPLIT-
01) and Phase 3 (SETT-PHASE-3-TOGGLE-COMPONENT-01) stay queued
for separate sessions per the user adjudication.

## Archived 2026-05-25 (EDITOR-DISPLAY-SETTINGS-01 CLOSED — 6-commit ship; per-device editor display preferences via toolbar popover)

Filed 2026-05-25 via the post-v0.36.0 ROADMAP refresh under
"Editor Display Preferences". User-pull came from authors who
want control over text width / font / size / line-height during
writing — the kind of in-editor display preferences Scrivener,
iA Writer, and Ulysses surface in their settings panes.

Pre-Inspection finding: editor width is NOT currently
constrained (`.tiptap-editor` + `.ProseMirror` fill their
parent). Font / size / line-height ARE styled via `.tiptap-
editor`'s existing CSS literals. Width control would be NEW.

Persistence-pattern fact-check: the prompt initially said
"persist via app.yaml user-overlay, per the pattern from word-
wrap" — but word-wrap is localStorage-backed, not app.yaml.
User adjudicated α (per-device localStorage) over β (per-
account app.yaml). Width preference is genuinely device-
dependent (different monitor sizes); font + size + line-height
preferences pair naturally with word-wrap conceptually (users
will group these toggles mentally).

### Scope shipped (6 commits, ``6197c35..2fb82f4``)

- **C1 (``6197c35``)**: `useEditorDisplaySettings()` hook in
  `frontend/src/hooks/useEditorDisplaySettings.ts`. Four
  preferences (width / fontFamily / fontSize / lineHeight) each
  with a 3-4 value enum. localStorage key
  `bibliogon-editor-display-settings` (mirrors useWordWrap
  precedent). CSS variables applied to
  `document.documentElement` so they cascade into every editor
  surface. Defaults match pre-feature literals (width=full →
  "none", font=serif → var(--font-display), size=medium →
  1.125rem, line=relaxed → 1.8). Width presets per reading-
  research recommendations (narrow=680px ≈ 45-55 chars at
  16-18px; medium=780px; wide=900px; full=none). 11 Vitest
  cases.
- **C2 (``77b0f29``)**: `<EditorDisplaySettingsPopover>` —
  toolbar button + click-toggleable settings panel with 4
  native `<select>`s + reset. Plain controlled-visibility +
  click-outside + Escape-close pattern (no Radix popover dep;
  no DropdownMenu happy-dom flake per the existing lessons-
  learned rule). 11 Vitest cases.
- **C3 (``b2e61af``)**: `.tiptap-editor` wired to read four
  `var()` references with fallbacks matching the pre-feature
  literals. Width applied via `max-width` on the inner
  `.ProseMirror` with `margin: 0 auto` so constrained text
  centers in the editor pane. Pre-feature snapshot tests stay
  green because the var() fallback chain matches the prior
  literals.
- **C4 (``b726814``)**: hook + popover mounted in
  `components/Editor.tsx` (just below the Toolbar, right-
  aligned). Single change covers BOTH chapter-based BookEditor
  AND ArticleEditor since they both import the same Editor
  surface. Picture-book + comic-book editors don't use
  Editor.tsx; the CSS vars still cascade globally, so a future
  RichTextEditor mount could add its own popover button
  without duplicating the storage logic.
- **C5 (``6cb3606``)**: 20 i18n keys × 8 catalogs under the
  new `ui.editor_display.*` namespace. DE real umlauts, EL/JA
  native scripts, FR typography spacing + accents, EN/ES/PT/TR
  per existing catalog style. Block placed BEFORE the existing
  `editor:` section so the two related namespaces stay
  neighbours.
- **C6 (``2fb82f4``)**: 2 Playwright smoke tests pinning the
  width-preset → CSS-var write + reload-persistence chain AND
  the reset → all-four-vars-restored chain. Uses
  `page.evaluate(getComputedStyle...)` to read vars directly
  off `document.documentElement` for assertion stability.

### Result

- Frontend Vitest: +22 new cases (11 hook + 11 component).
- i18n parity: 75/75 across 8 catalogs.
- tsc clean throughout. Playwright spec parses + lists 2 tests.

### Architectural rationale

α (per-device localStorage) was picked over β (per-account
YAML) because:

- Width preference IS device-dependent (different monitor
  sizes); forcing the same width on every device is the wrong
  shape for this preference class.
- Pairs conceptually with word-wrap (Alt+Z toggle is also per-
  device, also localStorage); users will group these editor-
  visual toggles together mentally.
- Simpler implementation (no backend schema change, no
  settings PATCH validator, no api.settings round-trip on
  every change).
- The design-intent-axis lessons-learned rule applies: per-
  device + per-account are GENUINELY different semantics; the
  existing useViewMode (per-account) and useWordWrap (per-
  device) hooks ship side-by-side for that reason.

### Cross-tab sync deferred

Multiple tabs open on the same browser would NOT auto-sync
mid-session — each tab reads localStorage once at mount, then
writes on change. Cross-tab sync via the `storage` event is
deferred until a user reports it; the per-tab session-scope is
the v1 MVP.

### Follow-up candidates (not filed)

- **Picture-book / comic-book editors** — currently use their
  own RichTextEditor / ComicBookEditor surfaces (not Editor.tsx),
  so the popover isn't reachable from those editors yet. The
  CSS vars still cascade. If the user requests per-editor-
  surface popover access, mounting the existing component +
  hook into those surfaces is ~2-3 commits.
- **Cross-tab sync** — `addEventListener("storage", ...)` in the
  hook would re-read localStorage when another tab writes.
  Defer until needed.
- **Custom CSS-variable values** — slider for width / size
  instead of preset enums. Defer; preset enums match Scrivener
  / iA Writer convention and avoid the "pixel-perfect
  optimization rabbit-hole" UX class.

---

## Archived 2026-05-25 (BOOK-REPOSITORY-URL-FIELD-01 CLOSED — 5-commit ship; manual git-repo URL field on Book metadata with plugin-git-sync read-precedence)

Filed 2026-05-25 via the post-v0.36.0 ROADMAP refresh under
"Book Metadata Extensions". User-pull came from authors who
track their book project in a git repository outside
plugin-git-sync (manually-created repos that are independently
versioned without using the import / commit-back round-trip).

Pre-Inspection finding: `GitSyncMapping.repo_url` already exists
but has NOT NULL constraints on `last_imported_commit_sha` +
`local_clone_path` — only books imported via plugin-git-sync
have a mapping. The manual-tracking case (book authored in
Bibliogon, separately versioned externally) had nowhere to
record the URL.

User adjudicated path α (additive): add `Book.repository_url`
nullable. The new field surfaces in BookMetadataEditor; when
GitSyncMapping exists, the field renders read-only with the
canonical mapping URL.

### Scope shipped (5 commits, ``8a8a11b..55829b8``)

- **C1 (``8a8a11b``)**: backend `Book.repository_url` Mapped[str
  | None] String(2000) nullable + Pydantic BookUpdate + BookOut
  edits + Alembic migration `s8c9d0e1f234` (batch_alter_table
  add_column; downgrade drop_column; reversible). 9 pytest
  cases covering model defaults / Pydantic accept / explicit
  None / serialization / patch round-trip / clear-to-null /
  omit-leaves-intact / long-URL within 2000-char cap / not on
  BookCreate.
- **C2 (``1659f5b``)**: frontend `Book.repository_url:
  string | null` in api/client.ts + 4 test-fixture files
  updated with `repository_url: null,` to satisfy the strict
  Book type (useBookFilters.test.ts, SaveAsTemplateModal.test.tsx,
  BookEditor.test.tsx, ExportPackage.test.tsx).
- **C3 (``58a885a``)**: BookMetadataEditor General-tab field via
  new `RepositoryUrlField` sub-component. Two render shapes:
  free-input branch (editing `Book.repository_url`) when no
  GitSyncMapping; read-only branch (surfacing
  `GitSyncMappingStatus.repo_url`) when a mapping exists. Per-
  book `gitSync.status` fetch on mount + on book.id change;
  silent failure falls back to the free-input branch. 5 new
  Vitest cases (66 → 71 in BookMetadataEditor.test.tsx).
- **C4 (``c59a20a``)**: 4 i18n keys × 8 catalogs
  (`ui.metadata.repository_url{,_placeholder,_hint,_managed_hint}`)
  with per-language diacritic convention preserved (DE real
  umlauts, EL/JA native scripts, FR typography spacing,
  EN/ES/PT/TR ASCII). i18n parity 75/75 held.
- **C5 (``55829b8``)**: 2 Playwright smoke tests pinning the
  free-input branch round-trip + clear-to-null. The read-only
  branch (plugin-git-sync-managed) is Vitest-covered; setting up
  a real GitSyncMapping for an E2E smoke is out of scope.

### Result

- Backend pytest: 2260 → 2269 (+9).
- Frontend Vitest: 66 → 71 in the touched file (other test files
  unchanged; +5 in this commit chain).
- i18n parity: 75/75 across 8 catalogs.
- tsc clean throughout. Playwright spec parses + lists 2 tests.

### Architectural rationale

α was picked over β (relax GitSyncMapping constraints) + γ
(surface-only, no manual entry) because:

- α is additive (nullable column on Book; no migration risk on
  GitSyncMapping's NOT NULL contract that plugin-git-sync's
  round-trip code depends on).
- α covers BOTH user shapes — git-sync-imported books (read
  from GitSyncMapping) AND manually-tracked books (read from
  Book.repository_url) — with a single UI surface that picks
  the right source based on `mapped: true/false`.
- The two storage shapes serve different lifecycles: the
  mapping is owned by plugin-git-sync (round-trip state) and
  the column is owned by the author (loose metadata
  reference). No competing source-of-truth: the UI's read-
  precedence (mapping wins when present) makes the
  relationship explicit.

## Archived 2026-05-25 (COMMENTS-ADMIN-PAGINATION-01 CLOSED — already-shipped; audit-finding was stale at filing time)

Filed 2026-05-15 by UX-Full-Audit G2-F3 against an observation
that "Comments admin tab renders all 49 comment rows in a single
DOM table without pagination or virtualization." The audit's
recommendation was "add pagination OR virtualization OR a hard
cap with 'Show all' affordance."

### Why closed without code

The fix was already in production THREE DAYS BEFORE the audit
filed the entry: commit ``fe55add`` (2026-05-12, "feat(frontend):
Settings comments-admin tab (list + filter + paginate)") shipped
the load-more pattern from day one. ``CommentsAdminSection.tsx``
has carried:

  - ``const PAGE_SIZE = 100;`` (line 37)
  - ``const [pageLimit, setPageLimit] = useState(PAGE_SIZE);``
    (line 86)
  - ``setPageLimit(PAGE_SIZE);`` reset on filter change (line 186)
  - ``setPageLimit((prev) => Math.min(prev + PAGE_SIZE, 500))``
    on Load-more click (line 1109)
  - ``data-testid="comments-admin-load-more"`` button (line 1107)

since fe55add. Server cap also enforced (500). The audit's
recommendation #1 (pagination) was already fulfilled at audit
time. Recommendations #2 (virtualization) + #3 (hard cap with
"Show all") are not needed — load-more is the lightest-touch
fix the audit itself recommended.

### Discovery context

Surfaced during the backlog walk that followed
``DASHBOARD-PAGINATION-LOAD-MORE-01`` close. The Pre-Inspection
for that ship had already read ``CommentsAdminSection.tsx`` end-
to-end as the prior-art reference for the new
``usePagedList`` hook — so the load-more infrastructure was
fresh in mind. The "trigger audit" pass through the deferred
backlog surfaced this entry's claim ("renders all comments in
a single DOM table without pagination") as factually wrong vs
current code.

### Closeable-stale-entry pattern

This is the inverse of the "Operational gaps masquerade as
wired infrastructure" lessons-learned rule: shipped
infrastructure was masquerading as an open gap. The pattern:
an audit observation taken at moment-T points at code that
gets fixed at T-N (N > 0), but the audit doc is filed unaware
of the fix. The entry then sits as a deferred backlog item
forever because its trigger ("user >200 comments OR Settings
sluggishness complaint") will never fire — the underlying
issue is gone.

Routine periodic backlog audits should add a "claim-vs-code
verification" pass for items filed by analyses against
moving-target state. The grep cost is small (one
``data-testid`` lookup per item); the noise-reduction value
is real.

### Future RCU candidate (filed implicitly)

The DASHBOARD-PAGINATION-LOAD-MORE-01 archive entry already
notes CommentsAdminSection as the 3rd candidate site for the
new ``usePagedList`` hook + ``PageSizeSelector`` component.
The current hardcoded ``PAGE_SIZE = 100`` could become user-
selectable via the new component. This is a separate concern
from "is CommentsAdmin paginated?" — that question is now
firmly answered ``yes``. The hook-extraction is filed via the
existing DASHBOARD-PAGINATION archive note; no new ID needed
unless a 4th consumer surfaces.

---

## Archived 2026-05-25 (DASHBOARD-PAGINATION-LOAD-MORE-01 CLOSED — 8-commit ship; Book + Article dashboards now paginated)

Filed 2026-05-25 from a pagination-pattern investigation that
identified the Book + Article dashboards as the only top-level
list surfaces fetching + rendering the full row set in one
batch. Trigger was deferred (latent, no user pain at the ~209
reference scale) but the scope + commit plan were locked in
at filing time; this archival ships exactly the planned 8-
commit shape with no scope creep.

### Scope shipped (8 commits, ``822050c..277dd1d``)

- **C1 (``822050c``)**: backend ``limit: int | None`` Query on
  ``GET /api/books`` + ``GET /api/articles`` with ``ge=1,
  le=1000`` bounds. Default ``None`` preserves the historical
  no-cap behaviour for non-dashboard callers (BookEditor
  navigation, backup, etc.). 10 pytest cases (5 each on books +
  articles) cover cap, ordering preservation under filter+limit
  composition, no-limit-returns-all backwards-compat, zero /
  negative 422 guard, above-cap 422 guard.
- **C2 (``dccbd58``)**: PATCH ``/api/settings/app`` validates
  ``ui.dashboard.{books,articles}_page_size`` against the enum
  {10, 25, 50, 100}; out-of-enum values produce 400 with a
  precise detail naming the offending key. Validation fires
  BEFORE the merge so invalid requests never reach disk. 5 new
  pytest cases.
- **C3 (``0bdaa3c``)**: ``usePagedList(scope)`` hook in
  ``frontend/src/hooks/usePagedList.ts``. Manages ``pageSize``
  (persistent, server-backed) + ``limit`` (ephemeral display
  cap). Read-merge-write on persist mirrors the existing
  ``useViewMode`` shape — sibling keys (other scope's page
  size, books_view, etc.) survive every write. 10 Vitest cases.
- **C4 (``be4e82d``)**: ``<PageSizeSelector>`` stateless
  ``<select>`` for the 4 allowed values. Native select chosen
  over Radix Select for happy-dom ergonomics + keyboard a11y
  by default. 5 Vitest cases.
- **C5 (``74dc8c6``)**: wire into ``pages/Dashboard.tsx``.
  Client-side slicing chosen over server-side limit because
  ``useBookFilters`` lives client-side; sending the limit to
  the server would mean filtering AFTER limiting, producing
  the awkward "Load more to see more matches" UX. Selection
  semantics preserved: select-all still operates on the full
  filtered set, not just the visible page.
- **C6 (``c35c628``)**: symmetric wire into
  ``pages/ArticleList.tsx``. Per the Articles-vs-Books
  parallel-surface asymmetry discipline, both surfaces shipped
  in a single coordinated session with mirrored testid
  namespaces (``dashboard-*`` vs ``article-list-*``).
- **C7 (``29177dc``)**: ``ui.dashboard.load_more`` +
  ``ui.dashboard.page_size_label`` keys in 8 i18n catalogs.
  i18n parity test 75/75 green; each catalog uses its
  established diacritic convention (DE real umlauts; EL/JA
  native scripts; FR typography spacing; EN/ES/PT/TR ASCII
  prose per existing catalog style).
- **C8 (``277dd1d``)**: 4 Playwright smoke tests (2 per
  surface) pinning load-more growth (via counted-tile
  assertions, avoiding flake-prone CSS selectors) + page-size
  dropdown persistence via PATCH ``/api/settings/app``.

### Result

- Backend: 2260 passed (was 2214 pre-session; +46 includes the
  C1 + C2 additions plus other in-flight tests).
- Frontend Vitest: 2010 passed (was 1986 baseline; +24
  includes the C3 + C4 additions plus other in-flight tests).
- i18n parity: 75/75 across all 8 catalogs.
- tsc clean. Playwright spec parses + lists 4 tests.

### RCU note

CommentsAdminSection.tsx is now the 3rd candidate site for the
same hook + selector component combination (it already runs
its own load-more pattern with a hardcoded PAGE_SIZE = 100).
Filed implicitly as a follow-up via the original backlog
entry's "RCU follow-up filed implicitly via this entry"
clause; not blocking, no separate ID needed unless a 4th
consumer surfaces.

## Archived 2026-05-25 (PLUGIN-COMICS-E2E-SMOKE-01 CLOSED — live-dev plugin-info smoke + stale version-assertion fix; 1 commit)

Filed 2026-05-18 by plugin-comics Session 1 smoke as the
operational-class gap that pytest-with-TestClient masks: a
broken plugin-load path (stale entry points, env-var
absence, post-install rediscover gap) silently passes in
pytest because the lifespan + plugin discovery run fresh per
test, but 404s against a long-running uvicorn. Trigger
"plugin-comics Session 2 starts" fired in v0.36.0; closed
2026-05-25.

### Scope shipped (1 commit, this archive entry)

- ``e2e/smoke/comic-book-editor.spec.ts``: new test
  ``plugin-info panel renders + no plugin-unreachable
  alert``. Creates a ``book_type = "comic_book"`` book,
  opens the editor, asserts the green
  ``comic-book-editor-plugin-info`` panel is visible AND
  contains the string ``"comics"`` (matches "comics v1.X.Y
  (session N)" without pinning version + session numbers
  that float across releases), AND asserts the
  ``comic-book-editor-plugin-error`` role="alert" element
  is absent (negative-path regression-pin against any
  future plugin-load break).
- ``e2e/smoke/user-overlay-migration.spec.ts``: Boy-Scout
  fix on the sibling smoke. The
  ``/api/comics/info responds 200 from the live stack``
  case previously asserted ``body.version === "1.0.0"``;
  Session 2 bumped the comics plugin to ``1.1.0`` and the
  hardcoded version became a latent stale-pin bug. Bumped
  to ``expect(body.version).toMatch(/^1\./)`` so the
  assertion survives future patch / minor bumps without
  test churn. Why the bug went unnoticed: this spec only
  runs when there's a real uvicorn at ``localhost:8000``
  AND the user-overlay parsing test was the headline of
  this file, so the version-pin test inherited the same
  reachability. The bump pre-empts a CI false-positive
  whenever this spec next runs.

### What was NOT touched (per the filing's "single
instance is incident, not pattern" discipline)

- ``LIVE-DEV-SMOKE-INFRASTRUCTURE-01`` (P4 if it gets
  filed): the original filing said "if a SECOND plugin
  needs the same pattern, extract a shared infrastructure
  item per the RCU 2-surfaces threshold". Today only
  plugin-comics needs this; no infrastructure extraction
  triggered. Filing deferred until a real 2nd plugin
  surfaces the same operational-gap pattern.

### Why this matters as a discipline-pin

The new test catches a class of bug that pytest cannot
catch by construction. Per the
"Operational gaps masquerade as wired infrastructure"
lessons-learned rule, any wired plugin-discovery /
entry-point path that LOOKS right in pytest can be silently
broken in the long-running production process. The live-dev
spec is the only mechanism that runs the actual code path
the user sees.

### Cross-references

- ``backend/app/main.py`` (USER-OVERLAY-PLUGIN-ENABLE-MIGRATION-01,
  the sibling C4 spec)
- ``plugins/bibliogon-plugin-comics/bibliogon_comics/routes.py``
  (the ``/api/comics/info`` endpoint under test)
- ``frontend/src/components/ComicBookEditor.tsx``
  (the ``pluginInfo`` / ``pluginError`` state-machine the
  test pins)

## Archived 2026-05-23 (DANGER-ZONE-RESET-EVERYTHING-01 CLOSED — full-system reset feature shipped post-v0.36.0; 5 commits)

User-directed feature shipped directly from a session directive
(no prior backlog entry). Modelled on the adaptive-learner
"reset everything" pattern but adapted to Bibliogon's single-
user local-first reality: no `user_id` to preserve, no
encryption-key concerns, just a clean factory-reset of all
user-created data behind a three-step HMAC-token-gated dialog.

### Investigations that informed the design

- **Data-landscape audit** (this session's earlier pre-inspection):
  catalogued 21 SQLite tables (all under `Base.metadata`, no
  plugin-side tables), 14 localStorage keys (mostly cosmetic
  prefs + 3 SSE F5-recovery handles), Dexie `BibliogonDB` with
  `drafts` table (the only real data-risk on browser clear),
  `<data_dir>` + `<config_dir>` split per `app.paths` (data_dir
  uploads + tmp + backup_history + config-overlays; config_dir
  holds `secrets.yaml`). Decided: data_dir wiped per file class,
  config_dir's launcher metadata preserved.
- **Identity-persistence investigation** (related directive,
  declined): confirmed Bibliogon has no `user_id`, no auth,
  no session, all durable data server-side. Browser-clear
  losses are cosmetic only (theme + dismissal flags). No
  `identity.yaml` filed; recommendation accepted by user.
- **User adjudications**: launcher `settings.json` preserved
  (OS-level install state, not user data); project-tree
  `licenses.json` untouched (licensing dormant); 5-minute token
  TTL; pre-reset backup offered-not-required; plugin
  `system_reset` hookspec deferred (no plugin currently needs
  it); endpoint pair under `/api/system/` namespace.

### Scope shipped (5 commits, `3c1381a..2cea204`)

**C2** `feat(system): POST /api/system/reset/prepare + POST /api/system/reset` — commit `3c1381a`
- `backend/app/services/reset_token.py`: per-process random
  32-byte secret signing tokens with 5-min TTL. Tokens cannot
  survive a server restart by design.
- `backend/app/services/reset_service.py`: `run_reset` cancels
  SSE jobs via new `JobStore.shutdown_all` → truncates all 21
  tables via `reversed(Base.metadata.sorted_tables)` (handles
  the `article_comments` SET-NULL → DELETE edge case via
  reverse-topo iteration) → re-seeds 5 book + 4 chapter
  built-in templates → wipes filesystem (uploads, tmp,
  backup_history, config overlays, installed plugins, secrets)
  → preserves production marker + migration breadcrumb +
  launcher state + project-tree licenses.
- `backend/app/routers/system.py`: extends the existing
  `/api/system/` namespace with `POST /reset/prepare`
  (returns `{token, expires_at, ttl_seconds}`) and `POST /reset`
  (requires `{token, confirmation: "RESET"}`).
- Tests (25 new): 8 token unit + 7 service integration + 7
  endpoint integration + 3 JobStore extension. Backend suite
  green: 2240 passed, 1 skipped.

**C4+C5** `feat(settings): Danger Zone section + 3-step reset dialog + post-reset cleanup` — commit `8b6a11b`
- `frontend/src/components/settings/DangerZoneSettings.tsx`:
  Radix Dialog with idle / typing / submitting state machine.
  Background prepare-call races user keystrokes so the
  destructive button is ready by the time the user finishes
  typing "RESET". Final-delete gated on
  `state === "typing" && token !== null && resetText === "RESET"`.
  Cancel + Escape blocked while submitting.
- Post-reset cleanup: `localStorage.clear()` +
  `sessionStorage.clear()` + Dexie `db.delete()` (drops
  `BibliogonDB`) + `navigate("/")` (Dashboard re-fires
  onboarding because the `bibliogon-onboarding` flag was just
  cleared).
- New tab `danger_zone` added to Settings.tsx as the last
  tab (after About). Mobile dropdown picks it up via the
  shared `tabDefs` SSoT.
- `api.system.resetPrepare` + `api.system.reset` added to the
  client.
- Vitest (9 cases): section render, dialog open + prepare
  call, warning + backup + RESET input rendered, button
  disabled on empty / lowercase, button enables on RESET,
  happy path through cleanup + navigate, backup button opens
  new tab, cancel closes dialog.

**C6** `feat(i18n): Danger Zone strings across 8 catalogs` — commit `bc363df`
- 1 tab key + 20 `ui.settings.danger_zone.*` keys.
- DE + EN native; ES, FR, EL, PT, TR, JA passthrough-EN per
  directive.
- i18n parity test green (51/51); the new passthrough keys
  show up in the heuristic-only "looks-like-untranslated-
  English" advisory output (expected, not a failure).

**C7** `test(e2e): Playwright smoke for Danger Zone reset flow` — commit `2cea204`
- 2 cases: full reset flow (open dialog → type RESET → execute
  → redirect → seeded book is gone) + cancel-does-not-reset.
- All testids `danger-zone-*` namespace positively asserted
  per the testid-namespace-pinning lessons-learned rule.

**C8** `docs: close DANGER-ZONE-RESET-EVERYTHING-01 + help pages` — this commit
- `docs/help/de/settings/danger-zone.md` + EN counterpart:
  full user-facing documentation covering when to use, what
  gets deleted, what stays, the three-click safety pattern,
  failure cases.
- `docs/help/_meta.yaml`: new Settings nav block (first
  Settings help-page in the doc tree).
- `docs/CHANGELOG.md`: Unreleased entry summarising the
  feature.

### What gets deleted (canonical reference — keep aligned with `reset_service.py` docstring + help pages)

- All 21 SQLite tables truncated, builtin templates re-seeded
- `<data_dir>/uploads/` (cover images + asset files), wiped + recreated empty
- `<data_dir>/tmp/` (Medium-import preview workspaces), wiped + recreated empty
- `<data_dir>/backup_history.json`
- `<data_dir>/config/app.yaml` (user-overlay)
- `<data_dir>/config/plugins/*.yaml` (per-plugin user-overlays)
- `<data_dir>/plugins/installed/*` (ZIP-installed plugins)
- `<config_dir>/secrets.yaml` (drops the AI API key)
- Browser: localStorage + sessionStorage cleared, Dexie
  `BibliogonDB` dropped (chapter drafts)
- In-memory JobStore cleared (running SSE jobs cancelled)

### What stays

- `.bibliogon-production` marker (test-isolation tripwire)
- `.migration-complete` marker (platformdirs migration breadcrumb)
- `<config_dir>/install.json` + `install.log` + `settings.json` (launcher-owned)
- `backend/config/licenses.json` (project-tree, licensing dormant)
- The app itself and the launcher install state
- The bundled built-in templates (re-seeded after truncation)

### Coexistence with /api/test/reset

The existing `/api/test/reset` (debug-only, used by e2e
tests for per-test clean state) was deliberately left
untouched. Two distinct surfaces with different security
contracts:

- `/api/test/reset` — DELETE method, debug-only (`BIBLIOGON_DEBUG=true`),
  covers 4 tables (Asset + Chapter + Book + Article), no
  HMAC, used by `e2e/fixtures/base.ts` auto-reset.
- `/api/system/reset` — POST method, production-available,
  HMAC-token + RESET-literal gated, covers all 21 tables
  + filesystem + browser storage.

---

## Archived 2026-05-23 (ACCESSIBILITY-AUDIT-WCAG-AA-01 CLOSED — 7-commit WCAG 2.1 AA audit shipped post-v0.36.0; user-adjudicated trigger override)

Filed in commit `59d55e3` during v0.36.0 release prep; trigger
("Pre-v1.0 release gate OR first accessibility complaint OR
legal-requirement event") explicitly overridden by user.
Shipped immediately post-v0.36.0 as 7 atomic commits.

### Scope shipped (7 commits, `457e01c..2349797`)

**C1** `a11y(C1): skip-to-content link + landmarks + heading hierarchy` — commit `457e01c`
- WCAG 2.1 SC 2.4.1 (Bypass Blocks) + SC 1.3.1.
- New `SkipToContentLink` component mounted at App root above
  OfflineBanner. `.skip-link` + `.sr-only` utilities added to
  global.css.
- `id="main-content"` added to every page's `<main>`: Dashboard,
  ArticleList, ArticleEditor, Settings, Help, GetStarted,
  MediumImportPage.
- BookEditor previously had ZERO `<main>` landmark — now wraps
  the chapter / metadata / loading / empty-state slot with a new
  `.content` flex-1 class in BookEditor.module.css preserving
  layout.
- BookEditor + ArticleEditor: visually-hidden `<h1>{title}</h1>`
  added so screen readers get top-level heading without visible
  layout change.
- `ui.a11y.skip_to_content` added to all 8 i18n catalogs.

**C2** `a11y(C2): keyboard focus indicator + KDP wizard step-change focus` — commit `0e3c852`
- WCAG 2.1 SC 2.4.7 (Focus Visible) + SC 2.1.1 (Keyboard).
- Audit found 17 `outline: none` sites without paired
  `:focus-visible` replacement.
- Universal `*:focus-visible` rule in global.css applies 2px
  accent outline + 2px offset on keyboard focus only.
  `!important` justified because per-component class rules win
  by specificity otherwise.
- KdpPublishingWizard now wires `stepContentRef` to
  `WizardShell.bodyRef` + useEffect-on-step-change mirroring
  the ConvertToBookWizard pattern (focus first interactive on
  step transition).

**C3** `a11y(C3): ARIA sweep` — commit `f4ec170`
- WCAG 2.1 SC 4.1.2 (Name, Role, Value) + SC 1.3.1.
- WizardShell step indicator: `aria-current="step"` on the
  current step dot. Previously N identical bullets.
- Toolbar (chapter editor) formatting buttons:
  `aria-pressed={btn.active}` on all 20+ toggle buttons
  (Bold / Italic / Underline / Strike / Code / Highlight / Sub /
  Sup / H1-3 / Align L/C/R/Justify / Bullets / Ordered / Tasks /
  Quote / Table / CodeBlock).
- RichTextToolbar already had aria-pressed (no work).
- Audit findings (no work needed): PageThumbnails Trash2 + grip
  + Add buttons all had aria-label; BulkActionBar had
  role="region" + aria-label; react-toastify provides
  role="alert" + aria-live="assertive" by default; HTML
  `required` not used (soft-validation pattern).

**C4** `a11y(C4): TipTap editor surface accessible name + explicit ARIA` — commit `5f201e5`
- WCAG 2.1 SC 4.1.2.
- Both Editor.tsx (chapter editor) and RichTextEditor.tsx
  (picture-book) now pass `aria-label` + `role="textbox"` +
  `aria-multiline="true"` via TipTap's
  `editorProps.attributes`. Previously screen readers
  announced just "edit text" with no name distinguishing the
  editor from any other contenteditable.
- `ui.a11y.editor_label` added to all 8 i18n catalogs.

**C5** `a11y(C5): WCAG AA color-contrast fixes across all 10 theme variants` — commit `aab984e`
- WCAG 2.1 SC 1.4.3 (Contrast Minimum) AA target.
- Audit script ran the 6 highest-risk fg/bg pairs across all
  5 theme palettes × light/dark = 10 variants. Found 30
  AA-Normal violations dominated by `--text-muted` (28 of 30)
  + 2 `--accent` failures. Worst case (cool-modern/dark) was
  1.93:1.
- 14 CSS edits. New values computed by walking the luminance
  gradient toward the variant's background-extreme until
  contrast ≥ 4.5:1 against the worst-case bg pair (which
  guarantees compliance against all bgs in that theme).
- User-adjudicated path α (fix all 30). Rationale:
  accessibility trumps "intentionally subdued" hierarchy when
  the result is below WCAG AA.
- Re-audit script confirms 0 remaining violations.

**C6** `a11y(C6): @axe-core/react integration (devDependency only)` — commit `475962b`
- WCAG 2.1 SC 4.1.1 + 4.1.2.
- `@axe-core/react ^4.11.3` added to devDependencies.
- Wired in `main.tsx` behind `import.meta.env.DEV` via
  dynamic import. Logs WCAG / Section 508 violations to
  browser DevTools console after every render (1000ms debounce).
- Production bundle verified clean (`grep -rl axe-core dist/`
  returns empty after `npm run build`).

**C7** `a11y(C7): prefers-reduced-motion universal rule` — commit `2349797`
- WCAG 2.1 SC 2.3.3 + WAI vestibular-disorder guidance.
- Audit baseline: 0 `prefers-reduced-motion` queries across
  the ~42 transition/animation declarations.
- Single universal rule added to global.css: when OS reports
  `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce`, all transitions and
  animations collapse to 0.01ms duration with single iteration.
  Preserves `transitionend` / `animationend` callbacks
  (Radix Dialog, ToastContainer, etc.).

### Pre-Inspection vs reality

Pre-Inspection findings AT START of session:
- Skip-to-content link: ZERO (gap) → fixed in C1
- `prefers-reduced-motion`: ZERO across all CSS (gap) → fixed in C7
- Landmark `<main>`: BookEditor had none (gap) → fixed in C1
- Heading hierarchy: BookEditor + ArticleEditor lacked h1 (gap) → fixed in C1
- 17 `outline: none` without focus-visible (gap) → fixed in C2
- 30 WCAG AA contrast violations (gap) → fixed in C5
- @axe-core/react: not integrated (gap) → fixed in C6
- Toolbar aria-pressed: missing on chapter editor (gap) → fixed in C3
- TipTap editor accessible name: missing (gap) → fixed in C4
- WizardShell aria-current="step": missing (gap) → fixed in C3

### What stayed as documented findings (not bugs)

- **react-toastify ToastContainer**: provides `role="alert"` +
  `aria-live="assertive"` by default. No work.
- **HTML `required` attribute**: not used; Bibliogon uses
  soft-validation pattern (notify.error on submit) instead.
  aria-required not applicable.
- **PageThumbnails @dnd-kit keyboard reorder**: already wired
  via `KeyboardSensor` + `sortableKeyboardCoordinates`. Also
  verified on ChapterSidebar, OrderedListEditor, KeywordInput.
- **Radix UI primitives** (Dialog, Tabs, Select, Dropdown,
  Tooltip): provide good baseline accessibility per design.
  No custom wrapper introduced new violations.
- **Color contrast deltas from C5**: `text-muted` is now
  visually more present in subdued contexts (timestamps,
  helper text, captions). Intentional per user adjudication
  — accessibility over aesthetic subtlety.

### Stop-conditions encountered

1. **C5 path adjudication required** (per the prompt's "Theme
   contrast fixes cascade into visual regressions" stop-
   condition). Surfaced to user with 3 paths (α full fix /
   β AA-Large only / γ defer all). User chose α.

No other stop-conditions fired. Editor accessibility (C4) did
not require ProseMirror patches. axe-core integration (C6)
did not surface > 20 critical violations because C1-C5 already
addressed the known categories. Color contrast fixes (C5) did
not cascade into visual regressions beyond the deliberate
text-muted change.

### Test deltas

- Vitest: 1986 / 1986 throughout (no test added or removed
  across the 7 commits).
- tsc --noEmit: clean throughout.
- i18n parity: 75 / 75 throughout (2 new keys added with all
  8 catalogs in lockstep — `ui.a11y.skip_to_content` + `ui.a11y.editor_label`).
- Production build: green; axe-core not in shipped bundle.

### Cross-references

- Source pattern: adaptive-learner accessibility audit
  (7-commit structure).
- Radix UI accessibility baseline preserved (audit focused
  on custom wrappers).
- `.claude/rules/coding-standards.md` testid conventions
  support the audit infrastructure.

### No follow-up filed

Closure self-contained. axe-core console output will surface
incidental findings as developers encounter them in dev
sessions; those become individual backlog items if substantial.
The deferred sub-parts (PDF tagged-PDF accessibility, WCAG AAA)
were explicitly out of scope for this audit and remain so.

## Archived 2026-05-23 (I18N-ARTICLES-NAMESPACE-CLEANUP-01 CLOSED — 7 silently-falling-back keys moved to ui.articles + 3 dead keys deleted + orphaned AuthorProfileSelect component+test removed)

Originally filed in the 2026-05-22 handover's "Unfiled Surfaces"
section as a 2-key scope (move `author_none` + `author_pen_names`
from `ui.template_picker.*` to `ui.articles.*`). Pre-Coding-
Reality-Check at session start surfaced that the actual scope
is 10× larger AND the 2 originally-flagged keys are now dead
post-AUTHOR-DATALIST migration. User adjudicated full-scope
path β (move live keys, delete dead keys, delete the orphaned
component).

### Scope shipped

**C1** (this session): all changes in one commit.

7 live silently-falling-back keys moved from `ui.template_picker.*`
to `ui.articles.*` across all 8 i18n catalogs (de/en/es/fr/el/pt/
tr/ja):

- `back_to_list_tooltip` (ArticleEditor)
- `back_to_dashboard` (ArticleEditor + ArticleList)
- `back_to_dashboard_tooltip` (ArticleEditor + ArticleList)
- `canonical_url` (ArticleEditor)
- `excerpt` (ArticleEditor)
- `tags_label` (ArticleEditor)
- `all_saved` (ArticleEditor)

Every one of these consumers had been calling `ui.articles.X`
since at least the AR-01 era and silently falling back to the
hardcoded German fallback string in the React `t(key, fallback)`
call. Bug class: i18n parity passes (because the key existed
SOMEWHERE in the catalog), but the consumer's namespace path
didn't match the actual location. Non-DE users saw German.

3 dead keys deleted from `ui.template_picker.*`:

- `featured_image_url` (no consumer; ArticleEditor uses
  `featured_image_url_label` + `featured_image_url_tooltip`
  which DO live correctly under `ui.articles`)
- `author_none` (orphan after AUTHOR-DATALIST migration)
- `author_pen_names` (orphan after AUTHOR-DATALIST migration)

`ui.template_picker.delete_failed` retained: CreateBookModal
legitimately consumes it for template-delete failures.

Orphaned `AuthorProfileSelect` component + test deleted:

- `frontend/src/components/AuthorProfileSelect.tsx` (164 LOC)
- `frontend/src/components/AuthorProfileSelect.test.tsx` (~270 LOC,
  12 tests)

Both consumers (ArticleEditor + BookMetadataEditor) migrated to
`AuthorSelectInput` (Pattern A) in the 2026-05-22 AUTHOR-DATALIST
batch; only the component's own test file imported it after that
migration. Removing the component closes the orphan.

Doc-comment cleanup at 3 sites that mentioned the deleted symbol
by name (BookMetadataEditor, ArticleEditor, BookMetadataEditor
test). Kept the WHY content (Pattern A rationale, no-auto-DB-create
invariant) but dropped the historical-ID + deleted-symbol-name
references per the "Don't reference the current task ... rots as
the codebase evolves" rule.

### Pre-Coding-Reality-Check finding

The handoff described the surface as 2 keys. The keystroke-time
grep revealed:

- The 2 originally-flagged keys (`author_none` + `author_pen_names`)
  have ZERO consumers — moving them would create dead keys in the
  correct namespace instead of dead keys in the wrong namespace.
  Net functional change: zero.
- 7 OTHER keys under the same misplaced block ARE consumed and
  silently falling back.
- The component associated with the dead keys is also orphaned.

Per the "Pre-Coding-Reality-Check: re-audit at the keystroke, not
just the audit" lessons-learned rule, the original spec was
revised with user approval before any code change shipped.

### Test deltas

- Backend pytest: 2213 → 2214 (+1, unrelated; i18n parity 75/75
  still green)
- Frontend Vitest: 1998 → 1986 (−12, AuthorProfileSelect.test.tsx
  deleted as orphan)
- i18n parity: 75/75 passing (key count parity preserved across
  all 8 catalogs because both ADD and DELETE applied to all 8)
- tsc --noEmit: clean

### No follow-up filed

Closure self-contained. The deleted component had no other
consumers; the cleaned doc comments preserve the design rationale
(Pattern A vs Pattern B, no-auto-DB-create) without the rot-prone
historical-ID references.
