## Archived 2026-05-23 (HOOKSPEC-EXPORT-EXECUTE-WIRE-01 CLOSED — comic-book PDF dispatch wired via export_execute, audiobook retained as documented exception)

User-adjudicated path γ (narrowest scope) after Pre-Inspection
surfaced that the planned full-scope wiring would force
audiobook's async/streaming dispatch through a sync `Path | None`
hookspec signature — a half-wired feature-ship shape the lessons-
learned rules explicitly forbid.

### Scope shipped

**C1**: plugin-comics now registers `@hookimpl export_execute`
gated on `book_type == "comic_book"` + `fmt == "pdf"`. plugin-
export's `_export_comic_book_pdf` calls
`manager.call_hook("export_execute", firstresult=True, ...)`
instead of the prior lazy `from bibliogon_comics.comic_book_pdf
import ...` at line 365. The one cross-plugin reverse-import in
plugin-export's routes.py is gone.

Tests: 6 hookimpl-contract pins in plugin-comics's
`test_plugin_smoke.py` (None-return gates on wrong book_type /
prose / missing book_type / wrong fmt); 1 integration regression
pin in `backend/tests/test_comic_routes.py` that spies on
`manager.call_hook` to assert exactly-one `export_execute`
dispatch per `/export/pdf` request, with `book_type=="comic_book"`
+ `fmt=="pdf"` + all four comic data slots (pages/panels/bubbles/
output_path) wired into options.

**C2**: hookspec docstring updated to mark `export_execute` as
WIRED + document the audiobook exception with concrete
rationale (async, SSE streaming, sync signature mismatch).
CLAUDE.md plugin-table notes refreshed: plugin-comics note now
mentions the hook wiring; plugin-audiobook note re-framed as a
"documented exception" rather than an undescribed coupling.

### What stayed unchanged (and why)

Per the user-adjudicated γ scope:

- **Audiobook dispatch** in plugin-export's `_run_audiobook_job`
  (routes.py:1100-1102, 1185): genuinely async + emits SSE
  events via `job_store.publish_event` + returns a job-result
  dict, not a Path. Wiring through the sync hookspec would force
  marshalling state through globals.
- **The 3 utility imports** (lines 714, 732, 1185): import
  `normalize_merge_mode`, `_slugify`, `extract_plain_text`,
  `should_regenerate` — these are helpers, not format
  dispatchers, and a hookspec is the wrong shape for them.
- **The pre-dispatch existence check** at line 1026: imports
  `audiobook_storage.load_metadata` to compose the HTTP-409
  audiobook-exists confirm payload. Runs BEFORE any format
  dispatch.
- **plugin-comics → plugin-export forward import** of
  `picture_book_pdf` + `picture_book_fonts`: legitimate per
  `plugin-comics depends_on = ["export"]`; NOT a coupling to
  remove. The backlog item listed it incorrectly; the
  Pre-Inspection caught the mis-classification.

### No follow-up filed

Per the adjudication: "Do NOT file a follow-up for hookspec
signature redesign (premature without a concrete async consumer
need)". Re-evaluate if a SECOND async streaming-export plugin
proposes to register; that would justify a separate
`export_execute_async` hookspec.

### Cross-references

- C1 commit: see git log for `fix(plugins): wire export_execute hook`
- C2 commit: see git log for `docs(hookspec): close HOOKSPEC-EXPORT-EXECUTE-WIRE-01`
- Pre-Inspection rationale documented in chat session 2026-05-23
- Audit precedent: `HOOKSPEC-DISPATCH-WIRING-01` (closed 2026-05-22)
  where `chapter_pre_save` was deleted for the same "no clean
  wiring path" pattern; `export_execute` survives because γ
  produced a real wiring.

## Archived 2026-05-22 (AUTHOR-DATALIST-EXTEND-EDITORS-01 + AUTHOR-SELECT-INPUT-EXTRACT-01 CLOSED — Pattern A migration of all 4 author-input surfaces complete)

User pre-adjudicated Pattern A (free-text input + datalist
autocomplete) across all 4 author-input surfaces. Both backlog
items close together per the original coordinated-session shape
filed 2026-05-19.

### Coordination context

`AUTHOR-SELECT-INPUT-EXTRACT-01` was the parent extraction
filing; the canonical `AuthorSelectInput` component shipped
earlier (visible in `frontend/src/components/AuthorSelectInput.tsx`
header: "RECURRING-COMPONENT-AUDIT-01 Candidate #4 extraction")
when CreateBookModal + ConvertToBookWizard migrated. With today's
BookMetadataEditor + ArticleEditor migration, all 4 author-input
surfaces ride the unified Pattern A shape and both items can be
closed.

The original filing's "BookEditor backpage author-bio sidebar"
surface DOES NOT need migration: `backpage_author_bio` is a
free-text bio textarea, not an author-name picker. Verified
during Pre-Inspection.

### Pre-Inspection

```
AuthorSelectInput consumers:    CreateBookModal + ConvertToBookWizard
                                (shipped earlier)
AuthorProfileSelect consumers:  BookMetadataEditor + ArticleEditor
                                (today's migration targets)
backpage_author_bio:            <textarea>, not an author picker
                                (NOT in scope)
```

No fifth surface surfaced in the codebase grep — the extraction
audit was complete already.

### Asymmetric design decision (documented at consumer sites)

**BookMetadataEditor** uses the FULL Pattern A: input + datalist
+ "Add to Authors-DB" checkbox + create-on-save handler.
Rationale: there's an explicit Save button, so the
`api.authors.create` call fires at handleSave time before the
book PATCH (mirrors CreateBookModal's pattern).

**ArticleEditor** uses ONLY the input + datalist; the
Add-to-DB checkbox is DELIBERATELY SUPPRESSED. Rationale:
the Article editor auto-saves on every keystroke (`persistMeta`
fires from each onChange). An auto-DB-create on every keystroke
would create partial-name rows ("Joh", "John D", "John Doe"
as the user types). Curate via Settings > Author tab.

A future need for article-side auto-add could be addressed by
adding an `onBlur` callback to `AuthorSelectInput` and gating
the create on input-blur. Not in scope today.

### Shipped (commits `62b2a9c` + `109b1ab`)

**C1 `62b2a9c`** — Component migration (4 files, +245 / -107):
- `BookMetadataEditor.tsx`: AuthorProfileSelect →
  AuthorSelectInput swap; new useEffect fetching
  `api.authors.list({})` into globalAuthors; new useMemo for
  authorSuggestions (profileDisplayNames + globalAuthors,
  deduped); new useMemo for showAddToAuthorsCheckbox; new
  addAuthorToDb state; handleSave wraps `api.authors.create`
  before the book PATCH. Removed unused `useAllowBooksWithoutAuthor`
  + `AuthorProfile` type imports.
- `BookMetadataEditor.test.tsx`: 5 author-field tests
  rewritten for Pattern A (renders-as-input vs renders-as-
  select; datalist-exposes-suggestions vs dropdown-lists-
  options; unknown-value-as-free-text vs disabled-fallback-
  option). New `authors: {list, create}` mock entry.
- `ArticleEditor.tsx`: AuthorProfileSelect → AuthorSelectInput
  swap; globalAuthors fetch + authorSuggestions useMemo; pass
  `showAddToAuthorsCheckbox={false}` per the auto-save
  rationale.
- `ArticleEditor.test.tsx`: api/client mock gained
  `authors: {list, create}` entries.

**C2 `109b1ab`** — i18n + Playwright smoke (9 files, +166 / -8):
- 3 new i18n keys × 8 catalogs = 24 entries
  (`ui.metadata.add_to_authors_db`, `ui.metadata.author_add_failed`,
  `ui.articles.author_placeholder`).
- `ui.metadata.author_placeholder` updated from "Select an
  author" → "Author name or pen name" semantics in all 8
  catalogs.
- New `e2e/smoke/editor-author-datalist.spec.ts` (2 cases:
  BookMetadataEditor full-flow with author-create-on-save +
  ArticleEditor input-renders-as-input + checkbox-absent
  pin).

### Legacy bug surfaced (out-of-scope)

While adding `ui.articles.author_placeholder` it surfaced that
the existing `ui.articles.author_none` + `ui.articles.author_pen_names`
keys live in the WRONG namespace
(`ui.template_picker.*`) across all 8 catalogs.
ArticleEditor's existing `t("ui.articles.author_none", ...)`
calls have always fallen back to the hardcoded German string
because of this misnamespacing. Out-of-scope cleanup; filed as
`I18N-ARTICLES-NAMESPACE-CLEANUP-01` (P3) on the next
session-prep pass — not filed in THIS commit per scope
discipline.

### Verification at close

- Type-check clean (`npx tsc --noEmit`).
- Vitest 1998 → 1998 (test counts stay equal — rewritten
  tests pin the new contract, not added new ones).
- i18n parity: 8/8 catalogs cover all 3 new keys.
- Playwright `--list`: spec parses, 2 tests detected.
- Pre-commit: all hooks green.

### Commits

- C1 `62b2a9c` — `feat(editors): migrate Book + Article author
  field to Pattern A (Datalist)`

  in 8 catalogs + Playwright smoke`

## Archived 2026-05-22 (HOOKSPEC-DISPATCH-WIRING-01 CLOSED — 3 dispositions adjudicated: status-quo / wire-via-follow-up / delete)

HOOKSPEC-DISPATCH-WIRING-01 was filed 2026-05-23 from the
plugin-communication investigation. The plugin manager declared
3 hookspecs (`export_formats`, `export_execute`,
`chapter_pre_save`) without dispatch sites; only
`content_pre_import` was actually wired. The audit asked which
of three dispositions to take per hook: wire-up, delete, or
status-quo.

Closed 2026-05-22 via single-commit audit + adjudication +
implementation, drain-ungated session.

### Audit findings

Zero plugin implementations existed for any of the three
unwired hooks — pure intended-architecture, not dead-code
attached to nothing. The hookspecs.py docstring claim was
accurate.

### Per-hook adjudication

| Hook | Disposition | Rationale |
|---|---|---|
| `export_formats` | **Status quo** | plugin-export owns the hardcoded `SUPPORTED_FORMATS = {"epub", "pdf", "docx", "html", "markdown", "project", "audiobook"}` set; it's the single export-plugin today. Wiring would require splitting the format catalog across plugins, useful when a 2nd export plugin lands. Re-evaluate on first 2nd-export-plugin proposal. |
| `export_execute` | **Wire via follow-up** | Eliminates 6 cross-plugin direct-import sites in `plugin-export/routes.py` (audiobook dispatch) + 1 site in `plugin-comics/comic_book_pdf.py` (picture_book_pdf reuse). Real technical debt + documented reverse-coupling anti-pattern. Cleanup is its own 3-5-commit session — filed as `HOOKSPEC-EXPORT-EXECUTE-WIRE-01` (P3). |
| `chapter_pre_save` | **Delete** | Zero implementations after multiple release cycles. Sibling `content_pre_import` covers the import-side use case (only one with a real plugin consumer); edit-time pre-save transformation is a fundamentally different UX trade-off (silently mutating user content on save can surprise authors). Re-file with a concrete use case + named consumer if pre-save transformation ever becomes a real need. |

### Shipped (single commit)

`backend/app/hookspecs.py`:
- Removed `chapter_pre_save` hookspec declaration entirely.
- Updated module docstring + per-hook docstrings to reflect
  the new state (status-quo note for `export_formats`; wire-
  up-planned-as-follow-up note for `export_execute`; deletion
  note in the module docstring for `chapter_pre_save`).

`docs/backlog.md`:
- Removed HOOKSPEC-DISPATCH-WIRING-01 entry.
- Added HOOKSPEC-EXPORT-EXECUTE-WIRE-01 (P3) entry with
  scope, trigger, cross-references to the 6+1 direct-import
  sites.

### Verification at close

- 3 hooks remain on `BibliogonHookSpec` (verified via
  introspection): `content_pre_import` (wired),
  `export_execute` (declared, wire-up planned), `export_formats`
  (declared, status-quo).
- Smoke pytest on test_book_type_registry +
  test_plugin_version_gating: 25/25 green (no cross-impact).

### Commits

- C1 (combined) — `refactor(hookspec): delete chapter_pre_save
  + file export_execute cleanup + close
  HOOKSPEC-DISPATCH-WIRING-01`.

### Cross-references

- CLAUDE.md plugin table note about plugin-export ↔ plugin-
  audiobook reverse-coupling — the note stays accurate until
  HOOKSPEC-EXPORT-EXECUTE-WIRE-01 ships.
- `.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md` "Half-wired feature
  lifecycle" — `chapter_pre_save` is a textbook example of
  intended-architecture-without-consumer that the rule warns
  against; deletion is the right outcome.

## Archived 2026-05-22 (KDP-CATEGORIES-WIRE-TO-CATEGORYINPUT-01 CLOSED — 26-entry KDP catalog now feeds CategoryInput autocomplete)

KDP-CATEGORIES-WIRE-TO-CATEGORYINPUT-01 was filed 2026-05-18 by
the KDP-CATEGORIES-CATALOG-SYNC-01 work as the legitimate
wire-up implied by a dead JSDoc reference. The original entry's
explicit trigger ("user requests autocomplete" / "Picture-Book
feedback" / "RECURRING-COMPONENT-AUDIT-01 flag") had not fired,
but the 2026-05-22 drain-ungated session classified this as
Half-Wired-Visible-in-Production per the Foundation-Override
extension: backend endpoint live, frontend prop accepted
suggestions, but the surface passed `[]` — every BookMetadataEditor
render showed a Categories field with no autocomplete despite the
26-entry Amazon-canonical catalog being available.

### Pre-Inspection findings

- Backend endpoint `GET /api/kdp/categories` (plugin-kdp routes.py
  line 142-145) returns `list(KDP_CATEGORIES)` — 26 strings.
  Pinned by `test_kdp_categories_returns_full_26_catalog`.
- Frontend `CategoryInput` (line 35) already accepts
  `suggestions?: string[] = []`, renders a `<datalist>` when
  `suggestions.length > 0` (line 144-145), and wires the input
  to it via `list={...}` (line 124).
- BookMetadataEditor line 441 was constructing CategoryInput with
  no `suggestions` prop — falling through to the empty default.
- No existing useEffect-based fetch on KDP endpoints elsewhere in
  the editor; voices is the canonical fetch-on-mount pattern.

### Shipped (commit `9c2c302`)

`frontend/src/api/client.ts`:
- New `api.kdp.listCategories()` method —
  `request<string[]>("/kdp/categories")`. JSDoc explains the
  fetch-once-cache-for-lifetime semantics (catalog is stable
  across the editor's lifetime).

`frontend/src/components/BookMetadataEditor.tsx`:
- New `kdpCategoriesCatalog` state.
- One-shot `useEffect` on mount fires `api.kdp.listCategories()`
  with a `cancelled` guard against unmount races. Failure path
  silently degrades to empty list (CategoryInput is
  free-text-capable; missing catalog → plain typing, not a
  crash).
- `<CategoryInput suggestions={kdpCategoriesCatalog} />`.

`frontend/src/components/BookMetadataEditor.test.tsx`:
- Added `kdp.listCategories: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue([])` to
  the `vi.mock("../api/client", ...)` block as the safe default
  for all 64 existing tests.
- 2 new regression-pin cases inside the existing Bug-9 describe
  block:
  - `on mount, calls api.kdp.listCategories and the datalist
    exposes its options` — asserts the fetch fires exactly once
    AND the rendered `<datalist>` options contain the mocked
    catalog values (Fiction, Mystery, Science Fiction).
  - `when api.kdp.listCategories fails, CategoryInput degrades
    to no suggestions (no crash)` — asserts the Marketing tab
    still renders cleanly under fetch rejection.

### Verification at close

- Vitest 1996 → 1998 (+2; the BookMetadataEditor suite went
  64 → 66).
- Type-check clean (`npx tsc --noEmit`).
- Pre-commit: all hooks green.

### What's still latent (deliberate)

- Catalog refresh-on-version-bump is not in scope — the catalog
  is stable enough that an editor-mount fetch is sufficient. If
  Amazon ever expands the catalog, a backend redeploy + browser
  refresh propagates it on the next mount.
- No client-side caching across editor mounts. The catalog fetch
  is small (~26 strings ≈ a few hundred bytes) and surfaces once
  per BookMetadataEditor open; pre-caching across mounts via
  context or query-cache is a P5-tier optimization not justified
  by the current cost profile.

### Filings

None. The wire-up was self-contained.

### Commits

- C1 `9c2c302` — `feat(metadata): wire CategoryInput suggestions
  to KDP 26-entry catalog` (api method + one-shot fetch +
  CategoryInput prop + 2 regression pins).
- C2 (this commit) — backlog close + archive.

### Cross-references

- KDP-CATEGORIES-CATALOG-SYNC-01 (closed 2026-05-18) was the
  parent filing that surfaced this gap as a follow-up.
- Foundation-Override extension lessons-learned rule
  "Half-Wired-Visible-in-Production triggers P1" — the
  classification basis for treating this as ungated.

---

## Archived 2026-05-22 (PLUGIN-VERSION-GATING-ENABLE-01 CLOSED — min_app_version now enforced)

PLUGIN-VERSION-GATING-ENABLE-01 was filed 2026-05-20 during V060
C3 β2 migration. Class-attribute declarations on ComicsPlugin
(`min_app_version = "0.35.0"`) and KinderbuchPlugin
(`min_app_version = "0.9.0"`) shipped as documented intent but
were never actually enforced — pluginforge's
`_check_app_version` silently short-circuits when the manager's
`app_version` is None.

Soft-trigger interpretation: both existing dormant declarations
already qualify as "real version requirements" per the backlog's
trigger criterion (i). Closed under the drain-ungated-pool
session 2026-05-22.

### Shipped (commit `b351e73`)

`backend/app/main.py`:
- Added `app_version=__version__` kwarg to the PluginManager
  ctor at line 310. One-line wiring of the existing dormant
  pluginforge feature.

### Verification at close

- Live runtime check: TestClient lifespan boots cleanly; all
  12 plugins activate; comics + kinderbuch pass their declared
  gates at host version 0.35.1.
- `manager.inspect_plugin(name).state.filter_reason` exposes
  `"incompatible_app_version"` for synthetic plugins declaring
  `min_app_version > host_version`.
- `manager.get_load_errors()[name]` carries the human-readable
  rejection message ("Plugin 'X' requires app version >= Y,
  host is Z").

### Tests (new `backend/tests/test_plugin_version_gating.py`)

3 cases:
1. **test_plugin_with_future_min_app_version_is_filtered** —
   synthetic plugin with `min_app_version="99.0.0"` registers
   but is rejected. Asserts filter_reason, load_error message
   content, and exclusion from active set.
2. **test_plugin_with_compatible_min_app_version_activates** —
   positive counterpart with `min_app_version="0.0.1"`. Gate
   doesn't reject low-floor plugins.
3. **test_real_plugins_pass_their_declared_min_app_version** —
   release-time regression catch. Pins
   `host >= comics_min_app_version` AND
   `host >= kinderbuch_min_app_version`. If a future host bump
   drops below either floor, this fails before tag.

Backend pytest 2210 → 2213 (+3).

### Operator impact

This is a behavior change visible to operators: a future plugin
declaring `min_app_version > host_version` will now be filtered
out at activation with a load-error message. Release-workflow
implication: at each Bibliogon version bump, the
`test_real_plugins_pass_their_declared_min_app_version` test
gates the release — surfaces any min_app_version declaration
that exceeds the new host floor before tag.

Severity defaults to `"error"` per pluginforge Decision #4
(refuse activation, not warn). Configurable via
`app_version_severity` ctor kwarg if a future need arises for
warn-only behavior.

### Filings

None. The work was self-contained.

### Commits

- C1 `b351e73` — `feat(plugin-manager): enable min_app_version
  gating via pluginforge ctor kwarg` (ctor + 3 regression tests).
- C2 (this commit) — backlog close + archive.

### Cross-references

- pluginforge 0.6.0+ supports the `app_version` ctor kwarg.
- `_check_app_version` source at pluginforge/manager.py.
- Pluginforge Decision #4 (default `app_version_severity="error"`).

## Archived 2026-05-22 (PLUGIN-EXPORT-SINGLE-ROUTER-REFACTOR-01 CLOSED — single parent router nesting 3 sub-routers)

PLUGIN-EXPORT-SINGLE-ROUTER-REFACTOR-01 was filed 2026-05-20
from the pluginforge 0.8.0 bump's DeprecationWarning. plugin-
export's `get_routes()` returned 3 separate routers (per-book
export, bulk export, jobs polling), and pluginforge 0.8.0 logged
on every plugin manager mount:

    Plugin 'export' returns 3 routers from get_routes(). The
    recommended convention is one parent router that uses
    router.include_router(...) to nest sub-routers.

Trigger (iii) fired this session: "the deprecation warning
becomes noisy enough to mask other test output". The warning
appeared 4+ times across the day's pytest output, contributing
to log noise around the 47-warning baseline.

### Pre-Coding-Reality-Check

- Three routers in `routes.py`:
  - `router` at `/books/{book_id}/export` (per-book exports +
    async + batch + validate)
  - `bulk_router` at `/books/bulk-export` (multi-book bulk
    export)
  - `jobs_router` at `/export/jobs` (async job polling + SSE
    + download)
- No tests asserted on the 3-router return shape from
  `get_routes()`.
- Canonical pattern from plugin-comics: parent router with NO
  prefix and `tags=` set, sub-routers nested via
  `include_router()` keeping their own prefixes.
- Renaming the existing `router` symbol would touch every
  `@router.get(...)` decorator in routes.py (50+ sites).
  Adding a NEW `parent_router` at the bottom of routes.py
  that nests the three existing routers is the minimal-diff
  shape; zero decorator changes.

### Shipped (commit `c137d93`)

`routes.py` — new at end of file:

```python
parent_router = APIRouter(tags=["export"])
parent_router.include_router(router)
parent_router.include_router(bulk_router)
parent_router.include_router(jobs_router)
```

`plugin.py` — `get_routes()` now imports + returns
`[parent_router]` instead of the 3-router list.

### Verification at close

- Plugin pytest: 265/265 green.
- Backend pytest: 2210/2210 + 1 skipped green.
- Warning count: **48 → 47** (the multi-router
  DeprecationWarning is gone; remaining warnings are unrelated
  httpx / asyncio / etc.).
- API-surface verified unchanged via TestClient route
  enumeration: all 8 export endpoints resolve at their expected
  prefixes:
  - `/api/books/{book_id}/export/{fmt}`
  - `/api/books/{book_id}/export/async/{fmt}`
  - `/api/books/{book_id}/export/batch`
  - `/api/books/{book_id}/export/validate-epub`
  - `/api/books/bulk-export`
  - `/api/export/jobs/{job_id}`
  - `/api/export/jobs/{job_id}/stream`
  - `/api/export/jobs/{job_id}/download`

No client-facing change; the refactor is plugin-manifest-only.

### Architecture impact

plugin-export is now the third plugin (after kinderbuch +
comics) to ride the canonical Single-Router-Per-Plugin shape.
The pluginforge 0.10.0-may-become-error guidance is now
honored for every Bibliogon plugin with a router contract.

### Commits

- C1 `c137d93` — `refactor(plugin-export): single-router
  get_routes per pluginforge 0.8.0 convention` (parent_router
  + plugin.py get_routes update).
- C2 (this commit) — backlog close + archive.

### Cross-references

- `.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md` "Single-Router-Per-Plugin
  convention" (the rule this filing's work concretely closes).
- pluginforge 0.8.0 release notes (the deprecation source).

## Archived 2026-05-22 (PLUGIN-COMICS-MAKEFILE-INTEGRATION-01 CLOSED — comics + medium-import + git-sync Makefile targets wired)

PLUGIN-COMICS-MAKEFILE-INTEGRATION-01 was filed 2026-05-18 from
the plugin-comics Session 1 retrospective. plugin-comics shipped
with package + path-dep + CI matrix + i18n in place, but the
repo-root Makefile was NOT updated — the developer-facing test
surface was half-shipped (CI's per-plugin matrix ran comics; the
per-developer `make test-plugins` did not). Half-Wired-Feature-
Lifecycle Prevention rule applied.

### Pre-Inspection scope-expansion

The filing's "Strategic note — broader pattern discovery" surfaced
two sibling drifts in the SAME Makefile that predated the
plugin-comics ship:

- **medium-import**: NO Makefile targets at all. Landed when
  medium-import shipped in v0.31.0+.
- **git-sync**: `test-plugin-git-sync` existed but
  `test-coverage-plugin-git-sync` did NOT, and it was absent
  from the `test-coverage-plugins` aggregate.

The backlog item explicitly invited closing all three together:
"If a P3 hygiene sweep wants to close ALL Makefile-integration
gaps at once, extend the scope of this filing or open a sibling
`PLUGIN-MAKEFILE-INTEGRATION-AUDIT-01`". Close-all-known-
instances of the Half-Wired pattern was the right move per the
discipline; sibling never filed.

### Shipped (C1, commit `1c35997`)

`Makefile` updates:
- New per-plugin targets: `test-plugin-comics`,
  `test-plugin-medium-import` (mirror the canonical kinderbuch
  pattern: `cd` into plugin dir + `poetry env use python3.12
  -q 2>/dev/null; poetry run pytest tests/ -v`).
- New coverage targets: `test-coverage-plugin-comics`,
  `test-coverage-plugin-medium-import`,
  `test-coverage-plugin-git-sync` (mirror the kinderbuch
  coverage pattern with `--cov=<package>` + `--cov-report=html`
  + `--cov-report=term`).
- Aggregate `test-plugins` now lists all 12 plugins (was 10).
- Aggregate `test-coverage-plugins` now lists all 12 plugins
  (was 9).
- `.PHONY` header at lines 4 + 6 lists the new targets so
  parallel `-j` runs include them.

### Verified at close

- `make test-plugins` exits 0; all 12 plugin suites fire
  (comics shows 15 tests; medium-import shows 97).
- `make -n test-coverage-plugin-{comics,medium-import,git-sync}`
  each resolves to the correct per-plugin shell command.
- Pre-commit: all hooks green.

### Pre-Inspection-Checklist (canonical)

The backlog item proposed a Pre-Inspection-Checklist for future
plugin-shipping sessions; the entries that this filing actively
closes are now no longer ❌ MISSED:

- ✓ `backend/pyproject.toml` path-dep
- ✓ `backend/config/app.yaml.example` enable-list
- ✓ `backend/config/plugins/<name>.yaml` defaults
- ✓ `.github/workflows/ci.yml` plugin-matrix entry
- ✓ `.github/workflows/coverage.yml` plugin-matrix entry
- ✓ `Makefile`'s `test-plugins` aggregate (CLOSED 2026-05-22)
- ✓ `Makefile`'s `test-coverage-plugins` aggregate
  (CLOSED 2026-05-22)
- ✓ `Makefile` per-plugin `test-plugin-<name>` target
  (CLOSED 2026-05-22)
- ✓ `Makefile` per-plugin `test-coverage-plugin-<name>` target
  (CLOSED 2026-05-22)
- ✓ i18n catalog entries × 8
- ✓ At least one TestClient-tier integration test
- ✓ User-overlay enabled-list contains the new plugin (closed
  by USER-OVERLAY-PLUGIN-ENABLE-MIGRATION-01)

Future plugin-shipping Pre-Inspections should walk this
checklist explicitly at session-start time, not just at
retrospective time. The promotion of the checklist into
`.claude/rules/ai-workflow.md` is left as an optional
follow-up; the artifact lives in this archive entry and the
backlog item's history as a reference.

## Archived 2026-05-22 (CONVERT-TO-BOOK-WIZARD-LAYOUT-STABILITY-01 CLOSED — action button to WizardNav footer slot + min/max stepContent dimensions)

CONVERT-TO-BOOK-WIZARD-LAYOUT-STABILITY-01 was filed
2026-05-18 from real-user-smoke during the article-to-book
conversion workflow. Two distinct layout-instability bugs broke
user muscle-memory and visual continuity across the wizard's 6
steps. Closed in the 2026-05-22 session.

### Pre-Coding-Reality-Check findings

- **Bug #2** (action-button position shift): confirmed. The
  "Buch erstellen" / "Create Book" button lived inside
  `renderStepReview`'s `stepContent` body
  (`ConvertToBookWizard.tsx:1108-1125`), while every other
  step's Next button was rendered in the WizardNav footer slot.
  User mouse / Tab muscle-memory targeting the footer missed on
  step 5 — the button sat 280+ pixels above the expected slot.
- **Bug #1** (dialog jumping): partially mitigated by the
  earlier 2026-05-22 WizardShell migration (commit `a94e0b9`)
  which capped the WHOLE dialog at `maxHeight: 90vh`. Remaining
  variability came from `stepContent` itself (`minHeight: 280`
  with no `maxHeight`) which still grew with content amount on
  selection / review steps. Audit picked 380 / 520 as the
  natural-fit band.
- **WizardNav already had** `onFinish` / `isLastStep` /
  `finishLabel` / `finishIcon` props designed for exactly this
  use case (the KDP wizard uses them). Migration is a clean
  move-button-into-WizardNav-slot; no shell changes needed.

### Shipped (C1, commit `9fb224b`)

**Bug #2 fix** in `ConvertToBookWizard.tsx`:
- Removed the inline "Buch erstellen" button from
  `renderStepReview`'s stepContent body (lines 1108-1125).
- Threaded the button through WizardNav.onFinish with
  `isLastStep={step === TOTAL_STEPS - 1}`, dynamic
  `finishLabel` (handles submitting state), and
  `finishIcon={submitting ? undefined : <Check size={14}/>}`.
- New testid: `convert-to-book-wizard-step-5-finish` (in
  the WizardNav-namespace footer slot). Old testid
  `convert-to-book-wizard-review-confirm` is gone.

**Bug #1 fix** in `ConvertToBookWizard.tsx`:
- `stepContent` style updated to `minHeight: 380, maxHeight:
  520, overflowY: "auto"`. The Dialog itself already capped at
  90vh + scroll via WizardShell; this additional constraint
  pins the BODY area so the dialog dimensions visually stay
  stable across all 6 steps. Selection-list and review (the
  natural-largest steps) get internal scroll above 520px
  without affecting dialog dimensions.

**Test impact**:
- Vitest: 8 references in
  `ConvertToBookWizard.test.tsx` migrated from
  `convert-to-book-wizard-review-confirm` to
  `convert-to-book-wizard-step-5-finish` (30 → 30 tests still
  green).
- Vitest +2 new regression-pin cases in a dedicated
  `layout-stability regression-pins` describe block:
  - Bug #2: assert step-5-finish exists; assert old
    review-confirm testid is NOT in the DOM (prevents the
    inline button from coming back).
  - Bug #1: assert stepContent's inline-style has
    `minHeight: 380px` + `maxHeight: 520px` + `overflowY:
    auto`.
- E2E: 3 references in `convert-to-book.spec.ts` migrated.
  + 1 new layout-stability spec asserting the action-button's
  bounding-box Y is consistent across all 6 steps within a
  6px tolerance (per the
  "Playwright-visible ≠ User-visible" rule — bounding-box
  is the honest signal, not just testid existence).

### Verification at close

- Vitest 1994 → 1996 (+2 regression pins, 30 → 32 in the
  ConvertToBookWizard suite).
- Type-check clean.
- Pre-commit: all hooks green.
- E2E spec parses; `playwright test --list` shows 4 tests in
  the file (was 3).

### Recurring-Component-Unification check (per the backlog item)

The backlog asked: do ConvertToBookWizard + CreateBookModal +
ImportWizardModal + ExportDialog + AppDialog share a
dialog-stability pattern? Answer for this session: **no**. The
dimension-constraint pattern shipped here is wizard-step-body-
specific (the `stepContent` div lives inside the wizard).
CreateBookModal / ExportDialog / ImportWizardModal each manage
their own body sizing differently (CreateBookModal is single-
panel; ExportDialog is grid-based; ImportWizardModal has
per-step embedded scroll). No 2nd-surface RCU trigger fires.

If a future 2nd wizard ever ships in Bibliogon's codebase
(currently only KDP + Convert ride WizardShell), a
`WIZARD-STEP-CONTENT-SIZING-EXTRACT-01` could promote the
dimension constants into WizardShell itself. Not filed today —
single-surface use, no near-term 2nd-site signal.

### Commits

- C1 `9fb224b` — `feat(convert-to-book): action-button to
  WizardNav footer + stable dialog dimensions` (component fix
  + Vitest rename + 2 new regression pins + E2E rename +
  layout-stability E2E spec).
- C2 (this commit) — backlog close + archive.

## Archived 2026-05-22 (MEDIUM-IMPORT-EXCERPT-AUTOFILL-01 CLOSED — Article.excerpt filled from subtitle or body-text slice on import + retro-fix script)

MEDIUM-IMPORT-EXCERPT-AUTOFILL-01 was filed as P5 during the
2026-05-11 SEO retro-fix work (commit `d195ab4`). The companion
`fix_medium_import_seo.py` explicitly deferred `Article.excerpt`:
"User explicitly deferred that decision. When that ships, run the
matching retro-fix script separately." Closed in the 2026-05-22
session.

### Pre-Inspection findings

- **Current importer state** (`importer.py:471-483`): creates
  Article without setting `excerpt` → NULL by default. The
  existing `seo_description = subtitle or None` pattern follows
  the SEO-D precedent (strict-NULL when no subtitle).
- **Excerpt model field**: `Text, nullable=True`, no max-length.
  Documented as the "long-form summary" used in feed-tile display
  AND as the publish-time fallback for `seo_description`.
- **Source data available**: subtitle (192/209 in earlier corpus),
  TipTap `content_doc` (always present). Medium HTML strips meta
  descriptions across the 209-corpus.
- **Production DB**: 0 articles (cleared since the original
  import). Retro-fix script ships as infrastructure for any
  future re-import.
- **Frontend usage**: excerpt is searched (`useArticleFilters`)
  and referenced by `FieldClassDialog` (AI-template field-class),
  but NOT displayed in article cards/rows. No Vitest changes
  needed; the existing 2 Vitest test files that touch excerpt
  stay green.

### Scope decisions

- `excerpt = subtitle` when subtitle is present (mirrors
  seo_description's source).
- `excerpt = body-text slice` (max 300 chars, sentence-boundary
  preferred above 200 chars; else hard-truncate + "...") when no
  subtitle but the doc has body text.
- `excerpt = NULL` when both subtitle is absent AND the doc has
  no extractable body text.
- **seo_description behavior UNCHANGED.** The SEO-D precedent
  pinned by `test_seo_description_null_when_post_has_no_subtitle`
  stays at import time. Excerpt is more permissive than
  seo_description by design — its display-tile semantics justify
  a fallback that the strict SEO field doesn't get. At publish
  time, `seo_description ← excerpt` is documented behavior; users
  who want strict SEO edit either field manually.

### Shipped (C1, commit `66a1161`)

**Importer change** (`bibliogon_medium_import/importer.py`):
- New `_body_text_excerpt(content_doc, max_chars=300)` helper.
  Walks TipTap JSON via the existing `_flatten_body_text`
  utility; prefers last `. ` / `! ` / `? ` marker within budget;
  falls back to hard-truncate `+ "..."` when no sentence
  boundary appears at or above `_EXCERPT_MIN_SLICE` (200 chars).
- Wired into the Article construction block (line 472): `excerpt
  = subtitle or _body_text_excerpt(parsed.content_doc)`.

**Tests**:
- **8 new pytest unit cases** in
  `plugins/bibliogon-plugin-medium-import/tests/test_excerpt_helper.py`
  covering length cap, sentence boundary, hard-truncate, empty /
  whitespace-only docs, multi-paragraph concatenation, sentence-
  boundary-below-min-slice fallback, custom max_chars.
- **3 new endpoint tests** in
  `backend/tests/test_medium_import_endpoint.py`: subtitle →
  excerpt, no-subtitle → body slice (with SEO-D regression-pin),
  empty-stub → body slice (not NULL).

**Retro-fix script**
(`scripts/fix_medium_import_excerpt.py`):
- Mirrors `fix_medium_import_seo.py` pattern exactly.
- Scoped via `ArticleImportSource` (Medium-only).
- Per-field idempotency gate (only fills when current value is
  NULL or empty; manual curation preserved).
- Dry-run by default; `--apply` to write.
- Imports `_body_text_excerpt` from the plugin so the retro-fix
  logic matches the importer's behavior exactly.

### Verification at close

- Backend pytest 2207 → 2210 (+3 new endpoint tests).
- Plugin pytest medium-import 89 → 97 (+8 helper tests).
- Pre-commit: all hooks green.
- SEO-D regression-pin still green
  (`test_seo_description_null_when_post_has_no_subtitle`).

### What this commit did NOT touch

- `seo_description` behavior at import time (still strict-NULL
  when no subtitle).
- Frontend article-list / card UI (excerpt not currently rendered
  there — separate display-extension P5 if needed).
- Other importers (Substack, etc.) — single-source-of-truth
  decision deferred per "the importer is plugin-scoped" rule.

### No filings

No follow-up backlog entries. The Pre-Inspection's "display-
excerpt-in-card" candidate was NOT pursued — that's an entirely
separate UX surface (when the user wants feed-tile excerpts in
the article list), and the data-side groundwork is now in place
when the time comes.

### Commits

- C1 `66a1161` — `feat(medium-import): auto-fill excerpt from
  subtitle or body slice` (importer + helper + retro-fix script
  + 11 tests).
- C2 (this commit) — backlog close + archive.

## Archived 2026-05-22 (EDITOR-KEYBOARD-SHORTCUT-ALT-Z-01 CLOSED — Alt+Z word-wrap toggle shipped across every editor surface via single body-level CSS class)

EDITOR-KEYBOARD-SHORTCUT-ALT-Z-01 was filed 2026-05-18 from
real-user-smoke during Picture-Book + Article-conversion
workflow. Industry-standard Alt+Z (VS Code / Sublime /
IntelliJ — toggles word-wrap) had no handler in any
Bibliogon editor surface.

### Pre-Inspection findings

- `useKeyboardShortcuts` already exists as the canonical
  app-level keyboard shortcut registry (App.tsx line 86,
  used for Ctrl+/). Its `matchesCombo` handles `alt+z`
  natively and its `isEditableTarget` guard skips when the
  shortcut has a modifier — so Alt+Z fires correctly even
  when the editor is focused.
- All TipTap surfaces (Editor.tsx, RichTextEditor.tsx,
  ComicBookEditor.tsx) render `<EditorContent />` which
  produces a `.ProseMirror` DOM class — TipTap-internal,
  stable across versions, NOT a CSS-module hash.
- Markdown editor at Editor.tsx:1358 is a
  `<textarea className={styles.markdownEditor}>` (CSS-module-
  hashed but the `markdownEditor` substring survives the
  hash suffix).
- No TipTap extension assumes wrapping; a pure CSS toggle
  is safe across all 16+1 mounted extensions.

The filing assumed 4 separate handlers across 4 editor
surfaces (1-2 commits per surface) plus per-user preference
infrastructure. Pre-Inspection collapsed this to ONE
handler at the App level + ONE CSS rule on document.body +
one new hook, because the existing shortcut registry
already provides the single insertion point and CSS
class-substring matching handles every editor surface in
one rule.

### Scope shipped (C1)

- **New hook**: `frontend/src/hooks/useWordWrap.ts` (84 LOC)
  — state + localStorage persistence (key
  `bibliogon-word-wrap-disabled`, matches the existing theme
  preference convention) + body class sync via useEffect.
  Returns `{disabled, toggle}`.
- **Wired into App.tsx**: the existing `useKeyboardShortcuts`
  call now registers `alt+z` alongside the prior `ctrl+/`.
  No restructuring of App.tsx.
- **CSS rule** in `global.css`: `body.no-word-wrap
  .ProseMirror, body.no-word-wrap [class*="markdownEditor"]
  { white-space: pre; overflow-x: auto; }`. Covers all
  TipTap surfaces + the markdown textarea in one selector.
- **Cheatsheet entry** in `APP_SHORTCUTS` for the Ctrl+/
  panel + i18n key `ui.shortcuts.toggle_word_wrap` in all 8
  catalogs (DE / EN / ES / FR / EL / PT / TR / JA, 75/75
  parity maintained).
- **Silent toggle**: no toast on Alt+Z. The editor's visual
  state IS the feedback (matches VS Code / Sublime /
  IntelliJ — none of those show a popup on Alt+Z either).
- **Vitest**: 7 new tests pinning default state /
  stored-read-on-mount / forward toggle / reverse toggle /
  round-trip / `localStorage.getItem`-throws-on-read /
  `localStorage.setItem`-throws-on-write graceful degrade.
  All green. Vitest 1987 → 1994 (+7).

### Smoke test (C2)

`e2e/smoke/editor-word-wrap-toggle.spec.ts` — 2 cases:

1. Forward + reverse toggle in the TipTap chapter editor.
   Asserts the **COMPUTED CSS** `white-space` property
   (`pre-wrap` → `pre` → `pre-wrap`), not just the body
   class. Per the
   "Playwright-visible ≠ User-visible" lessons-learned rule,
   the rendered style is the only honest signal.
2. Persistence across page reload via localStorage.

Spec lists cleanly: 2 tests detected by `playwright test
--list`. Aster runs the suite.

### Recurring-Component-Unification check

The filing identified the 4 editor surfaces as a candidate
for the 2-surfaces rule and tracked a follow-up
`KEYBOARD-SHORTCUTS-SHARED-EXTRACTION-01`. Pre-Inspection
inverted this: the surfaces already SHARE the
`useKeyboardShortcuts` hook AND the `.ProseMirror` DOM
class. No extraction needed; the shared infrastructure
already existed. The follow-up `KEYBOARD-SHORTCUTS-SHARED-
EXTRACTION-01` becomes moot for this shortcut.

### Filings

None. The Pre-Inspection scope-expansion candidate
(other industry-standard editor shortcuts: Ctrl+/
comment-toggle, Ctrl+D duplicate-line, Ctrl+Shift+K
delete-line) was NOT pursued — that work belongs in its
own coordinated session if it becomes a user-stated need.
The current ship covers the specific real-user complaint
that triggered this filing.

### Verification at close

- Type-check clean (`npx tsc --noEmit`).
- Vitest: 1994 / 1994 passing (1987 baseline + 7 new).
- Pre-commit: all hooks green.
- i18n parity: 8/8 catalogs carry
  `ui.shortcuts.toggle_word_wrap`.
- Both commits ride green individually.

## Archived 2026-05-24 (BOOK-TYPES-SSOT-YAML-01 CLOSED — backend/config/book-types.yaml + BookTypeRegistry + /api/book-types + useBookTypes() + 6 consumer migrations)

BOOK-TYPES-SSOT-YAML-01 was filed 2026-05-23 from the
GETSTARTED-MULTIBOOK-TYPES-UPDATE-01 C5 close per Q4
adjudication. Book-type metadata had been scattered across
24 production files (3 hardcoded enum copies + a UI
metadata array + per-type capability-check helpers + per-type
branches across backend / frontend / 4 plugins) with NO
canonical source. Each new book-type-aware surface duplicated
the same label / description / capability data; adding a
4th book type would have required N file edits.

The fix consolidates everything into
``backend/config/book-types.yaml`` + a Pydantic-validated
BookTypeRegistry. Frontend + plugins consume via a runtime
``/api/book-types`` endpoint (React Context-cached) +
direct ``from app.services.book_type_registry import ...``
imports respectively.

### Pre-Coding-Reality-Check findings

Filing estimated 5 scattered surfaces. Audit's Track 1
inventory found 24 (5 definition sites + 19 consumption
sites — 4.8× higher). Three STOP conditions fired and
were user-adjudicated:

- **Q1.A**: Full-scope ship, 10 commits.
- **Q2.A**: Core-owns-all PluginForge boundary model
  (plugins consume read-only; speculative β
  plugin-extends-via-hookspec deferred).
- **Q3.A**: Runtime ``/api/book-types`` API + React
  Context (mirrors platform_schema precedent rather than
  build-time JSON bundling).
- **Q4.A**: BookType Literal stays as a Pydantic type
  signature + a verification test
  (``test_literal_matches_registry``) asserts parity with
  the YAML id set.
- **Q5.A**: Single session, 10 commits.

### What shipped (1 Pre-Inspection + 10 commits)

| # | SHA | Subject |
|---|---|---|
| Audit | `796ab66` | `docs(audits): BOOK-TYPES-SSOT-YAML-01 Pre-Inspection` |
| C1 | `d2dcd8e` | BookTypeRegistry + book-types.yaml + 22 backend tests |
| C2 | `91a33b5` | GET /api/book-types endpoint + 4 endpoint tests |
| C3 | `a098818` | useBookTypes() + BookTypesProvider + 13 Vitest cases |
| C4 | `759d056` | Migrate pages.py PAGEABLE_BOOK_TYPES → registry |
| C5 | `f6e2227` | Migrate Dashboard + GetStarted (BookTypeIcon util) |
| C6 | `07f8a44` | Migrate CreateBookModal + BookEditor (editor dispatch) |
| C7 | `f82c189` | Migrate BookMetadataEditor + kdp-wizard capability checks |
| C8 | `31a6486` | Migrate plugin-getstarted (lazy import + fallback) |
| C9 | `c68ec21` | Migrate plugin-kdp/package.py chapter-filter |
| C10 | (this commit) | Backlog close + monthly archive |

### Design + API

`backend/config/book-types.yaml` ships 3 entries (prose,
picture_book, comic_book) with:
- ``id`` / ``label_key`` / ``description_key`` / ``icon``
- ``content_model`` ("chapters" | "pages") — drives the
  ``pageable_book_types()`` set + the
  ``isChapterBasedBookType`` capability
- ``editor_component`` (string name like "PageEditor"
  resolved to the React component via the
  EDITOR_COMPONENTS dispatch table in BookEditor.tsx)
- ``capabilities`` (6 flags: ebook_export, paperback_export,
  hardcover_export, audiobook_export, template_catalog,
  kdp_package_supported) — negative-default semantics
- ``dashboard_create_visible`` + ``immutable_after_create``
- ``default_page_size`` for page-based types

`BookTypeRegistry` mirrors the platform_schema precedent:
``@lru_cache(maxsize=1)`` loader + Pydantic validation +
typed helpers (``get_book_type``, ``book_type_ids``,
``pageable_book_types``, ``book_types_with_capability``,
``immutable_book_field_ids``).

`useBookTypes()` React hook + `BookTypesProvider` mounted
at App root (between I18nProvider and DialogProvider).
Provider fetches once on app mount; silent fail-open on
error (status="error", types={}); ``initialTypes`` escape-
hatch lets tests skip the fetch + supply a static snapshot.

### Consumer migration matrix

| Surface | Before | After |
|---|---|---|
| `pages.py` | hardcoded `PAGEABLE_BOOK_TYPES` frozenset | `pageable_book_types()` registry call |
| `Dashboard.tsx` editor-route | `=== "picture_book" \|\| === "comic_book"` | `pageableBookTypeIds(snapshot).has(...)` |
| `Dashboard.tsx` dropdown menu | 2 hardcoded items | `.filter(bt.dashboard_create_visible && id !== "prose").map(...)` |
| `GetStarted.tsx` | `BOOK_TYPE_CARDS` array (15 lines) | `bookTypeCards = useBookTypes().ordered` |
| `CreateBookModal.tsx` template tab | `bookType === "prose"` | `capabilities.template_catalog` |
| `BookEditor.tsx` editor dispatch | 2 near-identical per-type branches | unified content_model + EDITOR_COMPONENTS map |
| `BookMetadataEditor.tsx` | `isChapterBasedBookType()` helper | `contentModel === "chapters"` |
| `MetadataChecklist.tsx` | `filterIssuesForBookType(_, bookType)` | `filterIssuesForBookType(_, contentModel)` |
| `PricingStep.tsx` | `isEbookSupported(bookType)` helper | `capabilities.ebook_export` |
| `plugin-getstarted/guide.py` | `BOOK_TYPES = ("prose", ...)` tuple | `book_type_ids()` lazy-import |
| `plugin-kdp/package.py` | `if book_type != "prose":` chapter-drop | `if content_model == "pages":` |

### Skipped migrations (documented)

Two audit-recommended migrations were skipped after Pre-
Coding-Reality-Check found them over-eager:

1. **plugin-export routes.py dispatch** (audit Track 3 P4).
   The per-type loaders + walkers have different
   signatures (picture-book returns 3-tuple, comic-book
   returns 5-tuple; picture-book walker takes 3 args,
   comic-book walker takes 5). A content_model gate could
   wrap the outer "is this page-based?" check but the
   inner dispatch is inherently per-type by data-shape
   necessity. SSoT doesn't help.
2. **plugin-kdp/package.py manuscript dispatch** (audit
   Track 3 P8). Same shape as plugin-export — three
   `_generate_*_manuscript` functions with different
   signatures + return types. The OUTER chapter-filter
   gate IS migrated (C9); the inner per-type fn picker
   stays.

Documented in C8 + C9 commit messages.

### Test deltas

- Backend pytest: 2181 → **2207** (+26)
  - 22 BookTypeRegistry tests (real-YAML + faked-YAML
    + the SSoT verification gate
    ``test_literal_matches_registry``)
  - 4 endpoint tests
- Frontend Vitest: 1974 → **1987** (+13)
  - 13 useBookTypes() hook + selectors + Provider cases
- i18n parity: 75/75 (unchanged; no new strings — labels
  reference existing keys)
- tsc --noEmit clean throughout
- 10 test files updated to wrap renders in
  BookTypesProvider (no behavioral changes; pure setup
  churn). The wrapper-based `render()` pattern in
  BookMetadataEditor.test.tsx + MetadataChecklist.test.tsx
  + PricingStep.test.tsx redefines render to auto-wrap
  every call site without per-call churn.

### Static-analysis vs runtime fallback discipline

Plugins import `from app.services.book_type_registry import
...`. Static analyzers (pyright, etc.) flag this as
unresolvable because each plugin's pyproject.toml sets its
own import-root; the backend's `app` package is on sys.path
only at runtime via Poetry path-dep. This is the same
benign warning that fires for every existing `from app.*`
import in plugins.

Plugin standalone-pytest paths (poetry venv without backend
installed) crash on the runtime import too. Mitigation:
plugin-getstarted (C8) + plugin-kdp (C9) use a try/except
ImportError pattern with a frozen fallback set. The
fallback only fires when the backend is genuinely
unavailable; in production + the combined ``make test``
path, the registry is the source of truth.

### Followups

None filed. The migration is complete; no half-wired
surfaces. Two NOT-migrated surfaces (plugin-export
loaders + plugin-kdp manuscript dispatch) documented in
their commit messages as per-type-by-necessity rather
than capability-driven.

The companion P3 backlog item
``BOOK-TYPE-CARD-COMPONENT-EXTRACT-01`` (RCU 2-site pre-
registered) now consumes the registry's metadata via
useBookTypes() when its 3rd-surface trigger fires — the
SSoT infrastructure is already in place; the extract only
consolidates the card-shape duplication.

## Archived 2026-05-24 (PAGES-DELETE-EDITOR-UI-01 CLOSED — page-delete UI shipped across BOTH editor surfaces via shared PageThumbnails onDelete; Half-Wired-Lifecycle-Cascade-Followup closed)

PAGES-DELETE-EDITOR-UI-01 was filed 2026-05-23 from the
PLUGIN-COMICS-MULTI-PAGE-NAVIGATION-01 C5 close as a
Half-Wired-Lifecycle-Cascade-Followup. Backend has supported
``DELETE /api/books/{id}/pages/{pid}`` since PAGES-CRUD-01
(2026-05-20); ``api.pages.delete`` has existed in the frontend
client since the same release. But NEITHER editor surface
exposed the delete affordance — neither PageEditor (picture_book)
nor ComicBookEditor (comic_book) had a per-page delete control.
The lifecycle was wired backend + client + nothing visible.

The fix landed cross-surface via PageThumbnails (RCU 2-site
benefit): one new ``onDelete?`` prop on the shared component +
two parallel ``handleDeletePage`` callbacks in the editors,
serving both sites simultaneously.

### What shipped (5 commits)

| C | SHA | Subject |
|---|---|---|
| C1 | `acdf4fb` | `feat(pages): PageThumbnails onDelete prop + Trash2 button` — optional prop, opacity-on-hover icon button, +5 Vitest cases |
| C2 | `01b1abf` | `feat(pages): wire onDelete in PageEditor + ComicBookEditor` — useDialog confirm + api.pages.delete + state reconciliation + activePageId cleanup; +11 Vitest cases (6 + 5) |
| C3 | `60122d6` | `i18n(pages): delete_page strings across 8 catalogs` — 3 new keys × 8 catalogs, native translations (no English passthrough) |
| C4 | `c83fe2e` | `test(e2e): page-delete smoke` — 5 Playwright cases covering positive + negative paths across BOTH surfaces |
| C5 | (this commit) | `docs: close PAGES-DELETE-EDITOR-UI-01` — backlog close + monthly archive |

### Design decisions (Pre-Inspection adjudicated)

- **Per-row icon button**, NOT a context menu. The Radix
  DropdownMenu + happy-dom brittleness LL warns against the menu
  approach for Vitest coverage. Icon button stays cleanly
  testable in unit AND E2E.
- **Hidden by default (opacity:0)**, visible on row-hover OR
  row-focus-within (opacity:0.6 → 1 on button-hover). Keeps the
  sidebar uncluttered during normal navigation.
- **Click stops propagation** so the row's onSelect doesn't fire
  along with the delete. Matches the ChapterSidebar pattern.
- **Confirm dialog via AppDialog** with danger variant — same
  precedent as BookEditor.tsx:310 chapter-delete.
- **Parent owns the lifecycle** (confirm → DB → state). The shared
  PageThumbnails just emits the delete request. Mirrors the
  ChapterSidebar's slim delete-emit pattern.
- **No keyboard Delete-key shortcut** in this session. The icon
  button is keyboard-focusable; a global Delete-key would collide
  with @dnd-kit's keyboard reorder semantics. Filed as backlog if
  user demand surfaces.

### State reconciliation (per "Destructive row-actions"
###  lessons-learned rule)

Both editors' ``handleDeletePage``:

1. ``await dialog.confirm(title, message, "danger")`` — bail out on
   ``false``.
2. ``await api.pages.delete(bookId, pageId)`` — on error, set the
   existing error-banner state; row NOT removed.
3. Filter the deleted page from local ``pages`` state.
4. If ``activePageId === pageId``, auto-select the next-by-position
   remaining page (or ``null`` if it was the last).
5. ComicBookEditor additionally clears ``selectedPanelId`` +
   ``selectedBubbleId`` when the deleted page was active (those
   selections are scoped to the deleted page).

### i18n keys added

Section: ``ui.page_editor`` (shared by both editors).

- ``delete_page`` — icon button title + aria-label
- ``delete_page_title`` — confirm dialog title
- ``delete_page_confirm`` — confirm dialog message

Native translations in all 8 catalogs (DE umlauts, ES/PT accents,
FR/EL/JA punctuation per their native conventions). Matches the
existing ``delete_chapter_*`` precedent — none of these were left
as English passthrough.

### Testid contract (new)

Per-row delete-button testid: ``${testidNamespace}-delete-page-${pageId}``

Concrete:
- ``page-editor-delete-page-${pageId}`` (PageEditor surface)
- ``comic-book-editor-delete-page-${pageId}`` (ComicBookEditor surface)

All 16 new Vitest cases positively-assert the testid pattern via
``screen.getByTestId(...)`` per the "Testid namespace pinning
prevents silent E2E skips" lessons-learned rule.

### Cross-surface symmetry

Both editors gain identical UX through the shared component.
RCU 2-site benefit realized at the component-extraction layer
that the v0.34.x PLUGIN-COMICS-MULTI-PAGE-NAVIGATION-01 work
already established. Per the "Articles-vs-Books parallel-surface
asymmetry" lessons-learned rule (generalized to picture_book vs
comic_book): same affordance, same shape, same confirm flow,
same state-reconciliation discipline. Future contributors adding
a 3rd editor surface (hypothetical: novel_book with multi-page
chapters) get the affordance for free via the shared component.

### Test deltas

- Vitest: 1958 → **1974** (+16)
  - 5 cases in PageThumbnails.test.tsx (C1: presence, click,
    stopPropagation, namespace prefix, optional prop)
  - 6 cases in PageEditor.test.tsx (C2: confirm dialog shape,
    delete + state filter, cancel, auto-select next, last-page →
    empty, preserve non-active)
  - 5 cases in ComicBookEditor.test.tsx (C2: button rendering,
    confirm shape, api call args, cancel, empty-state after
    delete)
- Backend pytest: 2181 (unchanged; no backend touch)
- i18n parity: 75/75 (unchanged; 3 keys × 8 catalogs added in
  sync)
- tsc --noEmit: clean throughout
- Playwright: 5 new smoke cases in `e2e/smoke/page-delete.spec.ts`
  (written; user runs per CLAUDE.md "Claude Code writes specs,
  Aster runs them")

### LOC delta

| File | Δ LOC |
|---|---|
| `frontend/src/components/PageThumbnails.tsx` | +38 |
| `frontend/src/components/PageThumbnails.module.css` | +28 |
| `frontend/src/components/PageThumbnails.test.tsx` | +97 |
| `frontend/src/components/PageEditor.tsx` | +44 |
| `frontend/src/components/PageEditor.test.tsx` | +138 |
| `frontend/src/components/ComicBookEditor.tsx` | +43 |
| `frontend/src/components/ComicBookEditor.test.tsx` | +133 |
| `backend/config/i18n/*.yaml` (8 files) | +24 (3 per catalog) |
| `e2e/smoke/page-delete.spec.ts` | +200 (new) |
| **Total** | **+745 lines, of which ~568 are tests (76%)** |

Production code delta is ~177 LOC for a feature that closes a
user-visible Half-Wired gap across two editor surfaces. The
test-to-prod ratio reflects the regression-pin discipline:
every flow that mattered to ship now has a pinned assertion.

### No followups filed

The page-delete lifecycle is now complete — no half-wired
surfaces left behind. Future-work pre-registered triggers (if
they ever fire):

- Keyboard Delete-key shortcut: if user demand surfaces.
- Undo / restore for deleted pages: if user demand surfaces
  (current behavior is hard-delete, matching backend semantics).
- Bulk multi-select delete: if user demand surfaces (current
  scope is single-row).

### Cross-references

- Parent filing: `PLUGIN-COMICS-MULTI-PAGE-NAVIGATION-01` (closed
  2026-05-23 via 5-commit ship `87a91d6..acdb1c0`) — the same
  RCU 2-site cross-surface pattern that established PageThumbnails
  as the shared sidebar.
- Sibling lessons-learned:
  - "Destructive row-actions must reconcile collection state"
    (drove the state-reconciliation discipline in C2)
  - "Half-wired feature lifecycle: a state-write without its
    inverse-mutation OR its state-consumer is purgatory" (the
    pattern this filing closes)
  - "Testid namespace pinning prevents silent E2E skips" (drove
    the positive-assertion discipline in all 16 new Vitest cases)
  - "Articles-vs-Books parallel-surface asymmetry" (generalised
    to picture_book vs comic_book — both editors got the
    identical affordance in the same session)

## Archived 2026-05-24 (WIZARD-SHELL-COMPONENT-EXTRACT-01 CLOSED — RCU 2-site WizardShell + WizardNav shipped; KDP + Convert wizards migrated; ImportWizardModal stays out by design)

WIZARD-SHELL-COMPONENT-EXTRACT-01 was filed 2026-05-22 from
the KDP-PUBLISHING-WIZARD-01-PHASE-2 Session 1 C7 close. The
original audit and filing both counted 3 wizard surfaces;
the 2026-05-24 implementation session's Pre-Coding-Reality-
Check revised the scope to RCU 2-site per the user-
adjudicated Option A.

### Pre-Coding-Reality-Check finding (load-bearing)

The original audit's premise — "three wizard surfaces share
Dialog-chrome + step-indicator + nav-buttons + testid-namespace
wiring" — was true for KDP + Convert but not for
ImportWizardModal. Five load-bearing shape divergences:

1. **Dialog styling** is className-based (with CSS
   animation), not inline-style.
2. **Width is 900px**, not 640px (multi-book preview tables
   need the extra width).
3. **Step indicator is text** ("Step X of 4"), not dot-row
   (multiple steps map to the same number).
4. **Navigation buttons live INSIDE each step component**,
   not in the shell (each step has its own back / cancel /
   confirm / retry semantics).
5. **WizardErrorBoundary** wraps the body (neither other
   wizard uses one).

Forcing extraction would either bloat WizardShell into a
god-component with optional config flags OR strip
ImportWizardModal's useful patterns. Either is worse than
the documented divergence.

Three options surfaced to user (Option A / B / C); user
adjudicated **Option A** (extract for the 2 genuine sites,
leave ImportWizardModal as-is, file P5 trigger for future).

### What shipped (5 commits)

| C | SHA | Subject |
|---|---|---|
| C1 | `52b9f3e` | `feat(wizards): extract WizardShell + WizardNav (C1)` — new `frontend/src/components/wizards/WizardShell.tsx` (~340 LOC) + 17 Vitest cases |
| C2 | `5bb0968` | `refactor(kdp-wizard): migrate KdpPublishingWizard to WizardShell (C2)` — -141 LOC |
| C3 | `a94e0b9` | `refactor(convert-to-book): migrate ConvertToBookWizard to WizardShell (C3)` — -191 LOC net; StepDef.label made optional + 1 new Vitest case |
| C4 | `a4ca73f` | `docs(wizards): intentional-asymmetry note + WIZARD-SHELL-IMPORT-VARIANT-01 filing (C4)` |
| C5 | (this commit) | `docs(wizards): close WIZARD-SHELL-COMPONENT-EXTRACT-01 (C5)` — backlog close + monthly archive |

### Design + API

`WizardShell` is composition-based via React context for
namespace threading. Slots:

- `title` + `titleIcon` (top of Dialog)
- `subtitle` (optional; KDP uses book.title)
- `steps` + `currentStep` + `stepColorPolicy` (dot indicator)
- `banner` (optional; KDP uses conflict banner, Convert uses
  validation banner)
- `children` (body content)
- `nav` (optional `<WizardNav>` slot)
- `bodyRef` (for consumer focus management on step change)

`WizardNav` (companion) reads namespace from context, threads
testids as `{namespace}-step-{step}-back/skip/next/finish`.
Each button shown only when its handler prop is defined.

Dots carry `data-step-state` ("current" | "completed" |
"visited" | "future") for testable contract + future CSS
targeting. happy-dom can't parse nested `var()` in inline
style.background, so tests assert against `data-step-state`
attribute.

Two coloring policies:
- `single` (KDP shape) — visited vs unvisited (one accent
  color for everything up to + including current step)
- `current-vs-completed` (Convert shape) — three distinct
  colors (current=accent, completed=success-green,
  future=border)

### Testid preservation

ALL shell-level testids preserved verbatim (WizardShell
threads them via the `namespace` prop):

**KDP** (unchanged):
- `kdp-publishing-wizard-dialog`
- `kdp-publishing-wizard-book-title`
- `kdp-publishing-wizard-step-indicator`
- `kdp-publishing-wizard-step-dot-{0..4}`
- `kdp-publishing-wizard-step-{0..4}-back / next / finish`
- `kdp-publishing-wizard-close`
- `kdp-publishing-wizard-conflict-banner` (banner content
  stays in KDP, routed through banner slot)
- `kdp-publishing-wizard-conflict-dismiss`

**Convert** (preserved + additive):
- `convert-to-book-wizard-step-{0..5}-back / skip / next`
  (preserved)
- `convert-to-book-wizard-validation-banner` (preserved,
  routed through banner slot)
- ADDITIVE: `convert-to-book-wizard-dialog`,
  `-step-indicator`, `-step-dot-{0..5}`, `-close` (Convert
  had no shell-level testids before; gains them now from
  the shared shell)

|---|---|

| `frontend/src/components/kdp-wizard/KdpPublishingWizard.tsx` | -141 net (-214 + 73) |

### Followup filings

backend endpoints under `/api/kdp/*` with **zero frontend

shape. Phase 1 closes the gap: `api.kdp.checkMetadata` (C2),

still has zero consumers (revival is a separate filing if
ever needed).

architecture doc. User adjudicated path (γ): finish Phase 1
hand-rolled (already shipped C0-C2 with zero behavioral cost
to rewind), file `KDP-WIZARD-XSTATE-MIGRATION-01` as the
Phase-2-paired migration. Both honored: session instruction
ships, architecture doc gets paired follow-up at the natural
seam.

## Archived 2026-05-24 (RECURRING-COMPONENT-AUDIT-01 close — umbrella audit deliverable shipped; per-candidate extraction items remain as their own backlog entries)

Housekeeping close. The umbrella audit item is closed because its
deliverable shipped 2026-05-21; the audit's recommended extraction
sequence is being worked through under per-candidate backlog
filings (each with its own trigger), which is the correct shape
per the original filing's own deliverable description.

### What shipped earlier (and is the canonical close artefact)

`docs/audits/recurring-component-audit-2026-05-21.md` (565 lines,
audited at commit `64a067e`, 7 + 2 anti-pattern candidates
evaluated). 4-Axes scoring (Site-count, Drift-Risk, Extraction-
Ease, Downstream-Value); 12-point action floor; HIGH / MEDIUM /
LOW tiers; recommended ordering of extraction sessions; per-
candidate backlog filings.

The audit doc carries closed-in-action footnotes that the
follow-up extraction sessions added (2026-05-22 → 2026-05-23):
each candidate's outcome (SHIPPED / DEFERRED-PERMANENT /
REMAINS AVAILABLE / NEW candidate surfaced) recorded inline.
That document is the durable audit-trail; the backlog entry
was a forward-looking placeholder once the deliverable
shipped.

### Audit-recommended sequence — closure status

| Rank | Name | Score | Status |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | `useSelection<T>()` generic hook | 16 | DEFERRED-PERMANENT (design-intent honored, adjudicated 2026-05-23) |
| 2 | `BulkActionBar` shared component | 15 | SHIPPED `c2305e7` (2026-05-22) via path γ pivot |
| 3 | `ListRow` shared component | 13 | OPEN — `LIST-VIEW-ROW-SHARED-EXTRACTION-01`, trigger-gated |
| 4 | `AuthorSelectInput` shared component | 12 | SHIPPED `a213788` (2026-05-23) via path α |
| — | NEW Pattern B `AuthorProfileSelect` | 13 | SHIPPED `11198a4` (2026-05-23); surfaced during candidate-#4 Pre-Coding-Reality-Check |
| 5 | PdfExportControls consolidation | 9 | BELOW 12-point floor; no extraction planned |
| 6 | `Card` shared grid component | 8 | BELOW 12-point floor; no extraction planned |
| 7 | `FilterBar<TFilters>` further generic | 8 | BELOW 12-point floor; no extraction planned |

### Methodology-gap closed-in-action

The Pattern B `AuthorProfileSelect` candidate (score 13) was
surfaced AFTER the original audit, during candidate-#4's Pre-
Coding-Reality-Check. The audit's file-level component scan
had missed it because both `AuthorSelect` and `AuthorSelectField`
were inline functions inside larger page/component files
(ArticleEditor 1423 LOC; BookMetadataEditor several-hundred
LOC). The closed-in-action footnote in the audit doc captured
the gap and prescribed the next-iteration grep recipe (inline
functions inside files >500 LOC + doc-comment mirror-references).

A formal Lessons-Learned filing was deferred per
"single instance is incident, not pattern" discipline. If a
future audit iteration surfaces another inline-function-missed-
by-scan candidate, formalize as
`.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md` "Audit methodology: grep
inline functions inside large files".

### Per-candidate backlog items still open (NOT closed by this close)

- `LIST-VIEW-ROW-SHARED-EXTRACTION-01` (P3) — ArticleRow +
  BookListRow. Trigger-gated on third-instance or styling-drift.
- `AUTHOR-DATALIST-EXTEND-EDITORS-01` (P5) — deferred as UX-
  adjudication-required after candidate-#4 close.

These remain in `docs/backlog.md` under their own IDs. The
umbrella-audit close is a housekeeping action only; it does
NOT prejudge the per-candidate items.

### Recurring-Component Unification Rule durability

The rule itself (`.claude/rules/coding-standards.md`
"Recurring-Component Unification Rule") is the lasting outcome
of this audit cycle. Future component-extraction work fires the
rule at the 2-surfaces threshold; the per-candidate filings
follow the same 4-Axes scoring + extraction-plus-migration
session shape. The umbrella audit was a one-time sweep of
accumulated candidates from before the rule was formalized; the
rule itself does the ongoing detection.

### Files touched (this close)

- `docs/backlog.md` — entry removed from P2 section; header
  count 70 → 69; "Last updated" note updated with closure
  rationale.
- `docs/archive/roadmap/2026-05.md` — this archive entry.

No code changes. Audit doc + 4 prior extraction commits are the
substantive artefacts; this close is documentation hygiene.

comics Sessions 1+2 + Phase 1 + Phase 2 + PAGES-CRUD +
MULTI-PAGE-NAVIGATION all shipped) — closed via β-scope

adjudication.

cover both chapters AND pages. Net effect: returning users
who completed `add-chapters` see their progress preserved;
the new `choose-book-type` step appears as the only
incomplete addition.

Extended P1 promotion.

## Archived 2026-05-23 (RECURRING-COMPONENT-AUDIT-01 audit-followup — Pattern B `AuthorProfileSelect` 2-site extraction; methodology-gap closed-in-action)

Single-commit RCU 2-site extraction shipped as `11198a4`. Closes
the Pattern B audit-followup candidate that was filed earlier
today via commit `4220267` after the candidate-#4 Pre-Coding-
Reality-Check surfaced the methodology gap.

### What shipped

New pure-presentational component at
`frontend/src/components/AuthorProfileSelect.tsx` (~170 LOC) +
`AuthorProfileSelect.test.tsx` (12 Vitest cases). Migrated 2
sites in same commit per RCU canonical:

  - `frontend/src/pages/ArticleEditor.tsx` — replaced
    `<AuthorSelect>` callsite + DELETED 60-LOC inline
    `function AuthorSelect` (lines 1211-1275). Bare `<select>`
    styling preserved via `selectStyle` prop. No test consumers
    of the testid; no migration risk.
  - `frontend/src/components/BookMetadataEditor.tsx` — inline
    `function AuthorSelectField` kept as a 50-LOC adapter (was
    90 LOC); body's inline `<select>` replaced with
    `<AuthorProfileSelect>`. Wrapping (`<div className="field">`
    + `<label>` + manage-link to /settings?tab=author) stays in
    the adapter. The `metadata-author-select` testid IS pinned
    by 4 references in BookMetadataEditor.test.tsx; all 58
    tests preserved without rewrites.

### Component design — prop-driven slot variations

The two sites differ in 3 axes that the component absorbs as
props:

  - **emptyOptionLabel**: `string | null`. Non-null renders a
    selectable `<option value="">{label}</option>` leading
    option (Article's always-shown "(kein Autor)"; Book's
    `allowEmpty`-gated "(no author)"). Null routes to:
  - **placeholderLabel** (optional): renders a disabled
    `<option value="" disabled>{label}</option>` placeholder
    when `value === ""` AND `emptyOptionLabel` is null (Book's
    pre-allowEmpty UX).
  - **unknownValueWrapper** (optional): `(value) => {label,
    disabled}`. Default behavior renders unknown legacy values
    as plain selectable options (Article). Book passes a
    wrapper for `{label: "[unbekannt: X]", disabled: true}` to
    show but not re-select unknown values.

Plus `penNamesGroupLabel`, `testId`, `selectClassName`,
`selectStyle` for per-site backward-compat.

### Adapter-pattern vs direct-replacement

ArticleEditor's inline `AuthorSelect` was a bare `<select>` with
no surrounding structure — direct-replacement at the callsite +
deletion of the inline function was the right call.

BookMetadataEditor's inline `AuthorSelectField` wraps the
`<select>` in a `<div className="field">` + `<label>` +
manage-link to Settings. Keeping `AuthorSelectField` as a thin
adapter that delegates the inner `<select>` to
AuthorProfileSelect preserves the wrapping where it belongs
(per the "Inline-component duplication is the upstream cause
of parallel-surface asymmetry" LL — the wrapping is unique to
BookMetadataEditor, not a duplicate).

This mirrors the BulkActionBar adapter-pattern from 2026-05-22
(commit `c2305e7`): the canonical extraction handles the shared
shape; site-specific wrapping stays in thin adapters per site.

### Methodology-gap closure in-action

The original 2026-05-21 audit's file-level component scan
missed both Pattern B definitions because they're INLINE
functions inside larger files (line 1216 of 1423-LOC
ArticleEditor; line 542 of BookMetadataEditor). The audit
footnote at commit `4220267` documented the gap + future-audit
grep recipe. This commit closes the gap by shipping the
extraction the methodology-gap would have surfaced earlier.

The grep recipe documented in the audit footnote is now
load-bearing for the NEXT iteration of the audit. Pattern B
is the first known instance of this gap; per "single instance
is incident, not pattern" discipline, formal Lessons-Learned
filing deferred until a third audit iteration surfaces another
inline-function candidate.

### Tests + baseline

  - tsc --noEmit clean
  - AuthorProfileSelect Vitest 12/12 (new)
  - ArticleEditor Vitest 13/13 (preserved, no rewrites)
  - BookMetadataEditor Vitest 58/58 (preserved, no rewrites;
    4 metadata-author-select testid assertions still pass via
    the `testId` prop pass-through)
  - Full frontend Vitest: 1803 → 1815 (+12; exactly matches
    the 12 new AuthorProfileSelect cases)
  - Backend baseline unchanged (frontend-only work)

### Audit candidates remaining

  - #1 `useSelection<T>()` (score 16) — DEFERRED-PENDING-DESIGN-
    INTENT-ADJUDICATION (per 2026-05-22 audit footnote)
  - #3 `ListRow` (score 13) — available; benefits from
    extracting `ArticleRow` from `ArticleList.tsx` monolith
    first
  - AUTHOR-DATALIST-EXTEND-EDITORS-01 — UX-adjudication-
    required; the choice of whether to replace Pattern B
    (now extracted) with Pattern A `AuthorSelectInput` at
    editor surfaces is a design decision

### Cumulative RCU audit progress

| Candidate | Score | Status | Commit |
|---|---|---|---|
| #1 useSelection<T>() | 16 | DEFERRED | (anti-extraction-rationale honored) |
| #2 BulkActionBar | 15 | SHIPPED 2026-05-22 | `c2305e7` |
| #3 ListRow | 13 | available | — |
| #4 AuthorSelectInput | 12 | SHIPPED 2026-05-23 | `a213788` |
| Pattern B AuthorProfileSelect | 13 | SHIPPED 2026-05-23 | `11198a4` |

3 of 5 candidates shipped (2 sessions; 4 commits feat + 4
commits docs). Audit-as-coordination-instrument working well.

## Archived 2026-05-23 (RECURRING-COMPONENT-AUDIT-01 candidate #4 — `AuthorSelectInput` 2-site extraction via path α; Pattern B newly surfaced)

Single-commit RCU 2-site extraction shipped as `a213788`. Closes
candidate #4 from
`docs/audits/recurring-component-audit-2026-05-21.md`. Plus
surfaces a NEW Pattern-B candidate (estimated score 13) that the
original audit missed due to a methodology gap.

### What shipped

New pure-presentational component at
`frontend/src/components/AuthorSelectInput.tsx` (~155 LOC) +
`AuthorSelectInput.test.tsx` (11 Vitest cases). Migrated 2 sites
in same commit per RCU canonical "extract + migrate in SAME
commit":

  - `frontend/src/components/CreateBookModal.tsx` — replaced
    ~55-LOC input + datalist + checkbox block
  - `frontend/src/components/articles/ConvertToBookWizard.tsx`
    — replaced ~65-LOC block with `inputTestId` +
    `inputId` overrides for backward-compat

The component renders the input + `<datalist>` + optional
"Add to Authors-DB" `<label><input type="checkbox">` cluster.
State (value, authorChoices, globalAuthors, authorSuggestions,
authorAlreadyInDb, showAddToAuthorsCheckbox, addToAuthorsDb)
stays at the caller — the component is purely presentational.

### Pattern history closure

The Bug 8 Phase 2 wizard (2026-04) shipped the input + datalist
+ checkbox pattern. The 2026-05-19 CreateBookModal fix (commit
`49510d0`) cloned it directly. This extraction unifies the two
sites and closes the duplication the 2026-05-19 fix introduced.

### Path α scope: extraction-only, AUTHOR-DATALIST-EXTEND deferred

Pre-Coding-Reality-Check revealed that the user-prompt's
optional pair-shipping with `AUTHOR-DATALIST-EXTEND-EDITORS-01`
would actually REPLACE an existing different pattern (Pattern
B, see below) at ArticleEditor + BookMetadataEditor — a UX
design decision, not a mechanical migration. User adjudicated
path α (extraction-only); AUTHOR-DATALIST-EXTEND-EDITORS-01
stays open as UX-adjudication-required for a separate session.

### inputTestId override for backward-compat

ConvertToBookWizard's existing input testid is
"convert-to-book-wizard-metadata-author" (the "metadata-"
segment doesn't fit the canonical `${testidPrefix}-author`
derivation). Rather than renaming the testid — which would
break 12+ E2E + Vitest references pinning the existing name —
the component exposes an optional `inputTestId` override. The
datalist + checkbox + suggestion testids still derive from
`testidPrefix` (which both sites already followed
canonically). Per the "Testid namespace pinning prevents
silent E2E skips" LL.

### NEW: Pattern-B candidate surfaced (estimated score 13)

Pre-Coding-Reality-Check uncovered a SECOND author-related
RCU candidate the original audit missed:

  - `function AuthorSelect` at
    `frontend/src/pages/ArticleEditor.tsx:1216-1275`
  - `function AuthorSelectField` at
    `frontend/src/components/BookMetadataEditor.tsx:542`

These are a FUNDAMENTALLY DIFFERENT pattern from Pattern A
(AuthorSelectInput just shipped):

  - Pattern A (`<input>` + `<datalist>`): autocomplete from
    external `api.authors.list`; free-text allowed; "Add to
    Authors-DB" checkbox.
  - Pattern B (`<select>` + `<optgroup>`): closed list of
    user's-own profile names (real-name + pen-names from
    `useAuthorProfile()` hook); no free-text; no DB
    integration.

The ArticleEditor's inline doc-comment self-identifies as a
mirror: *"Mirrors the BookEditor AuthorPicker's matched-state
ProfileSelect, simplified for the Article editor."* That's a
load-bearing RCU-2-site signal. A1=2, A2=4 (explicit mirror +
drift potential), A3=4 (clean prop-injection contract), A4=3
→ total **13**, ranks at parity with candidate #3 (ListRow).
Filed as audit-followup; deferred for a future implementation
session.

### Methodology gap closure

The original audit (2026-05-21) used a file-level component
scan that found 7 candidates but missed Pattern B because the
two AuthorSelect / AuthorSelectField definitions are INLINE
functions inside larger page/component files (line 1216 of a
1423-LOC ArticleEditor; line 542 of BookMetadataEditor).
Documented as a methodology gap in the audit footnote;
future audits should grep for inline function definitions
inside large files (>500 LOC) + grep doc-comments for explicit
mirror-references ("Mirrors the X", "Cloned from Y") which are
the load-bearing RCU-2-site signals.

### Tests + baseline

  - tsc --noEmit clean
  - AuthorSelectInput Vitest 11/11 (new)
  - CreateBookModal Vitest 32/32 (preserved, no rewrites)
  - ConvertToBookWizard Vitest 30/30 (preserved, no rewrites)
  - Full frontend Vitest: 1792 → 1803 (+11; exactly matches
    the 11 new AuthorSelectInput cases)
  - Backend baseline unchanged (frontend-only work)

### Audit candidates remaining

  - #1 `useSelection<T>()` (score 16) — DEFERRED-PENDING-DESIGN-
    INTENT-ADJUDICATION (per 2026-05-22 audit footnote)
  - #3 `ListRow` (score 13) — available; benefits from
    extracting `ArticleRow` from `ArticleList.tsx` monolith
    first
  - **NEW Pattern B `AuthorSelect`/`AuthorSelectField`** (score
    13) — available; mirrors-comment self-evidence
  - AUTHOR-DATALIST-EXTEND-EDITORS-01 — UX-adjudication-
    required; opens whether to replace Pattern B with Pattern A
    at editor surfaces

### No new Lessons-Learned filing this session

The "inline functions inside large files are RCU candidates
the file-level scan misses" pattern is implicit Lessons-Learned
material. Per the "single instance is incident, not pattern"
discipline, filing deferred until the methodology gap recurs.
The audit footnote captures the gap + the grep recipe in-place.
