## Archived 2026-05-22 (RECURRING-COMPONENT-AUDIT-01 candidate #2 — `BulkActionBar` shell extraction via path γ pivot)

Single-commit RCU 3-site extraction shipped as `c2305e7`. Closes
candidate #2 from `docs/audits/recurring-component-audit-2026-05-21.md`.

### What shipped

New shared shell component at
`frontend/src/components/BulkActionBar.tsx` (~80 LOC) + matching
`BulkActionBar.module.css` (.bar + .count byte-identical rules
previously duplicated across the 3 adapter module.css files) +
`BulkActionBar.test.tsx` (5 Vitest cases pin: countLabel
rendering, ariaLabel pass-through, children slot between count +
Clear, onClear callback fires, custom testid namespacing).

The 3 sibling adapters now render
`<BulkActionBar>{site-specific actions}</BulkActionBar>`:

  - `frontend/src/components/articles/ArticleBulkActionBar.tsx`
  - `frontend/src/components/BookBulkActionBar.tsx`
  - `frontend/src/components/comments/CommentBulkActionBar.tsx`

Each adapter keeps its entity-specific action cluster (format
dropdown / mode toggle / AI dropdown / Convert button / Delete
menu — varies per surface). The 3 adapter `.module.css` files
slimmed to their site-specific rules only (label, select,
modeGroup, spacer, warning, error).

### Architecture decision: adapter-pattern vs direct-to-callers

The audit suggested "thin wrapper + children-slot for actions"
(path α). Implementation refined to adapter-pattern: each existing
adapter file stays as a thin specialized composition around the
new shell. Caller pages (ArticleList.tsx 1434 LOC, Dashboard.tsx,
CommentsAdminSection.tsx 1144 LOC) do NOT change — they still
import `ArticleBulkActionBar` / `BookBulkActionBar` /
`CommentBulkActionBar`. The adapter layer is the n-specialization
layer per the RCU canonical pattern (mirrors
LayoutConfigComicBubble + LayoutConfigComicPanel +
LayoutConfigSpeechBubble using Tier1Section without becoming
inline-renderers in their parent pages).

Inlining the per-entity action clusters into the 3 caller pages
would have compounded the inline-monolith pattern that the
"Inline-component duplication is the upstream cause of
parallel-surface asymmetry" Lessons-Learned guards against.

### Path γ pivot — candidate #1 deferral

Pre-Coding-Reality-Check on candidate #1 (`useSelection<T>()`,
score 16) surfaced an explicit anti-extraction rationale at
`useBookSelection.ts:7-10`: *"Kept as a separate hook (rather
than a generic `useSelection`) so that future per-entity
divergence (e.g. books-only constraints around audiobook job
state) lands in one place without a cross-entity refactor."*

The audit's `diff` correctly identified implementation-identity
but missed the documented design-intent in the doc-comment.
Honoring the rationale + pivoting to candidate #2 per the
user-confirmed γ path. Candidate #1 deferred-pending-design-
intent-adjudication; documented in audit footnote alongside a
methodology-gap note (future audits should grep for anti-
extraction-rationale markers as a soft anti-signal).

### Tests + baseline

  - tsc --noEmit clean
  - 4 BulkActionBar-scope test files green: 28/28 (5 new wrapper
    cases + 23 existing adapter cases preserved)
  - Full frontend Vitest: 1783 → 1792 (+9; +5 new BulkActionBar
    + 4 incidental from intervening commits)
  - Backend baseline unchanged (frontend-only work)

### Audit candidates remaining

  - #1 `useSelection<T>()` (score 16) — deferred-pending-design-
    intent-adjudication
  - #3 `ListRow` (score 13) — available for future session;
    benefits from extracting `ArticleRow` from `ArticleList.tsx`
    monolith as part of the work
  - #4 `AuthorSelectInput` (score 12) — available for future
    session; pairs with already-filed
    `AUTHOR-DATALIST-EXTEND-EDITORS-01` follow-up which plans 2
    additional callsites (ArticleEditor + BookEditor)

### No new Lessons-Learned filing this session

The "Audit-Score should include design-intent-documentation as
anti-extraction-signal" pattern from the candidate-#1 pivot is
implicit Lessons-Learned material but per the "single instance
is incident, not pattern" discipline (see
`.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md`), filing deferred until the
pattern recurs. The audit footnote captures the methodology gap
in-place.

Phase 2 of the 4-user-findings work. Closes Findings #1
(Panel-Image-Upload — schema-ready since Comics-Session-2 but no
UI surface) + #3 (LayoutConfigComicPanel — empty-state text in the
side-pane when a panel was selected). Bundled into one P2 ship
because both findings share the ComicBookEditor side-pane
integration point (lines 599-620 in the post-Phase-1 source);
LayoutConfigComicPanel hosts both the panel-config knobs AND the
image-upload affordance.

### Findings resolution

|---|---|---|

**All 4 user-findings closed.** Phase 3 EXTENDED-FEATURES-01
(BLOCKED-BY Phase 2 per the Phase 1 audit) is now unblocked.

### Half-Wired-Lifecycle closures (cumulative)

This Phase 2 ship closes ALL three half-wired surfaces that
Comics-Session-2 left latent on the comic-book editor:

1. **bubble-list endpoint** — closed Comics-Session-2 C7 (full editor
   wiring; not in 2026-05-21 archive).
2. **`assetUrls` map never populated** — closed by C4 of this Phase 2.
   `image_asset_id`-set panels now actually render their image in
   the editor body.
3. **panel_config schema-ready but no UI surface** — closed by C1+C2
   of this Phase 2. The panel's per-row Tier1Section config now has
   a writer.

### Architecture decision audit-trail

**Option A confirmed** (use Tier1Section AS-IS with all 8 fields):
the resume-prompt suggested a 4-field subset; user adjudicated for
full-8 because (a) Tier1Section is explicit RCU-designed (the
`testidPrefix` + `i18nKeyPrefix` props prove n-site intent), (b) all
8 fields are semantically reasonable for ComicPanel, (c)
Option B (subset prop) adds complexity without use-case evidence,
(d) Option C (new PanelVisualStyle.tsx) duplicates explicitly-
RCU-extracted code. Field-subset prop available as 1-commit polish
later if smoke surfaces "too overwhelming" UX feedback.

### Lessons-Learned (no new filings this session)

Applied (no new): "Recurring-Component Unification Rule"
(Tier1Section 3rd-site application), "Half-wired feature
lifecycle: a state-write without its inverse-mutation OR its
state-consumer is purgatory, not a feature" (C4 closure),
"Playwright-visible ≠ User-visible" (C6 bbox assertions),
"Pre-Coding-Reality-Check at the keystroke" (caught the
547-567 → 599-620 line-number drift in handover doc).

### Phase 3 trigger gate

EXTENDED-FEATURES-01 trigger fully met now:
- Findings #1-#4: all resolved
- Multi-panel base layouts: 7 templates shipped (Phase 1)
- LayoutConfigComicPanel: shipped (Phase 2)
- Image-upload affordance: shipped (Phase 2)

Phase 3's 17-23-commit polish scope (drag-to-position, snap, undo,
RTL, z-order, panel gutter, auto-tail-direction, full E2E matrix)
is now consumable as a multi-session arc when the user's
prioritization elevates it from P3 to P2.

## Archived 2026-05-20 (PLUGINFORGE-RECURSION-LIMIT-REGRESSION-01 close via pluginforge 0.8.0 bump — P1 tier now empty)

Closed by a single coordinated dependency bump in commit `3fe8633`.
pluginforge 0.8.0 ships the idempotency fix in `mount_plugin_routes`
that the P1 backlog item recommended as Path (a). The recursion-
limit baseline that Comics-Session-2 C2 introduced (originally
13 fail + 13 err per the filed audit; drifted to 1 fail by HEAD
`534bea9` before this work landed) is fully resolved: backend
pytest sweep now passes 2116/2116 (was 1 failed on a stale
`'1.0.0' == '1.1.0'` plugin-comics version assertion).

### Why P1 (the only one in the tier)

The 2026-05-20 backlog re-prioritization audit promoted this item
to P1 on architectural-debt grounds: it blocked any further
backend test-surface growth (Comics-Session-2 resumption + new
plugin endpoints + V060-style admin-route extensions). With it
closed, the P1 tier is now empty.

### Path (a) confirmed effective

The two alternative paths from the backlog body — (b) fresh-
FastAPI-app-per-TestClient fixture-level churn, (c)
`sys.setrecursionlimit(5000)` bandaid — are no longer needed.
The upstream library fix addresses the root cause cleanly:
pluginforge now checks `app.routes` for matching path+methods
before adding, so cross-test lifespan re-mounts don't accumulate
duplicate routes past the recursion ceiling.

### Coordinated 12-pyproject bump

Per the "Two installation paths" lessons-learned rule, the
backend's combined `poetry.lock` and each per-plugin
`poetry.lock` are independent verification gates. All 12
pyproject.toml files bumped from `^0.7.0` → `^0.8.0`, then:

- `cd backend && poetry lock && poetry install` (backend)
- `make lock-all-plugins` (11 plugin lockfiles)
- `make verify-plugin-locks` → OK, all 12 pairs in sync

### Stale test assertion fix bundled

`backend/tests/test_user_overlay_migration_lifespan.py:110`
asserted `body["version"] == "1.0.0"` for plugin-comics. Comics-
Session-2 commit `a33baf3` bumped the plugin to 1.1.0 but this
test wasn't updated. Pre-bump: this was the single failing test
(masking the recursion regression's actual disappearance). Post-
bump + assertion-fix: green.

### Deprecation warning surfaced (filed as follow-up)

pluginforge 0.8.0 logs a DeprecationWarning on plugin-export:
"Plugin 'export' returns 3 routers from get_routes(). The
recommended convention is one parent router that uses
router.include_router(...) to nest sub-routers. Multiple top-
level routers per plugin are supported in v0.8.0 and v0.9.0,
and may become an error in v0.10.0."

The Single-Router-Per-Plugin convention is already documented
in `.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md`. plugin-export was authored
before that convention. Refactor to single-parent-router-with-
nested-sub-routers tracked as
`PLUGIN-EXPORT-SINGLE-ROUTER-REFACTOR-01` (P3) in the active
backlog. Non-blocking through v0.9.0.

### Phase status after ship

| Item | Status |
|---|---|
| PLUGINFORGE-RECURSION-LIMIT-REGRESSION-01 | closed (this archive) |
| Backend pytest sweep | 2116/2116 (was 1 failed pre-bump) |
| P1 tier | EMPTY |
| pluginforge pin (all 12 pyproject) | `^0.8.0` |
| pluginforge installed | `0.8.0` |
| Plugin lockfiles | all 12 re-synced, verify-plugin-locks OK |
| Deprecation follow-up | `PLUGIN-EXPORT-SINGLE-ROUTER-REFACTOR-01` (P3) |

### Cross-references

- Backlog body originally proposed three fix paths; Path (a)
  shipped via upstream library version.
- `.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md` "Single-Router-Per-Plugin
  convention" — the documented rule that the new pluginforge
  deprecation enforces.
- `.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md` "Two installation paths"
  — the discipline that drove the 12-pyproject coordinated bump.
- pluginforge 0.8.0 release (PyPI, 2026-05-20).

## Archived 2026-05-20 (PLUGIN-COMICS-SESSION-3-PAGES-CRUD-01 close in 4 commits — Path A1 architectural relocation of pages router from plugin-kinderbuch to backend core + PageLayout enum extension + Half-Wired ComicBookEditor closure)

Shipped as `PLUGIN-COMICS-SESSION-3-PAGES-CRUD-01` (P1, Foundation-
Override-Extended: Half-Wired-Visible-in-Production). Four commits
`879df22..00a18f8` close the half-wired ComicBookEditor state that
told users to seed pages via direct SQL.

### Why P1 (Foundation-Override-Extended)

The 2026-05-20 backlog re-prioritization audit promoted this item
from P3 to P1 via the Half-Wired-Visible-in-Production criterion
(new lessons-learned rule filed in the same audit). Comic-book
authors who landed in ComicBookEditor in production saw a
"Noch keine Comic-Seiten" dashed-border message with prose
instructing them to seed pages via direct SQL — a user-visible
half-wired state, not an internal-only gap.

### Path A1 chosen over A2 (per Pre-Inspection adjudication)

Two paths were proposed in the Pre-Inspection audit:

- **A1**: move pages router from plugin-kinderbuch to backend
  core, relax gate. Cleaner architecture; 4 commits.
- **A2**: relax gate in-place in plugin-kinderbuch's pages.py.
  Minimal-diff; 3 commits.

User chose **A1** with rationale: Page model + Page schemas
already lived in core; the router was a v1-historical artefact
from when picture_book was the only Page-using book_type. Single-
Source-of-Truth + Recurring-Component-Unification both point at
"core CRUD belongs in core, not in a plugin."

### Q2 + Q3 adjudication

- **Q2** (PageLayout enum strategy): option (b) — add
  ``comic_panel_grid`` literal to the existing PageLayout
  ``Literal[...]``. Honest schema-evolution; future book types
  (graphic-novel, illustrated-text) extend the same enum without
  architectural friction. Route-level cross-validation between
  layout + book_type explicitly deferred (accept-as-degenerate-
  case): the route accepts any PageLayout for any pageable
  book_type; frontend pickers filter per book_type.
- **Q3** (empty-state UX): option (b) — "Create first comic
  page" action button. Mirrors PageEditor's empty-state pattern;
  avoids Books-endpoint auto-create-on-creation coupling.

### Commits

- **C1 — `879df22`** refactor(pages): move pages-CRUD router
  from plugin-kinderbuch to backend core (no behavior change).
  Zero behavior delta — gate still `book_type == "picture_book"`;
  C2 relaxed it. Plugin-kinderbuch's `get_routes()` now returns
  ONE router (marginally reduces per-lifespan ASGI registration
  accumulation tracked by PLUGINFORGE-RECURSION-LIMIT-REGRESSION).
  Tests: backend test_pages_routes 41/41, adjacent 88/88,
  kinderbuch self-tests 8/8.
- **C2 — `0cb64cc`** feat(pages): accept comic_book in pages-CRUD
  gate + add comic_panel_grid layout. Three-part atomic-green
  commit: (1) PageLayout enum extension at schemas + frontend
  type union + two exhaustive `Record<PageLayout, …>` consumers
  (LayoutPicker + PageCanvas); (2) gate relaxation in core
  pages.py (helper renamed `_get_picture_book_or_400` →
  `_get_pageable_book_or_400`, frozenset constant
  `PAGEABLE_BOOK_TYPES`); (3) inverted obsolete tests + new
  `TestComicBookPagesCRUD` class with 9 positive cases covering
  list, create (with + without layout_config), patch, delete-
  with-shift, reorder, plus 2 cross-validation pins documenting
  accept-as-degenerate-case decision. Tests: test_pages_routes
  41→50, adjacent 88/88, tsc clean, Vitest 179/179.
- **C3 — `00a18f8`** feat(comic-book-editor): create first-page
  button closes Half-Wired empty state. ComicBookEditor's empty
  state replaces SQL-instruction message with a `btn-primary`
  action button (testid `comic-book-editor-create-first-page`)
  calling `api.pages.create(bookId, {layout: "comic_panel_grid"})`
  + refreshing pages list. New `refreshPages` helper +
  `handleCreateFirstPage` callback. 8 i18n catalogs updated
  (DE real-umlaut: "Erstelle deine erste Comic-Seite, um Panels
  und Sprechblasen zu platzieren." + button "Erste Comic-Seite
  erstellen"). Vitest 179→191 (+12 ComicBookEditor cases:
  empty-state-with-button + click-creates + error-surface).
  Closure-flag mock pattern per documented React-18-strict-mode
  + mockImplementationOnce lesson.
- **C4 — _this commit_** docs(backlog): close PAGES-CRUD-01 +
  archive entry. Backlog entry removed (lines 177-209); header
  Last-Updated updated; archive section added; Playwright smoke
  `comic-book-editor.spec.ts` updated to assert the action
  button + a new test that clicks → creates → page nav appears
  (replaces the obsolete "degraded no-pages" assertion).

### Phase status after ship

| Item | Status |
|---|---|
| PLUGIN-COMICS-SESSION-3-PAGES-CRUD-01 | closed (this archive) |
| ComicBookEditor Half-Wired-State | closed |
| pages-CRUD architectural location | core (was plugin) |
| PageLayout enum | extended with `comic_panel_grid` (6 entries) |

| i18n catalogs | 8 catalogs updated (DE real-umlaut; EN canonical; 6 passthrough-EN); new `create_first_page` key |

### Lessons-learned reaffirmations

- **Half-Wired-Lifecycle-Closure** (existing): closed the
  state-write-without-state-consumer family — Session 2 shipped
  the ComicBookEditor that READS `pages.list` but had no surface
  to WRITE the first row.
- **Recurring-Component-Unification** (existing): empty-state
  action-button pattern mirrored from PageEditor, not invented
  fresh.
- **React-18-strict-mode + mockImplementationOnce** (existing):
  applied the closure-flag pattern instead of fragile
  per-call mock-ordering for the click-creates-page Vitest case.
- **Pre-Coding-Reality-Check** (existing): exhaustive
  `Record<PageLayout, string>` consumers (LayoutPicker +
  PageCanvas) caught BEFORE the enum extension via grep, not
  AFTER via tsc failure.

  - "Articles-vs-Books parallel-surface asymmetry" (the
    asymmetry-prevention pattern that this rule applied at a
    different scale)

  (the half-wired surface that this work closes was shipped
  there).

atomic-green-per-commit-delta discipline; the

Commit chain (origin/main):

| # | Commit | Scope |

### Closed backlog entries

#### `PLUGINFORGE-V070-ADOPTION-01` (was P1) — PluginForge v0.7.0 identity adoption

Shipped via commits 2 + 3. All 12 first-party plugins declare
`target_application="bibliogon"`. Host `app_id="bibliogon"` at
the single `PluginManager(...)` site. Smoke probe: 12/12
activate, 0 errors (any severity), 0 `wrong_application` filters.
Bibliogon-side v0.8.0 readiness: ✓.

#### `PLUGINFORGE-V060-ADOPTION-01` (was P2) — PluginForge v0.6.0 lifecycle adoption

Shipped via commits 4-9. Five consumer changes:

- 3 private-state pokes (`manager._app_config = merged` × 3) →
  `manager.refresh_config()` public API. Quiet bug-fix: the
  poke silently did NOT propagate the new config to each
  plugin's `self.app_config`; refresh_config does.
- `_log_plugin_diagnostics_pre/_post` (~80 LOC hand-correlated)
  → single `DiscoveryResult` consumer with severity filtering.
- `min_app_version` β2 migration (YAML → class attribute on
  ComicsPlugin + KinderbuchPlugin).
- `POST /api/admin/rediscover` endpoint (subsumes Surface A of
  PLUGIN-DEV-SERVER-RESTART-HELPER-01).
- PluginCard status-column UI consuming
  `PluginError.user_facing_message` via the extended
  `/api/settings/plugins/discovered` endpoint.

#### `PLUGIN-FILTERREASON-I18N-MAP-01` (was P3) — FilterReason i18n surface

Shipped via commit 8 (V060 C5). 80 i18n string slots (9
FilterReason values + 1 identity-deprecation-warning, × 8
languages). PluginCard renders the localized status badge for
non-activated plugins; `pre_activate_rejected` maps to
`license_check_failed` per Bibliogon's application-specific
semantic.

#### `PLUGIN-REDISCOVER-INTEGRATION-TEST-01` (was P3) — rediscover real-world test

Shipped via commit 9 (V060 C6). 5 scenarios in
`backend/tests/test_plugin_rediscover_integration.py`:

1. `rediscover_stable_no_diff_after_lifespan` — baseline
2. `rediscover_picks_up_newly_added_dist_info` — the
   real-world cache-invalidation test PluginForge unit tests
   cannot cover
3. `rediscover_respects_not_enabled_filter` — enabled-list
   honored
4. `rediscover_filters_wrong_target_application` — v0.7.0
   identity gating
5. `rediscover_is_idempotent` — invariant

### Updated backlog entries

#### `PLUGIN-DEV-SERVER-RESTART-HELPER-01` (still P4 — Surface B only)

Surface A (make dev dev-server stale) is now **CLOSED** by
`POST /api/admin/rediscover` (commit `b62c339`). Surface B
(Docker prod image staleness) is structurally different — the
image's venv lacks the new plugin entirely; even cache

### Lessons-learned formalization

Three Plan-vs-Reality / Pre-Coding-Reality-Check instances in
one session (PDF-KDP-FORMATS-01 half-wired surface +
V060 C4 install/uninstall wiring inapplicability + V060 C5
endpoint-duplication risk) crossed the recurrence threshold for
formalization. New entry "Pre-Coding-Reality-Check: re-audit at
the keystroke, not just the audit" in
[`.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md`](../../.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md).
Rule fires AT keystroke time before writing the first line of
code for a committed-plan step; 30-60 seconds of re-grep catches
audit blind spots.

### Closed backlog entry

#### `PICTURE-BOOK-PDF-BLEED-MARKS-01` — KDP 0.125in bleed + crop marks

Originally filed P3 from the Session 6 PDF-export audit's D4
finding (2026-05-17). Trigger fired on user request — "proceed
with PDF-BLEED-MARKS-01" — without waiting for a KDP rejection or
Aster's print-shop-quality demand.

Architectural decisions:

- **Q1 shared component + dual surface**. PictureBookPdfExportControls
  mounted at both PageEditor header AND BookMetadataEditor Design
  tab. Recurring-Component-Unification Rule canonical 2-site
  extract-plus-migrate (per coding-standards.md). Half-wired
  surface from PDF-KDP-FORMATS-01 closed as explicit side-effect.
- **Q2 marks-only ship**. Emit `@page { bleed: 3mm; marks: crop; }`
  but DO NOT extend background paint into the bleed area in this
  session. If real print-shop demand surfaces, file
  `PICTURE-BOOK-PDF-BLEED-EXTENSION-01` as follow-up.
- **Q3 Producer metadata `(bleed)` suffix**. Extends the existing
  Producer line — no new metadata pipeline wiring. Downstream
  tools (KDP, print shops, archivers) detect via standard PDF
  metadata inspection.
- **Q4 filename suffix**: format-first-then-bleed nominal grouping.
  - default + bleed=false → `<slug>.pdf` (back-compat)
  - default + bleed=true → `<slug>-bleed.pdf`
  - non-default + bleed=false → `<slug>-<format>.pdf`
  - non-default + bleed=true → `<slug>-<format>-bleed.pdf`
- **Q5 default bleed=false**. Ship-stable; no behavior change for
  existing exports.
- **Q6 uniform 0.125in (3mm)** across all 5 KDP picture-book
  formats. NO per-format override.
- **Q7 localStorage key** `bibliogon-picture-book-bleed-marks`,
  matching the format key's namespace exactly.

Anti-speculation boundary preserved:

- NO `Book.pdf_bleed_marks` column (future Settings field if per-
  book defaults become real).
- NO per-format bleed override (uniform spec stays safe).
- NO background-extends-into-bleed (Q2 marks-only deferred).
- NO EPUB-for-picture-books (separate filing if needed).

Cross-references:

- `docs/audits/session-6-pdf-export-audit-2026-05-17.md` (D4
  finding that filed this item)
- `60ff913` / `c96a1fc` / `b6eaf2c` (PDF-KDP-FORMATS-01 precedent
  with the half-wired surface this session closed)
- `.claude/rules/coding-standards.md` Recurring-Component
  Unification Rule (2-surfaces threshold canonical application)
- WeasyPrint 66.0 `@page { marks; bleed }` CSS Paged Media spec
  support (verified locally + via the C1 integration tests
  parametric over all 5 formats × bleed=true)

### Test counts shipped

### Half-wired surface closure (PDF-KDP-FORMATS-01 follow-up)

The Pre-Inspection for this item surfaced a half-wired surface
left behind by PDF-KDP-FORMATS-01: `BookMetadataEditor` Design-
tab Export-PDF button (`metadata-export-picture-pdf` testid)
called `api.documentExport.download(book.id, "pdf", new
URLSearchParams())` with EMPTY params — ignoring the format
dropdown selection that lived only in PageEditor.

C2's shared-component extraction closed this gap. Both surfaces
now use the same `PictureBookPdfExportControls` component; format
+ bleed selection persists via localStorage to both sites. The
Playwright spec at C4 explicitly asserts the dual-surface
state-sync.

This is the Recurring-Component-Unification Rule's "canonical
2-site extract-plus-migrate" pattern from coding-standards.md.
2 surfaces existed; component-extraction landed in the SAME
coordinated session that added the new feature.

## Archived 2026-05-19 (PICTURE-BOOK-PDF-KDP-FORMATS-01 close in 3 commits)

Fourth named member of the Phase 4 close trigger gate closed.
Picture-book PDF export now supports the full set of canonical KDP
trim sizes; the 8.5x8.5 square MVP from v0.35.0 stays as the
default-on-read for back-compat.

Three-commit atomic-green session:

| # | Commit | Scope |
|---|---|---|
| C1 | `60ff913` | Backend: `PICTURE_BOOK_FORMATS` constant (5 entries) + `_resolve_picture_book_format` (default-on-read gamma-shim) + `_format_css` (CSS-variable-driven `@page` + `--content-h`) + `generate_picture_book_pdf` / `_build_html` / route handler all accept `picture_book_format` kwarg + filename-suffix policy (non-default formats append `-<format>`). Static `_BASE_CSS` `.page { height }` rewired to `var(--content-h)`. +26 plugin pytest + 11 backend integration tests |
| C2 | `c96a1fc` | Frontend: `<select>` dropdown next to Export-PDF in PageEditor; localStorage persistence (`bibliogon-picture-book-format`, matching the existing `bibliogon-theme` namespace); defensive `readStoredFormat` + try/catch around `localStorage.setItem` (privacy-mode browsers degrade to React-state only). Default-format export sends empty query params (preserves the back-compat filename). +8 Vitest cases |
| C3 | (this commit) | i18n × 8 catalogs (6 keys × 8 = 48 entries: `pdf_format_label` + 5 `pdf_format.<id>` entries) + Playwright E2E smoke (12th test in `picture-book-editor.spec.ts`; covers dropdown selection + localStorage round-trip + filename suffix on download + back-to-default empty-suffix verification) + backlog close-and-archive |

### Closed backlog entry

#### `PICTURE-BOOK-PDF-KDP-FORMATS-01` — multi-format picture-book PDF export

Originally filed P3 from the Session 6 PDF-export audit's D3 finding
(2026-05-17). Trigger fired on user request — "continue with
PDF-KDP-FORMATS-01" — without waiting for a real KDP rejection or
second-picture-book demand signal.

Key architectural decisions:

- **Q1 inches-tuple format-ID naming** (`8.5x8.5` / `8x10` / `8.5x11`
  / `11x8.5` / `10x8`). Self-describing, decoupled from KDP marketing
  rename risk, no translation burden for the ID itself.
- **Q2 default-on-read contract** for missing / null / empty /
  unknown `picture_book_format` → `8.5x8.5`. Same gamma-shim pattern
  as `bubbles[0]` precedence from `4421f02` (4c-B-2 C1). Preserves
  MVP UX exactly for API consumers that don't update.
- **Q4 uniform 0.5in margin** across all 5 formats. KDP-safe;
  per-format tuning deferred until a real rejection surfaces.
- **Q5 CSS-variable-driven `@page` sizing**. Python emits `:root
  { --page-w / --page-h / --content-h }`; static CSS uses
  `var(--content-h)` for `.page` height. Keeps Python ↔ CSS
  coupling loose; matches Bibliogon's theming-token pattern.
- **Q6 localStorage persistence** for the dropdown selection
  (browser-scoped, NOT per-book). Survives reloads; tiny scope
  addition for substantial author-iteration UX win. Privacy-mode
  browsers degrade gracefully.
- **Q7 filename suffix** only when non-default: `<slug>.pdf` for
  8.5x8.5 (back-compat); `<slug>-<format>.pdf` for non-default.
  Disambiguates author exports of multiple formats per book.

Anti-speculation boundary preserved:

- NO `Book.pdf_format` column (future Settings field, deferred until
  per-book defaults become a real authoring pain).
- NO per-format margin tuning (uniform 0.5in stays the safe default).
- NO EPUB-for-picture-books — the 410-message in `routes.py` was
  corrected to reflect this; EPUB needs its own filing if requested.
- NO bleed marks (PDF-BLEED-MARKS-01 is its own item; the last
  remaining named Phase 4 picture-book-scope gate).

Cross-references:

- `docs/audits/session-6-pdf-export-audit-2026-05-17.md` (D3 finding
  that filed this item)
- `4421f02` (gamma-shim default-on-read precedent from 4c-B-2 C1)
- `frontend/src/components/PageEditor.tsx` (dropdown wiring +
  localStorage namespace conforming to `bibliogon-theme` pattern)

## Archived 2026-05-19 (PADDING-FONT-STYLE-01 close + EXTENDED-SHAPE-01 close-as-superseded)

Trimmed-scope follow-up to 4c-B-2. Adds the two non-comic-coupled
properties from the original EXTENDED-SHAPE-01 spec (padding +
font_style); defers shape-variants (oval / rectangle / cloud /
explosion) to plugin-comics scope where they architecturally belong
per the NQ1 commitment in
[docs/explorations/comic-foundation.md](../explorations/comic-foundation.md).

Three-commit atomic-green session:

| # | Commit | Scope |
|---|---|---|
| C1 | `0782209` | Uniform padding slider under `bubbles[0].padding` (0-32 px, default 12 = mean of legacy 10/14 asymmetric CSS-module rule). UI + render + PDF + Vitest + pytest. +4 Vitest + 3 PageCanvas render + 6 pytest cases |
| C2 | `fa2fc33` | Italic toggle under `bubbles[0].italic` (boolean per Q4; not enum). UI + render + PDF + CSS-module inherit override + Vitest + pytest. +5 Vitest + 2 PageCanvas render + 5 pytest cases |
| C3 | (this commit) | i18n × 8 catalogs (2 new keys × 8 = 16 entries) + Playwright E2E smoke (11th test in `picture-book-editor.spec.ts`) + backlog close-and-archive (this entry) |

### Closed backlog entries

#### `PADDING-FONT-STYLE-01` — padding + font_style trimmed scope

Filed mid-session as the trimmed scope of EXTENDED-SHAPE-01 (Tier 3
extended-properties). Two new per-bubble fields under
`layout_config.bubbles[0]`:

- **`padding`** (slider 0-32 px, default 12). Q3 decision: uniform,
  not per-side. Per-side deferred without backlog filing —
  anti-speculation per coding-standards.md "Don't add abstractions
  beyond what the task requires".
- **`italic`** (boolean, default false). Q4 decision: boolean,
  not enum. Maps to CSS `font-style: italic | normal`. Oblique
  variant deferred without backlog filing.

Q5 decision: padding lands in Tier 1 Visual Style (box-model
property); italic lands in Tier 2 Typography. No Tier 3 section.

TipTap risk audit: zero. speech_bubble is Tier-Property layout =
plain-text storage, NOT TipTap. Italic toggle scoped to
`layout_config.bubbles[0].italic`; TipTap layouts use a different
config component entirely.

#### `PICTURE-BOOK-SPEECH-BUBBLE-EXTENDED-SHAPE-01` — closed-as-superseded

Original Tier 3 scope: shape variants + tail configuration +
padding + font_style. Three sub-scopes already migrated:

- **Tail configuration** → `PICTURE-BOOK-SPEECH-BUBBLE-TAIL-01`
  (promoted out 2026-05-19 / Finding E).
- **Padding + font_style** → `PADDING-FONT-STYLE-01` (this session).
- **Shape variants** (oval / rectangle / cloud / explosion) →
  `PLUGIN-COMICS-FOUNDATION-SCAFFOLDING-01` Session 2 (bubble_type
  variants speech / thought / narration / shout / whisper /
  sound_effect — `comic-foundation.md:286-294` + `comic-foundation.md:321-324`).

Pre-Inspection finding that drove the close-as-superseded:
shape variants are bubble-type semantics; bubble-type semantics
belong to plugin-comics per NQ1 ("Comic-Foundation is plugin-comics
work, NOT a Picture-Book extension"). Shipping shape variants in
picture-book scope first would have:

1. Violated `comic-foundation.md:335` ("None of these belong in
   Picture-Book's scope").
2. Triggered the Recurring-Component-Unification half-migration
   risk (same axis my earlier session's Track-B audit identified
   for TAIL-01: 1st surface = picture-book single bubble with 4
   shape variants; 2nd surface = plugin-comics multi-bubble with 6
   bubble_type variants; Session 2 forced into extract-plus-migrate
   work that should have been native).
3. Produced data-shape churn: picture-book `shape: "oval"|...` vs
   plugin-comics `bubble_type: "speech"|...` are parallel taxonomies
   for the same visual concept, not composable.

Archive-as-superseded precedent: matches the 2026-05-18 close
pattern for `PICTURE-BOOK-MULTI-BUBBLE-PER-PAGE-01` (P3) +
`PICTURE-BOOK-SPEECH-BUBBLE-DRAG-POSITION-01` (P5), both closed-as-
superseded in picture-book scope and absorbed into
`PLUGIN-COMICS-FOUNDATION-SCAFFOLDING-01`.

NO new backlog item filed for shape-variants — already covered by
the existing PLUGIN-COMICS Session 2 scope; double-filing prevented
per the C3 stop-condition.

## Archived 2026-05-19 (PICTURE-BOOK-SPEECH-BUBBLE-EXTENDED-PROPERTIES-01 - 4c-B-2 close in 6 commits)

Phase 4 Tier-Property work shipped. Eleven per-bubble properties land
under the new ``layout_config.bubbles[0]`` wrapper shape (NQ2
scope-anticipate decision from
[docs/explorations/comic-foundation.md](../explorations/comic-foundation.md));
plugin-comics Session 2 inherits the same per-bubble shape via the
``comic_bubbles`` schema without migration coordination.

Six-commit atomic-green session:

| # | Commit | Scope |
|---|---|---|
| C1 | `4421f02` | bubbles[0] wrapper-shape read-path shim (Q1 gamma decision: Inclusive-on-write, flat-fallback-on-read) + types. 19 new regression-pin tests across 3 surfaces (TS, Python, frontend component) |
| C2 | `e5ac3bf` | Tier 1 Visual Style (6 fields): background_color + border_color + border_width + border_style + border_radius + shadow + shadow_intensity. Radix Collapsible "Visueller Stil" section (closed by default). +11 Vitest + 6 PageCanvas render + 9 pytest |
| C3 | `149ad35` | Tier 2 Typography (5 fields): font_family (reuses v0.35.0 5-font OFL catalog per Q4) + font_size + font_weight + text_color + text_align. Radix Collapsible "Typografie" section. +10 Vitest + 6 PageCanvas render + 10 pytest. CSS-module inherit overrides for textarea cascade |
| C4 | `9f0a4c4` | i18n × 8 catalogs (DE / EN / ES / FR / EL / PT / TR / JA): 23 keys per catalog = 184 entries. German uses real umlauts (Schriftgröße / Schattenintensität) |
| C5 | `93f7e72` | E2E + PageEditor merge-logic tests: 2 Vitest cases pinning handleUpdateLayoutConfig + writeBubble + legacy-flat-to-bubbles[0] promotion. 1 Playwright smoke covering Tier 1 + Tier 2 reload-persistence round-trip |
| C6 | (this commit) | Backlog close + archive |

### Closed backlog entry

#### `PICTURE-BOOK-SPEECH-BUBBLE-EXTENDED-PROPERTIES-01` — Tier 1 + Tier 2 visual + typography properties

Originally filed P3; closed by the 6-commit 4c-B-2 session described
above.

Scope shipped:
- **Tier 1 — Visual Style** (6 fields): `background_color` (default
  `#ffffff`), `border_color` (`#000000`), `border_width` (0-8 px,
  default 2), `border_style` (solid/dashed/dotted/none, default
  solid), `border_radius` (0-50 %, default 50), `shadow` (toggle,
  default on) + `shadow_intensity` (0-10, default 5). Q3 (a)
  decision: intensity slider disabled when shadow is off but stays
  visible with preserved value.
- **Tier 2 — Typography** (5 fields): `font_family` (5-font OFL
  catalog from v0.35.0; default Atkinson Hyperlegible), `font_size`
  (10-32 pt, default 14), `font_weight` (normal/bold, default
  normal), `text_color` (default `#000000`), `text_align`
  (left/center/right, default center).

Key architectural decisions:
- **Q1 gamma (Inclusive-on-write, flat-fallback-on-read).** Per-
  bubble fields stored under `layout_config.bubbles[0]`. Read-path:
  `bubbles[0].X || flat X || default`. Write-path: always writes
  to `bubbles[0]`. Flat keys fade naturally (same template as
  `size → bubble_width` from `c63db21`). NO Alembic migration —
  JSON-encoded Text column accepts any shape.
- **Q2 (no speculative CollapsibleSection extraction).** Radix
  Collapsible used inline. `<CollapsibleSection>` extraction is
  deferred to `PICTURE-BOOK-TEXT-CONFIGURATION-01` (canonical 2nd
  surface per Recurring-Component-Unification Rule).
- **Q4 (5-font OFL catalog reused verbatim).** `PICTURE_BOOK_FONTS`
  from `src/data/picture-book-fonts.ts` powers the Tier 2 font
  family dropdown. Already battle-tested by the v0.35.0 PDF embed
  pipeline.
- **Q5 (per-bubble defaults only).** No per-book default story to
  avoid Half-Wired-Lifecycle risk.
- **Q6 (native color picker).** `<input type="color">` for all
  three color fields.

Cross-references:
- Comic-Foundation NQ2 scope-anticipate decision:
  [docs/explorations/comic-foundation.md](../explorations/comic-foundation.md)
  lines 104-115
- Comic-Bubbles schema parity reference: comic-foundation.md
  lines 282-294 (`bubble_config (json) -- per-bubble Tier-Properties`)
- c63db21: canonical wrapper-shim template (size → bubble_width)

Test counts shipped:
- 1637 / 1637 Vitest passing (was 1600 before C1)
- 122 / 122 plugin-export pytest passing (was 88 before)
- 75 / 75 backend i18n pytest passing
- 52 / 52 backend pages/PDF pytest passing
- 1 new Playwright smoke (covered by C5; Aster runs)

This is the first named member of Phase 4 close. Remaining Phase 4
open items per the trigger gate: `EXTENDED-SHAPE-01`,
`PDF-KDP-FORMATS-01`, `PDF-BLEED-MARKS-01`, optional `TAIL-01`.

## Archived 2026-05-19 (Medium-Import async-progress family close-out)

Three backlog items closed in the 2026-05-17/18/19 work-stream that
shipped the Medium-import v2 dry-run preview + async-progress UI +
TS-interface sync + two smoke-driven gap-fixes. All four user-
facing surfaces (preview table, SSE-driven progress, run-in-
background badge, persisted result panel) live on `origin/main`
and are part of the v0.35.0 release bundle.

Origin commits (chronological):

| Phase | Commit | Scope |
|---|---|---|
| V2 Phase 1 — Backend | `e5ef73d` | preview + selection endpoints + cache lifecycle (+26 tests) |
| V2 Phase 2 — API client | `6acf1a0` | TS types + 3 mediumImport methods (+10 tests) |
| V2 Phase 3 — UI | `7b29fa4` | PreviewTable component + state-machine (+11 tests) |
| V2 Phase 4 — i18n+E2E | `d4f9b4c` | 8 catalogs + 3-test Playwright smoke |
| Async Phase 1 — Backend | `fa0369e` | async endpoint, SSE events, cooperative cancel, +14 tests |
| Async Phase 2 — Frontend | `c380cc2` | MediumImportJobContext + API methods + progress UI + state-machine swap (+22 tests) |
| Async Phase 3 — Playwright | `8595053` | 4-test smoke extension |
| Response-Interface-Sync | `cb7edc5` | TS interface comment fields + Result-UI comment sections (+4 tests, 8 catalogs) |
| Smoke gap-fix #1 | `ce6b85e` | Run-in-background badge (MediumImportGate) + Go-to-comments link (+8 tests, 8 catalogs) |
| Smoke gap-fix #2 | `a7c53ff` | Remount-during-importing renders progress UI even when local preview state empty (+1 test, 2 keys × 8) |
| Smoke gap-fix #3 | `3c53054` | Result persistence across navigation (move to context) + active-content reordered above Settings + Upload (+3 tests, 1 reframed) |

### Closed backlog entries

#### `MEDIUM-IMPORT-V2-01` — dry-run preview UI

Filed P2; closed by V2 Phases 1-4 + the three follow-up gap-fixes.
Per-post table with checkboxes for deselection, native i18n across
8 catalogs, cross-layer Playwright pin. Cache-lifecycle backend
(30-min TTL + on-success reap + explicit cancel endpoint) sits
under `plugins/bibliogon-plugin-medium-import/bibliogon_medium_import/preview.py`.

#### `ASYNC-IMPORT-PROGRESS-01` — server-side progress with SSE

Filed P2; closed by Async Phases 1-3 + the three smoke gap-fixes.
Replaces the indeterminate spinner with per-post progress events
streamed via the existing generic `/api/export/jobs/{id}/stream`
endpoint (reused per the Pre-Inspection Q2 decision; the endpoint
is misnamed but generic over `job_store`). Worker uses
`await asyncio.sleep(0)` between posts for cooperative
cancellation. New `MediumImportJobContext` mirrors the
AudiobookJobContext pattern (SSE listener in context, not in
modal/page; localStorage F5-recovery; per-event-type state
machine). Run-in-background badge component
(`MediumImportGate`) mounted at App root next to
AudioExportGate. Per Q1 of Pre-Inspection: only the v2 path went
async; the v1 endpoint stays synchronous for back-compat with
direct curl / scripts / the 46 existing test paths.

#### `MEDIUM-IMPORT-RESPONSE-INTERFACE-SYNC-01` — TS-interface drift

Filed P3 during the V2 Phase 1 Pre-Inspection; closed by `cb7edc5`.
The `MediumImportResponse` TypeScript interface was missing four
comment-routing fields the backend has been emitting since v0.31.0
(`imported_comments_count`, `skipped_comments_count`,
`imported_comments[]`, `skipped_comments[]`). Drift surfaced
because the v0.31.0 work shipped backend-side without a paired
frontend audit. Now mirrors the backend `ImportZipResponse`
Pydantic shape; `MediumImportResult.tsx` renders the two extra
counts + per-comment collapsible sections (gated on > 0 so
plain-article archives don't see them).

### Smoke-driven gap-fixes (filed + closed in the same session)

Three bugs surfaced by the user's manual smoke on the shipped work
and closed inside the same session, NOT filed as separate backlog
items because each rolled up immediately:

1. **Missing "Run in background" button** — fixed by `ce6b85e`
   (new `MediumImportGate` component matches the audiobook pattern).
2. **Missing "Go to comments" button** — fixed by `ce6b85e`
   (sibling of "Go to articles" in the result panel, gated on
   `imported_comments_count > 0`, links to `/settings?tab=comments`).
3. **Remount loses progress UI** — fixed by `a7c53ff` (changed
   page's render gate from `{preview && inPreview}` to
   `{(preview || isImporting) && inPreview}` so the importing
   section renders even when local `preview` state was wiped on
   navigate-away; two-state heading reflects the with-preview vs
   without-preview paths).
4. **Browser-back loses result panel + result hidden below scroll**
   — fixed by `3c53054`. Two root causes: result was local
   `useState` (dies on unmount) AND JSX put active-content after
   Settings + Upload cards. Moved result to context-backed
   `job.result`; stopped page's watcher from calling `job.clear()`
   on completion (only `handleReset` clears now); MediumImportGate
   auto-dismiss reworked to hide-badge-only (badgeDismissed flag,
   doesn't touch job state); JSX reordered so active content
   (preview/importing + result panel) is topmost.

### Lessons-learned candidates surfaced

Two patterns worth a separate hygiene-doc touch on the next
docs-only commit:

1. **Shared-working-tree commit bundling**. Twice during this work
   the parallel session's commits absorbed my staged-but-uncommitted
   YAML edits — first in `bd2b878` (their Export-PDF i18n commit
   bundled my async-progress keys), then again in `7aa108f` (their
   TipTap toolbar commit bundled my in-progress-card keys). Both
   functionally correct, both commit-message-vs-content mismatched.
   Mitigation pattern I used throughout my own commits:
   `git commit -- <specific paths>` to scope the commit to exactly
   my files. The parallel session didn't use this pattern.

2. **Page-local state vs context-backed state across navigation**.
   The remount-loses-progress and browser-back-loses-result bugs
   shared the same root cause: `useState` in a page component
   dies on unmount. Any feature where state must survive
   navigation needs context-backing OR localStorage rehydration.
   The `MediumImportJobContext` is the canonical exemplar after
   this work — it persists `result` indefinitely (not just job
   lifecycle state) so post-import navigation works correctly.

### Test surface delta across the whole stream

- Backend: +14 tests (medium-import async + result endpoint + 3
  result-endpoint pins)
- Plugin: +11 tests (preview cache lifecycle + selection
  plumbing + progress_callback emission + cooperative cancel)
- Frontend Vitest: +47 tests across 6 files (PreviewTable +
  page state-machine + context + progress UI + result-panel
  comment sections + gate badge)
- Playwright: 4-test medium-import-preview smoke
- i18n: ~80 new keys across 8 catalogs (preview namespace +
  async-progress namespace + gate namespace + comment-routing
  namespace + smoke-fix namespaces)

### Documents shipped

- `docs/journal/manual-smoke-2026-05-19-medium-import-async.md` —
  6-flow per-step smoke gate (commit `0c93a65`)
- `docs/journal/session-handoff-2026-05-18-v0.35.0-release-cut-sequence.md` —
  4-stream v0.35.0 sequence under the parallel session's revision
  (commit `d763a99`; subsequently revised by parallel session to
  move AUTHOR-SELECT + RECURRING-COMPONENT POST-release)

## Archived 2026-05-18 (EDITOR-FULLSCREEN-NATIVE-01 - 7-commit fullscreen rollout)

Browser-native Fullscreen API affordance shipped to all 5
editor surfaces in 7 commits. Shipped in parallel with
USER-OVERLAY-Migration-Session backend work + the Backups-tab
relocation; zero cross-session conflicts (frontend hook scope,
backend overlay scope, settings-tab scope all disjoint).

Origin commits (chronological):

| Phase | Commit | Scope |
|---|---|---|
| C1 - Hook | `630202c` | useFullscreenToggle hook + 7 Vitest cases (mocked Fullscreen API in happy-dom) |
| C2 - Editor.tsx Toolbar | `625c115` | Covers ArticleEditor + BookEditor via shared Editor.tsx + Toolbar (2 user-facing surfaces in 1 integration point); Ctrl+Shift+F via existing useKeyboardShortcuts hook |
| C3 - PageEditor | `519017f` | Picture-Book per-page editor header button |
| C4 - ComicBookEditor | `685e4cc` | plugin-comics Session 1 placeholder gets the button (Session 2 inherits when the placeholder is replaced) |
| C5 - i18n | `a68f054` | ui.toolbar.fullscreen + exit_fullscreen in all 8 catalogs |
| C6 - E2E | `8798b5f` | Playwright smoke for the 3 integration points (testid + aria-keyshortcuts assertions; Fullscreen API state-change assertion intentionally NOT made in headless mode per the spec comment) |
| C7 - Archive + P4 filing | (this commit) | Archive + FULLSCREEN-PATTERN-RECONCILE-01 (P4) per F3 decision |

### Pre-Inspection findings

7-track Pre-Inspection produced 4 spec-vs-reality decisions
that the user confirmed:

- **F1 (F11 handler reading)**: Reading A confirmed - F11
  stays browser-default (intercepting it is unreliable across
  browsers); Ctrl+Shift+F is the JS-controlled secondary path
  + toolbar button covers the click path. aria-keyshortcuts
  declares both.
- **F2 (fullscreen target)**: documentElement (whole window)
  confirmed - matches the filing's "entire window" language.
  Element-level was the alternative, rejected.
- **F3 (EnhancedTextarea coexistence)**: leave the existing
  state-CSS pattern as-is, file FULLSCREEN-PATTERN-RECONCILE-
  01 (P4) for future reconcile when a 3rd surface emerges.
- **F4 (aria-keyshortcuts text)**: "F11 Control+Shift+F" per
  W3C ARIA syntax.

### Architecture-rule alignments

- **Recurring-Component-Unification**: 5 surfaces x same
  handler -> extract `useFullscreenToggle` first, apply to all
  surfaces in SAME session (per the 2-surfaces threshold). All
  5 surfaces land in C2-C4; no half-migration.
- **Half-Wired-Lifecycle Prevention**: every surface that
  exposes the button also wires the underlying API call AND
  the keyboard shortcut. No write-without-consumer; no
  consumer-without-write.
- **Single-Source-of-Truth**: fullscreen state is read from
  document.fullscreenElement (browser-managed); the hook's
  React state is a derived view kept in sync via the
  fullscreenchange listener. Two independent toggle clicks
  on different surfaces would still converge to the same
  state because the browser is the SSoT.
- **Audit-First**: Pre-Inspection done before code; 4
  user-decisions surfaced; 2 reading-A-vs-B branches resolved.

### Cross-session coordination

- USER-OVERLAY-Migration-Session shipped C2 + C3 (d00948b,
  170a715) between EDITOR-FULLSCREEN C3 and C5. No file
  overlap (backend overlay + lifespan vs frontend hook +
  editors).
- About-Session idle during the rollout.
- plugin-comics Session 1 shipped before this stream started;
  C4 touched ComicBookEditor.tsx (their placeholder) safely.

### In-stream production bug-fix sidecar

C5 -> C6 transition flagged a `make stop` blocker the user hit
mid-session. Fix landed as `1c15d82` (separate commit, not
part of the 7-commit sequence): two distinct Makefile bugs
(self-killing `pkill -f` pattern + dev target that never saved
its uvicorn PID). Real orphan PID 14917 cleaned up live before
the user's next `make dev`.

### Follow-up filed

``FULLSCREEN-PATTERN-RECONCILE-01`` (P4) - tracks the future
reconcile between this stream's Browser-Fullscreen-API pattern
and EnhancedTextarea's existing state-CSS pattern. Defer
reason: zero current pain; both patterns work correctly in
their contexts (whole-window for editor surfaces vs in-dialog
expand for textareas).

## Archived 2026-05-18 (USER-OVERLAY-PLUGIN-ENABLE-MIGRATION-01 closed in 4 commits)

Closes the silent feature-invisibility class identified during
plugin-comics Session 1 smoke (2026-05-18): a stale user-overlay's
``plugins.enabled`` list silently filtered out newly-shipped plugins
because ``deep_merge`` treats lists as REPLACE. Result was 404 on
``/api/comics/info`` for every upgrading user despite green pytest.

Chosen option: **B** — startup-time migration helper that appends
project-tree plugins missing from the user-overlay's enabled list,
respecting any ``plugins.disabled`` opt-out. Preserves the
"lists replace" merge rule globally; migration LIVES BESIDE the
merge, not instead of it.

Origin commits (chronological):

- `edb7e28` — feat(config-overlay): migration helper +
  9 pytest cases + extended regression-pin (Part 1: replace +
  Part 2: migration effect).
- `d00948b` — feat(main): wire migration into lifespan +
  4 integration pytest cases (TestClient + manager-state
  assertions for the FastAPI-route-mount-stickiness limitation).
- `<C3>` — this archival + lessons-learned rule.
- `<C4>` — live-dev E2E smoke (sister to PLUGIN-COMICS-E2E-SMOKE-01).

Affected files at close-out: ``backend/app/config_overlay.py``,
``backend/app/main.py``, ``backend/tests/test_config_overlay.py``,
``backend/tests/test_user_overlay_migration_lifespan.py``,
``e2e/smoke/user-overlay-migration.spec.ts``,
``.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md`` (new rule).

Mechanism + contract pinned at three test tiers:
- **Unit**: ``test_migrate_*`` (9 cases) — pure function semantics.
- **Integration**: ``test_user_overlay_migration_lifespan.py``
  (4 cases) — end-to-end via TestClient + lifespan.
- **E2E smoke**: live dev server + curl assertion.

Backlog header: 63 active P2..P5 → 62 (P2: 2 → 1).

Pairs with: 2 sibling backlog items filed today around the same
operational class — ``PLUGIN-DEV-SERVER-RESTART-HELPER-01`` (P4,
covers Surface A `make dev` stale-process + Surface B Docker
prod image staleness) and ``PLUGIN-COMICS-E2E-SMOKE-01`` (P4,
the precedent this commit's C4 follows).

### PICTURE-BOOK-MULTI-BUBBLE-PER-PAGE-01 (P3)

Was: support multiple speech-bubbles per page in picture-book.
Schema change `layout_config.speech_bubbles[]` array within
the existing `speech_bubble` PageLayout.

**Closed by:** Comic-Foundation reframe (2026-05-18).
Multi-bubble work migrated to plugin-comics architecture.
Picture-Book stays single-bubble. Plugin-comics ships its
own `comic_bubbles` table + panel hierarchy; the JSON-array-
within-picture-book approach is rejected per the existing
`comic_book` reservation.

Original strategic note (now superseded) framed this as the
architectural anchor of a "Comic-Foundation Session" within
picture-book scope. CC's pre-audit critique (2026-05-18)
surfaced the conflict with the `comic_book` schema
reservation; the reframe moves the work to plugin-comics.

Successor: `PLUGIN-COMICS-FOUNDATION-SCAFFOLDING-01` (P3,
active backlog).

### PICTURE-BOOK-SPEECH-BUBBLE-DRAG-POSITION-01 (P5)

Was: pointer-drag handle on the picture-book speech-bubble
for free-form positioning beyond the 9 anchor presets.

**Closed by:** Comic-Foundation reframe (2026-05-18).
Drag-to-position belongs to plugin-comics' bubble-system
work (Session 3 of the plugin-comics roadmap). Picture-book
keeps the 9-preset anchor grid + width/height/opacity
sliders shipped in v0.35.1; if picture-book users hit the
preset ceiling, the request gets re-evaluated against
plugin-comics scope (the bubble visual primitive ships in
plugin-comics regardless).

Successor: `PLUGIN-COMICS-FOUNDATION-SCAFFOLDING-01`
(Session 3 in the roadmap).

## Archived 2026-05-18 (KDP-CATEGORIES-CATALOG-SYNC-01 + 2 dead-property cleanups)

Single-commit fix shipped in parallel with plugin-comics Session 1.
Pre-Inspection surfaced a 3-axis drift broader than the backlog
description, but contained within the KDP plugin scope so the
"single-commit fix" constraint held.

### `KDP-CATEGORIES-CATALOG-SYNC-01` — drift collapse to a code SSoT

Filed P3 (IMPROVEMENT). Originally framed as a 2-axis drift
(``plugins/bibliogon-plugin-kdp/config/kdp.yaml`` 26 entries vs.
``routes.py`` 10-entry hardcoded subset).

Pre-Inspection found a 3rd axis: the canonical runtime YAML at
``backend/config/plugins/kdp.yaml`` (the file PluginForge actually
loads per the "Plugin settings YAML lives in
``backend/config/plugins/``" lessons-learned rule) carried no
``categories`` block at all. So the plugin manifest's
``_settings.get("categories", [])`` reached an empty dict at
runtime, while the endpoint shipped 10 entries. Three sources,
three different answers.

**Resolution:** ``KDP_CATEGORIES`` module-level constant in
``plugins/bibliogon-plugin-kdp/bibliogon_kdp/routes.py`` is the
single source of truth, paralleling the existing
``KDP_COVER_REQUIREMENTS`` (also code-side because Amazon dictates
the values, not the user — same 2026-04-11 audit precedent). The
endpoint + the plugin manifest both read from it. The bundled
``plugins/bibliogon-plugin-kdp/config/kdp.yaml`` was stripped of
its drifted ``settings:`` block; only ``plugin:`` metadata
remains. The canonical YAML at ``backend/config/plugins/kdp.yaml``
was already correct (no categories block) and is unchanged.

**Boy-scout cleanup in the same commit:** the
``cover_requirements`` + ``manuscript_requirements`` ``@property``
helpers on ``KdpPlugin`` were also removed. Both read from
``_settings.get("cover"/"manuscript", {})``, both returned ``{}``
at runtime since the 2026-04-11 audit removed those YAML blocks
from canonical, both had zero consumers. They were left over
from the audit and walked the same drift line as the categories.

**Boy-scout cleanup in the same commit:** stale JSDoc on
``frontend/src/components/CategoryInput.tsx`` referenced an
``api.kdp.listCategories()`` method that did not exist in the
API client. Replaced with a pointer to the legitimate wire-up
follow-up filed below.

**Regression-pin palette** (in
``backend/tests/test_plugin_routes.py::TestKdpCategories``):

- ``test_kdp_categories_returns_full_26_catalog`` — pins the
  exact catalog size + 6 pre-fix-subset entries that must stay
  + 6 drift-restored entries that the pre-fix subset was
  missing (Cookbooks, Education & Teaching, Religion &
  Spirituality, Travel, Teen & Young Adult, Reference).
- ``test_kdp_plugin_manifest_categories_match_routes`` — pins
  that ``KdpPlugin.get_frontend_manifest()["categories"] ==
  GET /api/kdp/categories``. The two sources cannot drift
  silently again.

**Closed by:** single commit on 2026-05-18 (post-v0.35.1).

**Follow-up filed:** ``KDP-CATEGORIES-WIRE-TO-CATEGORYINPUT-01``
(P5) tracks wiring the live endpoint into the
``CategoryInput`` ``suggestions`` prop so authors get
autocomplete from the canonical KDP catalog. Pure feature work,
not drift-cleanup.

## Archived 2026-05-15 (v0.32.0 cycle close-out + UX-Full-Audit + Bug-A retrospective)

Retrospective close-out for three overlapping streams of work that
landed between v0.31.0 (2026-05-13) and v0.32.0 (2026-05-14). The
individual commits + CHANGELOG entries are already in the repo;
this is the cycle-level catalog so future bisect / "what shipped
in this window?" queries resolve in one place.

### v0.32.0 Phase B-F cycle

The v0.32.0 release shipped as a five-phase user-facing-improvement
batch. Phase labels (B / C / D / E / F) come from the planning
workspace; the repo carries them in commit messages + CHANGELOG
entries as `F1` / `F2a` / `F2b` / `F2c` / `F3`. Mapping for the
record:

- **Phase B — BulkActionBar selection cleanup** (commits `02553fb`
  + `926decb`). Single-item destructive handlers
  (soft-delete, permanent-delete, restore from trash) now call
  `selection.remove(id)` after the API call succeeds and before
  the success notification, so the bulk-action-bar count never
  references an orphan id. 14 Vitest hook tests pin the behaviour
  for both `useArticleSelection` and `useBookSelection`; positive
  E2E regression-pin added in a follow-up commit.

- **Phase C — Heuristic v2 for Medium comments** (`95c72c8`,
  CHANGELOG `F2a`). Two-tier comment-detection. Tier 1 is
  v0.31.0's strict 500-char gate; tier 2 fires on
  conversational markers (second-person address / question mark
  in first or last paragraph) within a 2000-char body that has
  no article-shape disqualifiers (no headings / code / images).
  Data-validated: v0.31.0 caught 8/8 detectable comments; v0.32.0
  catches 11/11, with 0 new false positives on the 209-file
  production corpus. Audit at
  `docs/audits/medium-comment-heuristic-2026-05-14.md`.

- **Phase D — Reciprocal Article ⇄ Comment reclassify
  endpoints** (`3288ba5`, CHANGELOG `F2b`). Two new endpoints
  perform transactional moves: source row deleted in the same
  commit as destination row inserted, atomicity guaranteed.
  `POST /api/articles/{id}/reclassify-as-comment` +
  `POST /api/comments/{id}/reclassify-as-article`. Comment ->
  Article path auto-derives the new article title from the
  first 200 chars of body (word-boundary trim + "..." truncation;
  fallback "Reclassified comment" on empty body). When the
  comment had a non-`"manual"` `imported_from` AND a
  `canonical_url`, a paired `ArticleImportSource` row preserves
  provenance through the move. 14 integration tests including
  an Article -> Comment -> Article round-trip that proves
  `body_json` survives two moves intact.

- **Phase E — UI reclassify actions** (`bb4a820`, CHANGELOG
  `F2c`). Two surfaces: ArticleEditor header kebab menu "Move
  to comments" (with confirm dialog spelling out lossy fields)
  + Settings -> Comments admin per-row "Move to articles"
  button. Both use the simple confirm dialog (not the heavier
  `TypeToConfirmDialog`) because the move is reversible via
  the reciprocal direction.

- **Phase F — Toolbar Copy split-button** (`3cedf78`, CHANGELOG
  `F3`). Primary click copies the article / chapter body as
  Markdown; chevron disclosure exposes "Copy as plain text".
  Both modes prepend the document title (+ optional subtitle).
  TipTap-to-Markdown converter extracted from `Editor.tsx`
  into a shared `utils/tiptap-markdown.ts` so the same code
  powers the existing WYSIWYG ↔ Markdown toggle and the new
  Copy action. 27 converter tests + 7 toolbar tests + a
  `copy-toolbar.spec.ts` E2E that pins the primary path and
  the chevron menu's two items.

### UX-Full-Audit 2026-05-14/15 close-out

The 2026-05-14 UX-Full-Audit produced 4 groups (G1-G4) of
findings against the Bibliogon UI; the 2026-05-15 sweep closed
the actionable backlog. Three discrete archive sessions already
landed earlier today:

- **MEDIUM-IMPORT-TESTIDS + SETTINGS-TABS + SETTINGS-TOPBAR**
  (commit `3ba6f13`, archived above). Three mechanical testid
  additions, batched as one commit because all were "S-effort,
  same UX-audit origin".

- **LOADING-INDICATOR-EXTRACT-01** (commit `78cd863`, archived
  above). Shared `<LoadingIndicator>` component + global
  `.spin` class, per the EMPTYSTATE-EXTRACT-01 template.

- **BOOKEDITOR-EMPTY-STATE-01** (commit `12c21e7`, archived
  above). Empty-state surface for the BookEditor matching the
  ArticleEditor pattern.

Remaining UX-Full-Audit findings are open as trigger-gated P3 /
P5 backlog items:

- `COMMENTS-ADMIN-PAGINATION-01` (P3) — waits for first
  >200-comments user OR Settings sluggishness complaint.
- `PLUGIN-SETTINGS-TESTID-COVERAGE-01` (deferred; the Settings
  monolith inline-component extraction has compounding parity
  value but no concrete trigger yet).
- `ARTICLEFILTERBAR-EXTRACT-01` (deferred; same shape as
  the Settings monolith — extraction is the prerequisite for
  Articles ↔ Books filter-bar parity).
- `THEME-TOKEN-COMPLETENESS-AUDIT-01` (filed as quarterly
  pre-release hygiene; 111 var(--token, #fallback) callsites
  in scope, token-vs-palette cross-check not yet performed).

Articles-vs-Books parity matrix
(`docs/audits/ux-full-audit-2026-05-14.md`) is the canonical
record: 13 features compared, 3 confirmed asymmetries
documented + 2 historical resolutions noted.

### Bug A close-out: workbox "broken" was a perception-lag UX bug

2026-05-14 user report: "Articles-Trash Restore button is
broken; workbox blocks the request". Investigation chain:

1. SW config audit — single `urlPattern: /^\/api\//` registered
   for GET only. Every non-GET API call triggers
   `No route found for: <url>` as informational pass-through
   (not blocking).
2. Manual smoke — restore POST fires, backend processes
   correctly, DB confirms article restored.
3. Real cause — `[Violation] 'click' handler took 419ms`
   browser violation log. Restore worked correctly; the
   handler chains two network roundtrips (`POST .../restore`
   + `GET /articles`) with synchronous `setTrash` + `setArticles`
   state updates in between. 419ms registers as "slow + no
   clear success signal" because the user stays in the
   trash view, a transient toast fires, and the restored row
   vanishes from the filtered list.

Outcome: no code change, two artefacts.

- **`RESTORE-UX-FEEDBACK-01`** (P3 IMPROVEMENT) filed in
  `docs/backlog.md` for the optimistic-update + clearer
  post-restore feedback redesign. Trigger: second user report
  with the same "feels broken" framing.
- **Lessons-learned promotion**: rule
  "Workbox 'No route found' is benign info, not a bug
  indicator" added at the bottom of
  `.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md` so the next investigation
  doesn't conflate the SW log with a functional break. Pair
  rule "User-perceived bug ≠ code bug: the perception-lag
  class" promotes the broader pattern (verify against
  Network tab + backend state BEFORE patching).

This is the third occurrence in the 2026-05 cycle of
"investigation surfaces a non-bug as the real signal" (the
prior two: D2 verification audit + Multi-tool collaboration
re-sync). Pattern is mature enough that the lessons-learned
section now carries three related rules + a meta-rule on
authoritative-source verification.

### Cross-references

- v0.32.0 CHANGELOG entry: `docs/CHANGELOG.md` (line ~7).
- UX-Full-Audit findings: `docs/audits/ux-full-audit-2026-05-14.md`.
- Pre-release verification: `docs/audits/pre-release-{verification,coverage,ux}-2026-05-12.md`
  (D-prefixed findings landed in v0.31.0 / v0.32.0 release windows).

## Archived 2026-05-15 (MEDIUM-IMPORT + SETTINGS-TABS + SETTINGS-TOPBAR testids)

commit (`3ba6f13`). All three were mechanical testid
additions on existing elements; batching saves
commit-message-overhead.

### MEDIUM-IMPORT-TESTIDS-01

Filed by UX-Full-Audit 2026-05-15 (G2-F6). Added testids to
the result-table count spans in `MediumImportResult.tsx`:
- `medium-import-result-imported-count`
- `medium-import-result-skipped-count`
- `medium-import-result-errored-count`

E2E specs can now make stable assertions like
`getByTestId("medium-import-result-imported-count").toContainText("N
Artikel importiert")`. The audit's mention of
`medium-import-file` was already satisfied by the existing
`medium-import-upload-input` testid in `MediumImportUploadZone.tsx`.

### SETTINGS-TABS-TESTID-COMPLETE-01

Filed by UX-Full-Audit 2026-05-15 (G3-F3). 3 of 7 Settings
tab triggers (app, author, plugins) lacked `testId` in the
`tabDefs` array. Added the three; all 7 tabs now have
testIds. Tightened the array type from `testId?: string` to
`testId: string` and removed the now-dead
`settings-tab-${value}-mobile` fallback in the mobile
DropdownMenu (the fallback's output was already identical to
the explicit-testId convention so no E2E spec breaks).

### SETTINGS-TOPBAR-TESTIDS-01

Filed by UX-Full-Audit 2026-05-15 (G3-F6). The 2 top-bar
buttons in Settings (back-arrow + Home-icon) lacked testids
AND identifying text — keyboard-nav focus passed over
nameless icon buttons.

  existing i18n key — no new translations needed).
- `settings-nav-home` on the Home button + explicit
  `aria-label` (previously had `title` but no `aria-label`).

Accessibility side benefit: both buttons now announce a
role-appropriate label to screen readers.

## Archived 2026-05-15 (LOADING-INDICATOR-EXTRACT-01)

### LOADING-INDICATOR-EXTRACT-01 — shared LoadingIndicator + global .spin

Filed 2026-05-15 by UX-Full-Audit 2026-05-15 (G4-F2) as
P3 IMPROVEMENT. Audit pointed to the EMPTYSTATE-EXTRACT-01
pattern as the template. Closed in commit `78cd863`.

The audit identified 24 ad-hoc loading state vars per-component
with inconsistent visual treatment. Closer survey also found
the `.spin` class referenced 8+ times but only locally defined
twice (the other 6+ rendered unstyled icons — silent
fall-through bug).

Two fixes shipped together:

- **Global `.spin` + `@keyframes spin`** in `global.css`.
  Closes the silent-fall-through. Removes two redundant local
  `<style>{@keyframes spin...}</style>` declarations in
  `DetectingStep.tsx` + `ExecutingStep.tsx`.
- **Shared `<LoadingIndicator>` component**: ~70 LOC.
  API: `<LoadingIndicator label? variant? size? testId? className? />`.
  `inline` (default) or `block` variant. `role="status"` +
  `aria-busy="true"` + `aria-live="polite"` for screen
  readers. Uses lucide `Loader2` + the now-global `.spin`.

Migrated 7 full-pane callsites in this commit (audit said
"incrementally"):

- `BookEditor.tsx` × 2 (book loading + chapter content loading)
- `Dashboard.tsx` (book list loading)
- `QualityTab.tsx` (metrics loading)
- `ChapterVersionsModal.tsx` (versions loading)
- `HelpPanel.tsx` (content loading)
- `BookMetadataEditor.tsx` (audiobook section loading)
- `CommentsAdminSection.tsx` (comments admin loading)

Folded in: `BookEditor.tsx` not-found state's hardcoded "Buch
nicht gefunden." routed through `t("ui.editor.book_not_found",
"Buch nicht gefunden.")` — the catalog entry itself is
deferred (fallback text matches the previous hardcoded prose
so behaviour is identical until catalogs are updated). Sets up
for a paired i18n cleanup commit if needed.

Regression-pin: 8 new Vitest specs in `LoadingIndicator.test.tsx`
covering spinner-only, +string label, +JSX label, aria-busy +
role=status, inline vs block variant root classes, custom size,
missing-testId defensive, className merge. Frontend total:
1010 → 1018.

Future contributors: use the component for loading UX. Remaining
13 callsites (mostly button-label-swap pattern like
`{saving ? "Laden..." : "Save"}`) migrate as their files are
touched in future work — that pattern is lower payoff than
the standalone-paragraph fixes covered here.

Tests: full suite green (backend 1698 passed (1 skipped),
frontend 1018 passed). All 3 audit hooks pass.

Cross-references:

- Same shape as EMPTYSTATE-EXTRACT-01 (also closed today). The
  two extractions together close the audit's "no shared
  UX-pattern components" cluster (EmptyState + LoadingIndicator
  were both filed by the same audit pass).

## Archived 2026-05-15 (BOOKEDITOR-EMPTY-STATE-01)

### BOOKEDITOR-EMPTY-STATE-01 — EmptyState UX for 0-chapter books

Filed 2026-05-15 by UX-Full-Audit 2026-05-15 (G1-F2) as
P3 IMPROVEMENT. Closed in commit `164f860`.

The audit's claim "BookEditor has no empty-state UX" was
inaccurate — there WAS an empty state, just visually
overwhelming (21 chapter-type buttons in 3 groups for a user
who just wants to start writing). The proper fix was a
redesign, not new wiring.

What changed:

- `BookEditor.tsx`: replaced the `noChapter` div (intro + grid
  of 21 chapter-type buttons in 3 groups) with the shared
  `<EmptyState>` component (shipped earlier today in
  EMPTYSTATE-EXTRACT-01). Single primary "Neues Kapitel" CTA
  invokes `handleAddChapter("chapter")` — the default chapter
  type for "I just want to start writing." Body text hints
  that other types live in the sidebar dropdown.
- ChapterSidebar's `chapter-add-trigger` +
  `chapter-add-dropdown` already exposes all 21 ChapterTypes;
  the deleted grid was fully redundant. No functionality lost.

Testid contract:

- `book-editor-empty-state` (wrapper) → preserved.
- `book-editor-add-chapter-chapter` (primary CTA) → preserved.
- Dropped (orphan): the 20 non-primary
  `book-editor-add-chapter-{type}` testids, the 3 group
  containers `book-editor-{front-matter,chapter,back-matter}-group`,
  and `book-editor-empty-state-text`. None were referenced by
  any spec; they were added in BOOKEDITOR-TESTIDS-01 earlier
  today to document the dense grid before this redesign
  removed it.

Fold-in i18n cleanup: the previous intro paragraph
"Erstelle dein erstes Kapitel, um zu beginnen." was hardcoded
German prose with no `t()` call. Added `ui.editor.empty_title`
and `ui.editor.empty_hint` to all 8 catalogs (DE, EN, ES, FR,
EL, PT, TR, JA) with native translations. Closes a
pre-existing i18n-coverage gap that predated this work.

Tests: full suite green (backend 1698 passed (1 skipped),
frontend 1010 passed). All 3 audit hooks pass.

Cross-references:

- Depended on EMPTYSTATE-EXTRACT-01 (also closed today). The
  shared `<EmptyState>` component made this fix a one-liner.
- Pair-closes with BOOKEDITOR-TESTIDS-01 (closed today): same
  audit found both findings on the same surface; the testids
  were added first to document the existing UX, then this
  redesign removed most of them.

## Archived 2026-05-15 (EMPTYSTATE-EXTRACT-01)

### EMPTYSTATE-EXTRACT-01 — extract shared `<EmptyState>` component

Filed 2026-05-15 by UX-Full-Audit 2026-05-15 (G1-F3) as
P3 IMPROVEMENT. Closed in commit `1d80c18`.

The audit named 4 ad-hoc empty-state implementations
(Dashboard, ArticleList, CoverUpload, HelpPanel). Closer
survey found **6** instances — HelpPanel turned out to have
no empty-state UX (audit was off by one). All 6 migrated.

What landed:

- `frontend/src/components/EmptyState.tsx` (66 LOC) +
  `EmptyState.module.css` (29 LOC). API:
  `<EmptyState icon? title? body? actions? testId? className? />`.
  Title/body each accept string (default `<p>` wrap) or JSX
  (caller controls heading level + classes). Actions render as
  flex row with gap; each button keeps its own testid.
- 6 migrations:
  - `Dashboard.tsx` trash-empty-state (icon + title)
  - `Dashboard.tsx` dashboard-empty-state (icon + title + body +
    3 CTAs) — per-action testids added as a fold-in
    (`dashboard-empty-create-book`, `dashboard-empty-import`,
    `dashboard-empty-get-started`)
  - `Dashboard.tsx` filter-empty-state (icon + title + body +
    1 CTA)
  - `ArticleList.tsx` article-list-empty (icon + title + body +
    2 CTAs); inline `EmptyState` function renamed to
    `ArticleListEmptyState` to avoid shadowing the shared
    component
  - `ArticleList.tsx` article-list-filter-empty (icon + body +
    1 CTA, no title)
  - `CoverUpload.tsx` empty-state (icon + body only); inline
    `EmptyState` function renamed to `CoverEmptyState`

Testid contract preserved: every existing testid value still
resolves to the same DOM element. No E2E or Vitest spec
needed to change.

Regression-pin: 10 new Vitest specs in `EmptyState.test.tsx`
covering icon-only, +title, +body, +actions, JSX-title bypass,
JSX-body bypass, className merge, missing-testid defensive
case, empty-string title omission. Frontend total: 1000 → 1010.

Full suite green (backend 1698 passed (1 skipped), frontend
1010 passed). All 3 audit hooks pass.

Unlocks `BOOKEDITOR-EMPTY-STATE-01` (still in backlog): with
the shared component now available, that item becomes "replace
BookEditor's dense 21-chapter-type-grid with a cleaner
EmptyState block + primary 'Add your first chapter' CTA."

## Archived 2026-05-15 (TEST-ISOLATION-MODULE-STATE-01)

### TEST-ISOLATION-MODULE-STATE-01 — module-state audit + drift gate

Filed by the 2026-05-14 CI-hygiene session after the
``platform_schema`` regression broke 5 ``test_publications.py``
tests via cross-file LRU cache poisoning. P3 IMPROVEMENT.
Closed 2026-05-15 in commit `c5488b6`.

Audit findings (codebase is current, gate is the deliverable):

- **1** `@lru_cache` decorator in `backend/app/`:
  `platform_schema.load_platform_schemas`. Already fixed via
  bidirectional `cache_clear()` autouse fixture in
  `test_platform_schema.py` (2026-05-14). Now allowlisted in
  the audit script with the verified audit note.
- **0** `@cached_property` in `backend/app/`.
- **0** `@functools.cache` in `backend/app/`.
- **1** module-level mutable runtime container in
  `backend/app/services/`: `_locks` in `git_sync_lock.py`.
  Safe-by-design — per-book UUIDs prevent cross-test
  collision; the file docstring already documents
  "intentionally never delete entries" as a deliberate choice.
  No fix needed; no allowlist entry needed (no decorator
  involved).
- All other module-level container assignments in `services/`
  + `routers/` are literal constants populated at import time;
  no test monkeypatches their input.

Drift prevention shipped:

- `scripts/audit_module_state.py` inventories every
  `@lru_cache` / `@cache` / `@functools.lru_cache` /
  `@cached_property` decorator in `backend/app/`. Cross-checks
  against an in-script `ALLOWLIST` of audited entries.
  `--enforce` exits 1 on any unallowlisted decorator;
  `--quiet` skips the totals summary.
- New pre-commit hook `module-state-audit` runs
  `--enforce --quiet` on every commit touching
  `backend/app/**/*.py`. Verified Passed on the full repo.
- Each `ALLOWLIST` entry carries a per-entry audit note
  explaining the cache's lifetime + the test fixture (if any)
  that handles the bidirectional clear. Adding a new entry is
  the **human verification step** — the script enforces "if
  it's not in the list, the contributor hasn't done the
  verification."

Bug-class status:

The "Module-level caches survive test boundaries" pattern
documented in `.claude/rules/lessons-learned.md` previously
relied on contributor awareness + post-incident audit cadence.
With this gate, any future `@lru_cache` added to `backend/app/`
fails the pre-commit hook until it's been added to the
allowlist with an audit note. The bug class moves from
"recurring per-incident" to "gated at commit time."

Tests: full suite green (backend 1698 passed (1 skipped),
frontend 1000 passed). All four shipped pre-commit hooks
(notify-error-apierror-coverage, theme-token-completeness,
module-state-audit, plus the existing six) pass.

Cross-references:

- Mirrors the gate-by-tooling shape of today's earlier
  `audit_notify_error_calls.py` and `audit_theme_tokens.py`.
  All three are drift-prevention scripts shipped this week
  that turn recurring bug-classes into commit-time blocks.

## Archived 2026-05-15 (VIEW-MODE-TESTID-PARITY-01)

### VIEW-MODE-TESTID-PARITY-01 — view-agnostic id attributes on books + articles

Filed 2026-05-15 by UX-Full-Audit 2026-05-15 (G2-F2) as
P3 IMPROVEMENT and CORRECTNESS-CLASS (not just hygiene — the
audit confirmed during the walkthrough that E2E specs silently
skipped when the wrong view-mode was persisted). Closed in
commit `2689fe5`.

What landed:

- `BookCard.tsx`: `data-book-id={book.id}` added alongside the
  existing `book-card-${id}` testid.
- `BookListView.tsx`: `data-book-id={book.id}` added alongside
  the existing `book-list-row-${id}` testid.
- `ArticleCard.tsx`: `data-article-id={article.id}` added
  alongside the existing `article-card-${id}` testid.
- `ArticleRow` (in `ArticleList.tsx`): `data-article-id={article.id}`
  added alongside the existing `article-list-row-${id}` testid.
- New E2E regression-pin spec
  `e2e/smoke/view-mode-testid-parity.spec.ts` (2 tests): toggles
  grid ↔ list on both surfaces and asserts the same
  `[data-{book,article}-id="X"]` selector finds exactly one
  match in each mode.

Design decision: separate semantic attribute name
(`data-book-id` / `data-article-id`) rather than a second
`data-testid` value. HTML doesn't allow two `data-testid`
attributes on one element, and Playwright's `getByTestId`
matches by exact value. The semantic-attribute approach gives
the cleanest selector without ambiguity AND doubles as an
explicit "this is a book/article wrapper" hint for future
contributors.

Pattern-class significance: this closes a CORRECTNESS class
where the wrong view-mode caused tests to silently skip
rather than fail. The new selector pattern is mode-agnostic
by design; future regressions in either wrapper's attribute
fail the parity spec loudly.

Tests: full suite green (backend 1698 passed (1 skipped),
frontend 1000 passed). Pre-commit hooks pass.

---

## Archived 2026-05-15 (BOOKEDITOR-TESTIDS-01)

### BOOKEDITOR-TESTIDS-01 — add data-testid coverage to BookEditor.tsx

  38). Mirrors the `article-editor-{role}` convention as
  `book-editor-{role}`.
- Coverage scoped to in-page roles only: layout / loading /
  not-found state / sidebar wrapper / mobile sidebar toggle /
  empty-state cluster.
- Empty-state cluster: the no-chapter view's intro paragraph
  (`book-editor-empty-state-text`), the three button groups
  (`book-editor-{front-matter,chapter,back-matter}-group`),
  and 21 per-ChapterType buttons
  (`book-editor-add-chapter-{type}`).

- **Chapter sidebar root, chapter list items, kebab menu,
  version-history modal trigger** → live in `ChapterSidebar.tsx`

  `Editor.tsx`, separately covered by that component's testid
  surface.

  `onMetadata` prop callback; the button itself is in

The "38 vs 0" parity comparison from the audit was misleading:
BookEditor delegates most of its surface to child components
(ChapterSidebar + Editor + BookMetadataEditor) whereas

have testids?" — closed for BookEditor.tsx itself with this
commit.

existing + future Playwright specs.

  partially verifiable via `book-editor-empty-state` — but the

  outdated; the no-chapter pane DOES render an empty-state

  may now be "audit finding is stale; close as already-met"
  rather than a new implementation. Leaving the item open for
