## Archived 2026-05-07

### v0.29.0 release — audit P1 cleanup + toolchain modernization

Released v0.29.0 (commit `4a48263`, tag `v0.29.0`). Hygiene
release; no user-facing behavior change. The five P1 audit
findings flagged at HEAD `5671cde` against the documented
frontend coding standards in `code-hygiene.md` and
`architecture.md` are all closed in this release:

- **3 confirm() -> AppDialog**: `SshKeySection` overwrite-confirm
  and delete-confirm, plus `GitBackupDialog` accept-local
  force-push confirm. All use the `"danger"` variant via the
  `useDialog` hook.
- **2 bare fetch -> api.ai.testConnection()**: `AiSetupWizard`
  step-3 connection test and `Settings` AI tab connection test
  both consume the new typed `api.ai.testConnection()` namespace
  method, satisfying the architecture rule "API calls ONLY
  through `frontend/src/api/client.ts`". The new method type is
  `AiTestConnectionResult { success, error_key, error_detail }`,
  matching the existing backend route at
  `backend/app/ai/routes.py:370` (route unchanged).

Three new title keys (`ui.ssh.confirm_overwrite_title`,
`ui.ssh.confirm_delete_title`, `ui.git.confirm_accept_local_title`)
added to all 8 i18n YAMLs (de/en/es/fr/el/pt/tr/ja). DE uses
real umlauts.

Toolchain alignment (P2 audit follow-up that the mechanical
cleanup commit explicitly deferred): `@types/node` ^22 -> ^24
to match `engines.node >=24.0.0` and the CI runtime; cascaded
into `tsconfig.json` `target` + `lib` ES2020 -> ES2022 because
`@types/node@24` correctly stops polyfilling
`Array.prototype.at()` and other ES2022 stdlib globals. Zero
call-site changes required; pattern captured in
`lessons-learned.md` for future `@types/node` major bumps.

Mechanical hygiene cleanup bundled in: README `Current version`
line `v0.26.6` -> `v0.28.0` (missed at v0.27.0 + v0.28.0 release
commits); inline `// any:` justifications added to two TipTap
command callbacks in `StyleCheckExtension.ts`;
`GetStarted.module.css` `.indicatorDone` `#fff` ->
`var(--text-inverse)`; `docs/backlog.md` last-updated note
tightened (DEP-09 + SEC-01 archived in `93a5ed3`, no longer
"awaiting next-release archive"); Maintenance / hygiene section
gained a pointer to `.claude/prompts/audit.md` per the
`ai-workflow.md` "Test coverage audits — When to run" rhythm.

Tests: backend 1298 unchanged; frontend 707 -> 712 (+5: four
`api.ai.testConnection` cases + one `AiSetupWizard` `onError`-path
assertion); launcher unchanged at 165; smoke Playwright 191/191
(one flake in `keywords-editor` retried clean — unrelated to
v0.29.0 changes; `addKeyword` timing under load).

Pre-tag chain green: `make test`, `tsc --noEmit`, `vitest`,
`playwright --project=smoke` (after flake retry), `ruff check`,
`mypy app/`, `pre-commit run --all-files`,
`pyinstaller bibliogon-launcher.spec --clean --noconfirm`. Tag
created with `git tag -a v0.29.0`. GitHub release published at
https://github.com/astrapi69/bibliogon/releases/tag/v0.29.0
with the per-release notes file at
`changelog/releases/v0.29.0.md`.

No corresponding ROADMAP / backlog item closures: the audit P1
cleanup was a direct sweep, not tracked as a backlog ID. DEP-09
and SEC-01 were already archived 2026-05-06 (Vite 8 upgrade
shipped post-tag of v0.28.0 on main; v0.29.0 is the first
tagged release that includes them).

## Archived 2026-05-06

### DEP-09 — Vite 7 -> 8 upgrade

Frontend bumped to Vite 8.0.10 + vite-plugin-pwa 1.3.0 + vitest
4.1.5 + @vitest/coverage-v8 4.1.5. Unblocked the same day by
upstream `vite-plugin-pwa@1.3.0` adding Vite 8 to its peer-dep
range (`^3.1.0 || ^4 || ^5 || ^6 || ^7 || ^8`). One Vite 8
breaking change required a code edit: Rolldown (Vite 8's
default bundler) only accepts the function form of
`manualChunks`, not the legacy object form Vite 7's Rollup
supported. `vite.config.ts` `manualChunks` was refactored from
a `{chunkName: [pkgs]}` literal to a function that matches the
module id against a packages-to-chunk map and returns the
bucket name; trailing-slash matching prevents prefix collisions
between sibling packages (`react` vs `react-dom` vs
`react-router-dom`). Build green: 4 chunks emitted with the
same shape Vite 7 produced (vendor-react ~190 KB,
vendor-tiptap ~401 KB, vendor-ui ~218 KB, index ~968 KB),
PWA SW regenerates with 37 precache entries. Test deltas:
frontend 707 passed unchanged; smoke Playwright 191 passed
unchanged. lessons-learned.md updated with the manualChunks
breaking-change note and the stale-dev-server pollution lesson
caught during this session. Will land in the v0.29.0
CHANGELOG.

### SEC-01 — vite-plugin-pwa vulnerability chain cleared

`npm audit --audit-level=high`: 3 high -> 0 high after the
DEP-09 bump. Cleared advisories: GHSA-5c6j-r48x-rmvq
(serialize-javascript RCE, CVSS 8.1) and GHSA-qj8w-gfj5-8c6v
(serialize-javascript DoS, CVSS 5.9), both reaching the
frontend via the transitive chain `workbox-build` ->
`@rollup/plugin-terser` -> `serialize-javascript`. The
unrelated `uuid` GHSA-w5hq-g745-h8pq advisory (moderate) stays
open and is its own track. Production bundle was never
affected (dev-only exposure). Will land in the v0.29.0
CHANGELOG.

### DEP-DBPATH-01 step 2 — `BIBLIOGON_DB_PATH` precedence flip

Shipped in v0.28.0. `BIBLIOGON_DATA_DIR` now wins when both env
vars are set; `BIBLIOGON_DB_PATH` is ignored with a clear
"ignored" runtime warning that names the value the user passed.
The DB_PATH-alone path keeps the v0.27.0 deprecation warning so
deployments that still set only the legacy variable migrate at
their own pace. Tests for the prior "both set, no warn" case
were renamed and inverted to assert the new precedence and the
new "ignored" warning. Step 3 (full removal of the
`BIBLIOGON_DB_PATH` override) stays open under the same ID,
queued for the release after v0.28.0. Commit: `7595ee4`.

### D-06 — cross-platform installer scripts

Shipped in v0.28.0. Three new entry points alongside
`install.sh`: `install.command` for macOS (10-line
Finder-doppelklickbar wrapper), `install.ps1` for Windows
(121-line PowerShell mirror generated from
`install.ps1.template` via `make sync-versions`), and
`install.cmd` (7-line Windows batch wrapper invoking
`install.ps1` with `-NoProfile -ExecutionPolicy Bypass` for
Group-Policy-locked corporate environments). All three ship
unsigned per launch decision; macOS Gatekeeper and Windows
SmartScreen warnings documented in both READMEs.
`scripts/sync_versions.py` refactored to a list-driven
`_INSTALL_ARTIFACTS` tuple so `install.sh` and `install.ps1`
share the substitution logic; `verify_version_pins.sh` rejects
hardcoded version literals in the static wrappers
(`install.command`, `install.cmd`). Validation pending on a
fresh macOS user account and fresh Windows 11 install — report
issues with the OS version and exact error message and they
fold into the next point release. Commit: `2b45654`.

### AR-BULK-PLAYWRIGHT-SMOKE-01 — Playwright smoke for bulk article export

Shipped in v0.28.0. Three specs in
`e2e/smoke/article-bulk-export.spec.ts`: per-tile checkbox +
bulk-action-bar + ZIP markdown download, series filter +
Select-all selecting only the currently filtered set, and
filter-change clearing selection. Caught one real bug while
writing the specs: `/api/test/reset` cleared
Asset / Chapter / Book but not Article, so state leaked between
specs. Fixed in the same commit by adding
`db.query(Article).delete()` to the reset path
(BIBLIOGON_DEBUG-only). Full smoke suite is now 191 passing.
Commit: `ca83e8f`.

### LAUNCHER-I18N-EXTRACT-01 — full launcher i18n extraction

Shipped in v0.28.0. Every remaining hardcoded English dialog
title and message body in
`launcher/bibliogon_launcher/__main__.py` (~50 dialogs:
Docker-daemon retry, env-prep failure, install-flow status
sequence, update-available, pending-uninstall cleanup,
launcher-stale, install-failed/complete, uninstall confirmation
+ per-phase status, installation-moved + folder-picker,
compose-failure, health-timeout, already-running) extracted
into the JSON i18n catalog. Five common-action strings
(`OK`, `Cancel`, `Retry`, `Close`, `Open browser`) de-duplicated
into a `common.*` namespace. DE catalog uses real umlauts
throughout; eight new umlaut spot-check assertions added to
`test_i18n_and_welcome` so ASCII-transliteration regression is
caught across the full extracted surface. Launcher tests
unchanged at 165 (assertions added to existing tests, not new
test functions). Commit: `38af8a1`.

### AR-BULK-BOOKS-PARITY-01 — bulk export from the books dashboard

Shipped in v0.28.0. `POST /api/books/bulk-export` accepts
`{book_ids: list[str], format: "epub"|"pdf"|"docx"}`, reuses the
per-book scaffolding pipeline (`_load_book` +
`_scaffold_and_prepare` + `run_pandoc`) per book, and returns a
date-stamped ZIP (`books-YYYY-MM-DD.zip`) of per-book exports.
Hard 200-book limit via Pydantic `max_length`. Filename
collisions get numeric suffixes. Combined-multi-book mode
intentionally not implemented (per-book pipeline produces one
project per book through manuscripta + write-book-template
scaffolding; merging N books would require deciding whose
metadata wins and which book contributes the cover, neither a
natural workflow). Frontend: per-tile checkbox overlay,
Select-all affordance above the grid, sticky `BookBulkActionBar`
with format dropdown + Export + Clear. 8 new
`ui.dashboard.bulk.*` i18n keys in EN + DE backfilled to all
six auto-translated locales. Commits: `ae76e12` (feature),
`d381e64` (CI test fix: pandoc skipif on TestZipShape).

### DEP-DBPATH-01 step 1 — `BIBLIOGON_DB_PATH` deprecation warning

Backend now emits a `logger.warning` when `BIBLIOGON_DB_PATH` is
set without `BIBLIOGON_DATA_DIR`. Shipped in v0.27.0. Step 2
(precedence flip so `BIBLIOGON_DATA_DIR` derivation wins) is
gated on the next release after v0.27.0; step 3 (remove the
override entirely) is gated on the release after that. The
backlog entry stays open under the same ID for those two steps.

### DEP-FE-VERSION-01 — frontend / backend version cross-check

Shipped in v0.27.0. `verifyBackendVersion` in
`frontend/src/utils/versionCheck.ts` fires once at app start,
fetches `/api/health`, and `console.warn`s on mismatch. Fails
open on every error path. Six Vitest cases cover match,
mismatch, network error, non-OK response, missing/wrong-typed
version field, JSON parse error.

### CI-PRECOMMIT-HOOK-01 — pre-push hook on tag pushes

Shipped in v0.27.0. `scripts/git-hooks/pre-push` runs
`pre-commit run --all-files` against the backend on
`refs/tags/*` pushes; branch pushes are a silent no-op. `make
install-hooks` symlinks the script into `.git/hooks/`.
Validated end-to-end during the v0.27.0 tag push itself.
Closes the gap that produced the v0.26.0..v0.26.6 hotfix
chain.

---

## Archived 2026-05-05

### D-05: Auto-install Docker Desktop — closed as won't-fix

Original ROADMAP P4 entry rescoped on 2026-05-04 (commit
`93af0b2`) from "full Windows installer (Docker Desktop + repo +
`.env`)" to "Docker Desktop auto-install only", because the
Bibliogon launcher already handles repo download, `.env`
generation, Docker image build, and browser open on first run
via `_install_or_welcome` / `_run_install_flow` in
`launcher/bibliogon_launcher/__main__.py`. Only Docker Desktop
itself remained terminal-required for fresh-machine setups.

Closed as **won't fix** on 2026-05-05 after the installer
discovery session
(`docs/explorations/installer-discovery-report.md`) confirmed
that the Docker Subscription Service Agreement Section 2.1's
non-sublicensable license grant forbids third-party silent
install of Docker Desktop. Solo-OSS-dev strict-EULA-reading
default applies; no legal-review budget exists to chase an
ambiguous interpretation.

The launcher's existing **detect-and-instruct** flow (open the
official Docker download page when Docker is missing, continue
the install once Docker is present) is the EULA-compliant
ceiling. Replacing it with a third-party silent install would
violate Docker's terms.

**Citation:** see
[docs/explorations/installer-discovery-report.md](../explorations/installer-discovery-report.md)
section "Docker Desktop integration" for the cited EULA
passages and the analysis chain.

**Related but NOT subsumed:** `LAUNCHER-SELFREPLACE-01` remains
an open P4 backlog item. Discovery confirmed it is a separate
scope (atomic launcher binary self-replace on Windows is
unrelated to Docker Desktop installation).
